[10/18, 2:48 PM] Sis Asma: 🦚🦚 ME MAGANI🦚🦚

AsmaBaffa






            BISMILLAH

    Yanda muka Fara lfy Allah yasa mu Kare lfy.

  Comments dinku nake bukata pls,sannan Ina neman Afwar duk wacce ta min comment ban Mata reply ba,wasu comments Yana sa min waiting bana gani,wasu Kuma Allah Bai sa na kula ba,sai Wanda ke min Sharhi na manta ban Basu page kuyi hakuri Kar kuyi fushi aci gaba da min Sharhi Dan Allah hakan shi ke sawa novel ya tafi dai dai,sannan na samu kwarin gwiwar typing.






     Wannan Page na JIDDER ZARIA ne da Kuma SUBBY tawa.








         Yar wata matashiya ce zukekiyar gaske Fara ce Amma ba Fara kwal kwal ba,ka rantse Yar Ethiopia ce baza ta wuce 17yrs ba, rike take da sandar wani Dattijo makaho Wanda baya gani ko kadan,hannunsa daya a shanye yake nakasshe ne sosai Yana 
rataye da Jakar maganin sa cike dam,wannan Dattijo ba bara yakeyi ba,magani yake siyarwa iri iri, Khairat da sandarta tana Masa jagora daya hannunta Kuma speaker ce katuwa irin ta maroka, Rana ta kwalle a kansu suna zaga kasuwa kasuwa a cikin birnin Kano.

    Sandar ya samu ya kwala Mata a kanta Dan ubanki baza kiyi tallan maganin ba sai dare yayi bamu samu komai ba,Kawu to wlh Ni bazan iya Furta kalaman tallan Nan ba,ace kamata mace budurwa Ina Furta kalmomin batsa,Ina ka taba Jin mace da tallan magani iri wannan? Ai gwara ka barni irin da na dinga Shiga gida gida Ina musu talla ba a kasuwa ba,Taya Zan iya Furta wannan kalmomi,Kuma kasan Ni ban iya ba yauce ranata ta farko Dana rakoka kasuwanni.
   
   Dan ubanki sai kinyi ko Kuma idan na koma gida wlh na fadawa talatu taci ubanki,Zaki min asara Allah ya Baki nasibi idan kinyi talla yanzu Nan Zaki ga an siye maganin Amma idan nine ko yarona Haka muke yini Babu ciniki wlh ko kiyi ko sai kinyi sati cur ba a Baki abinci a gidan ba kin San Halina kin San Kuma wace ce Talatu.

   Jin za a hanata abinci tace to Bari zanyi yanda kakeyi ai Allah ya gani bani da laif...kafin ta Karasa ya sake rafka Mata sanda yana Fara yi Dan ubanki,shegiya, tsinanniya ke dai Allah wadaran halinki.
   Ba shiri ta kafa speaker a bakinta cikin zazzakar Muryarta me dadin saurare ta fara tallan magani kamar Haka...

     Ga Magani...ga...magani,nice me magani, sai an gwada Akan San na kwarai da yardar Allah zaku warke,ba mune muke warkarwa ba,Allah ne, da Iznin Allah idan ka siyi wannan magani cikin hukuncin Allah zaku warke,ga maganin waraka,Mata da maza Hajiya ko Alhaji Azo a siyi magani araha garabasa,maganin warakar dukkan wasu cututtuka,ga me gani tazo ga araha ga aiki...da masifa Makahon yace Baki Fadi na ko wacce cututtuka ba? Fadi Yar iska,ta jinjina nauyin Maganar Amma Haka ta jawo gyalenta me zarnin fitsarin yaran gidansu ta rufe Fuskarta sabo da kunya tace.

    Jama'a kuzo ga maganin Basir,Ciwon sanyi me cutar da mace ko Namiji,fitar farin ruwa a gaban mace ko Namiji ya rage Masa karfi ya Sa Masa kasala Wanda baya iya gamsar da Matarsa baya iya tsinana Mata komai ya rasa Kuma ya gagara gane Dalilin to sanyi ne ke damunsa, ga waraka tazo kuyi maza ku garzayo domin siyen wannan magani.
   Naira dari biyu ne kacal anyi shi da ingattun Yayan itatuwa.

   Murmushin jin Dadi Makahon yayi yace yawwa Khairat ci gaba,tace Namiji gabansa na kankancewa kamar an roko Masa yazo ga Magani,mace wacce Bata Jin dadin saduwa da mijinta tazo tana da  cutar sanyi ga Magani ya samu,bamu mukeyi ba Allah ke warkarwa ta silar Amfani da maganin Kawu Mai baiwar makanta,Makaho ne Amma Allah ya bashi baiwar Ilmin hada magunguna,Makahon ya sake Mata rada a kunne Aiko ta karo karfin Muryarta jikinki na Miki kaikayi mace taji wani Mar mar kamar tsutsa na yawo ajikinki maza zo ga Magani,Amarya wacce ake Shirin aurenta tazo ga Magani Kar Ango yace an cuceshi, rada a kunne Makahon ya sake yi Mata,tace Muna da Sa Ango kuka,muna da makale Mata,Mannau shima muna dashi,Amarya Kisha kiga aiki ke da kishiya sai dai ki gani a makwafta.

   Duk wannan tallan da Khairat ke yi kusan Abubuwa kadan take gane me ake nufi,kawai dai tana yin yanda Makahon kawunta ke yi.
   Da yawan mutane maza da Mata kallonta akeyi wasu suna dariya,wasu na zaginta a ransu Bata da tarbiya,Bata da gata,wasu Kuma ganin Makaho Dattijo sun gano shi ya tirsasawa budurwar irin wannan tallan sai suke Jin tausayinta suna Jin haushin Makaho,ta wani bangaren Kuma wasu Makahon ya burgesu akan ya dinga bara da roko to gwara ya nemi na kansa wannan ya nuna me zuciyar neman na kansa ne sakamakon wasu daga nakasa ta samesu ko yayane sai zuciyarsu ta mutu kawai sanaarsu bara da roko.

   Khairat taci gaba da Magani....azo a garzayo a siyi magani zaku ga amfaninsa,ta fara bada labarin karya wani saurayi matashi yazo wajen Kawu Makaho  yace Kawu na Shiga uku  ka tallafa min gaba daya gabana kullum ja baya yakeyi,Kawu na ya tambayi matashin yace yaro idan ka tashi da safe Yana motsawa? Matashin yace Kawu kamar lagwanin resho Haka yake,Kawu yace yaro na gane komai matarka ma Bata ko saurarenka sai dai kullum fada ko? Yaron yace exertly Kawu Nan Kawu ya bashi wannan Magani tare da Furta maza jika a ruwa kasha har kwana uku zaka ga aiki,Bayan sati daya sai ga saurayin Nan ya dawo Yana Godiya tare da  yiwa Kawu kyauta me tsoka sabo da yaji dadin wannan magani,Mun gaji Wannan  magani tun iyaye da kakanni...Alumma ku garzayo ga maganin gaskiya ba algus.Makaho sai washe Baki yake yaji khairat ta zage tana sambada karya yanda yake yiwa mutane Ana siyan maganinsa yayi ta bayar da labarin karya,ya Jinjinawa Khairat data iya yanda yake tallan har ma ta fishi iyawa dake tana da basira.
  
    Kafin wani lokaci mutane irin Wanda suka shigo kasuwa daga kauye Mata da maza da Kuma Yan Tasha suka Fara rubibin siyan magani Nan da Nan sai ga Magani ya kusa karewa kaf,Makaho kuwa murna kamar zai tashi sama Yana wani lallaba Khairat.
   Khairat kuwa kamar ta saki Ihu Haka take ji ga kunya ta rufeta bata iya kallon mutane,kwalla ta cika Mata Ido,Idonta yayi ja sabo da bacin Rai ji take kamar ta kashe kanta ta huta,Kawu Makaho kuwa ko a jikinsa kudi kawai yake Tarawa abinsa.
   
    Yana washe Baki yace Khairat kwana Nan zamu Fara Shiga kauyukan Kano,Litinin zuwa Alhamis kauyuka zamu dinga zuwa sune Wanda suke da karancin wayewa zamu fi samun ciniki,Birni Kuma daga Jumaa zuwa Lahadi zamu dinga zagawa.
   Harara Khairat ta zabga Masa tare da cewa Ni wlh bazan iya ba shike Nan tunda na taso bani da ishashen ilmi daga Talla sai talla,kwata kwata jss2 kuka katse min karatu na,Islamiyya ma Dan Ina kokarin zuwa ta dare ne da bazan San ko Fatiha ba,ga yaronku Nan su har ta Gaba da Secondary sukeyi,Ni kun maidani jakarku sabo da Baku Kuka haifeni ba,Kalleka Kawu kana kanin Babana Uwa daya uba daya Amma kaci Amanar iyalinsa baka iya yi min komai sai zaluntata da kukeyi,matarka ta cuceni,yaranka da Kai kanka Kawu tana Gama Fadi ta fashe da kuka,ko saurarenta baiyi ba yaci gaba da siyar da maganinsa ko a jikinsa Yana jinta ta kifa kanta a cinyarta tana ta kuka,idan mutane suka tambaya wannan lfy kuwa? Sai yace ai kanta ne yake ciwo yanzu Tasha magani Haka take yi idan tana Ciwon Kai.

    Takaici yasa Khairat ta mike tace a Nan Zan barka Kawu in yaso ka mutu a Nan bazan maida ka gida ba gwara na Shiga bariki,Ta Kama hanyar tafiya kenan Kawu ya tabbatar da gaske ne idan ta tafi wa Talatu zata sai aiki,sannan shi kanshi wa zai tayashi tallansa, Aiko ya dauki speaker ya fara sanarwa jama'a ku taimakeni ga yarinyata can zata Shiga duniya a taimaka wlh mahaukaciya ce,tana da Ciwon hauka,kullum sai ta fito rannan ma sai da akayi sati Uku ba a San inda take ba,Nan take Khairat ta kwashe da gudu tana ihu,ganin Haka yasa mutane suka yarda da Zancen Kawu Makaho gata dama dukun dukun da ita,sai ko mutane sukayi Mata Tara Tara aka kamata.
   Da kyar Kawu Makaho ya lallasheta ta rike sandarsa suka tafi gida tana Hawaye.

    A hankali tace Kawu yunwa nake ji ka siya min ko yogourt ce na Sha tunda an yi ciniki,Kawu yace Dan ubanki nawa ne kudin? wasu na kirkine uwar son banza Zaki ce na siya Miki har yogourt Ashe Dadi kika zo ci,ko Ni ban Sha ba sai ke Yar gwal,ubanki me ya mutu ya Bari,uwarki data mutu zoben farin karfe kawai kika gada gayyar tsiya,to ko Zan siya bazan siya Miki ba,ban siyawa yarana ba su Zainabu ko matata Talatu sai ke,ke din banza ballagazar wofi.
   To tunda baka siya min ba ai sai ka kyaleni ba sai ka zageni ka zagi iyayena ba,Kuma wlh duk ranar da Allah ya bani Rana nayi kudi sai na Rama abinda Kuka yi min,bazan ji wani tausayinku ba,Kuma yogourt sai na Sha Nan ta samu Kawu ta turmushe shi a kasa kamar ta samu yaro ta dauki Naira Hamsim Kawu Yana ta ihu Jama'a a taimaka min ga Yar fashi, ta siyi yogourt ta Hamsim me sanyi tana Sha tana yiwa Kawu jagora Wanda kayansa sukayi futu futu sabo da turmusheshi da tayi  kasa suka dinga kokawa.
   Khairat Allah ya Bata karfi ba yanda Kawu ya iya sai yace Allah ya Isa tsinanniya kinsha wuta Bal Bal.

   Dariya tayi kyawawan hakoranta kanana suka bayyana,dama Dan bakinta cut kamar cokali bazai Shiga ba,lips dinta pink,Muguwa dama bakya dariya sai mugunta ta faru anan Zaki Shiga dariya Azzaluma.
   Kawu wlh baka ji yogourt din ba Dadi ga sanyi tayi kankara,Banza yayi Mata suna tafiya sunzo dai dai majalisar samari Sai Kawu Makaho yaji wani Makaho Dan uwansa Yace Malam Sabi'u ya gari? Ai Ina Jin Muryar yarka na gane Kaine,Kawu Makaho yace Af Haladu Makaho ne? Sannu Dan Uwa,Haladu shima da yaronsa karami Yana Masa jagora yace Alhmdllh ya aka ji da Sana'a? Kawu yace Alhmdllh,Ai ka samawa kanka lafiya da baka bara barar Nan ko wahala gamu duk mun lalace cewar Haladu.
   Kawu yace wuuuu rabani da bara,bara a Arewa musamman Kano ko wahala ba a sadakar arziki daga biyar sai goma Ina Zan iya wahala Haka,Kano sadakarsu daga biyar sai goma,sai dariya kake ji kyakyakya matasan Samarin Nan dake Majalisa suna ta dariya,Yan Jagora Kuma sunyi Miki Miki sabo da su suna gani sun San Kuma a majalisar Maza suka tsaya,su Kuma makafi basa gani.
    Kunya ta rufe jagoran Haladu da Kuma Khairat jagorar kawu Sabiu Makaho,sai zungurin Kawu take da kafa tana da mutane fa Kawu Amma Bai gane ba yaci gaba da...

    Ai musamman matasan Kano Malam akwai son Kudi sai Yan Mata suke kashewa yanzu idan a kudu ne ba Arewa ba da tuni mun sauke Farali Munje Makkah Amma Nan Malam haba gayyar tsiya, Haladu ya karbe da musamman Ghana ko Uganda Hajji da Umrah sai mun ture,kaga sanda naje Nayi bara a Chadi sai da na Kai gyatimina da gyatimata aikin Hajji kafin su rasu Amma Nan sai dai ma su zageka suce ka fisu kudi.
    Kawu yace ai Allah ya tsinewa Yan Arewa musamman Yan Kano Basu San mutunci ba Sadaka daga biyar sai goma,matasan Majalisa suka Kara kwashewa da Dariya, Haladu yace Sabiu nake Jin dariya ko a fillin kwallon kafa muke ne? Kawu yace to wa ya sani ke Dan Ubanki Khairat a Ina muke,Kawu a majlisa muke fa, sai kunya ta Kama Haladu yayiwa Kawu Sallama ya tafi Khairat ma suka tafi gida suka bar matasa suna ta dariya.

     Suna zuwa gida Talatu ta fito da gudu kamar mahaukaciya jikinta na doyi da tsamin Dauda ta tarbi mijinta Kawu Makaho ko kunyar yaranta Bata ji ta rungume Kawu Wanda shima wari yake ga Rana ta buge shi,Kawu yace Talatu ta yau Kuma wani sabon salo ne Yana washe Baki,Talatu tayi fari warr da Ido Wai ita a Dole me kula da Miji tace Hmm Sabiu na yau karatun littafin Hausa naji Ahmad Isa na karantawa a radio soyayyar ta birgeni shine Nima nayi koyi da fadakarwarsa, dariya ce ta Kwacewa Khairat tsofai tsofai Talatu tana yiwa Makaho fari da Ido Bai San me takeyi ba ihu Bayan Hari kenan,ruwa me sanyi ta kawowa Mijinta da Abinci, Khairat Kuma ta watsawa Harara tana daka Mata tsawa Dalla malama fita can tsakar gida munafuka kin tsaya Mana a kai.
   Can ta fita gindin bishiya ta tsaya,Zainab yarta wacce take B u k Jamia level 1 itace ta ebo kayan wanki ta zubewa Khairat a gabanta gashi Nan kiyi sauri ki wanke min anjima Zan koma schl Hostel maza sauri.

   Fuska Khairat ta hade tace Ni wlh na gaji sai na ci Abinci daga dawowata....tas Zainab ta kwashe Khairat da Mari,dake Khairat itama Bata barin ko ta kwana Haka ta cakumi Zainab suka Fara kokawa tukuru Allah yasa Khairat karfi gareta sai ko ta fasawa Zainab Baki,Talatu ta fito tana ihu ta kwalawa danta Babba Kira ya fito da sauri daga dakinsa, tace Ammar Soja kalli yanda Khairat tayiwa kanwarka ta jini.
   Ammar Wanda akewa lakabi da Soja ya zare belt ya Shiga dukan Khairat iya karfinsa kamar ya samu gardi Dan uwansa ya zaneta tas ya farfasa Mata jiki tana ta kuka har ta gaji bacci ya kwasheta a Nan yashe a kasa.
   Sabo da Khairat sarkin bacci ce watarana ko aikenta kayi to tana Jin bacci sai ta nemi bishiya a waje kawai ta kwanta ta rushe da bacci.
    Ba ruwanta da sai ta dawo gida ko ta nemi wurin bacci a wajen da bacci yazo Mata a Nan Zata kwanta.

   Talatu tace yawwa Sojana,Soja marmari daga Nesa sai ka Zama Soja inshallah,Murmushi yayi kawai yaja karnukan sa guda hudu suka fice daga gidan,Soja ma Yana  karatu a makarantar sojoji ta Kaduna Yana level 2 hutu suka samu yazo gida shine yake yiwa kowa rashin mutunci yanda yake so gashi mummunan gaske Baki wuluk dashi duk ya bude yayi mummunar siffa karnukansa guda hudu manya maza,kamar mutane Haka suke Shiga duk inda suke so a gidan,har dakunan bacci,har saman katifa ko gado Hawa suke,tare yake bacci dasu,gashi ko Ina suyi Kashi da fitsari har bedroom,baka Isa ko tsawa kayiwa Karen Soja ba sai ya karyaka Akan ka yiwa karensa tsawa,ko iyayensa Basu Isa ba.

    Su kansu sun San indai har Bacci ya dauke Khairat to baza ta tashi ba sai ta Gama,shi yasa suke zaginta da me cutar bacci,sai da tayi bacci ta koshi sannan ta tashi da kyar tayi wanka da ruwa me zafi,tayi Alwala tayi sallar Azahar da laasar sabo da tana da addini dai dai gwargwado gata da yawan adduoi Kullum sai ta Ware wani lokaci daban tayi karatun Qurani,tasbihi etc sannan tayi adduo inta.
   Su kuwa tun daga kan su Kawu zuwa yaransu Addini Bai damesu ba,basu damu ba,yaran kuwa Sallah sai sunga dama suke yi ko idan suna bukatar wani Abu sai su Fara sallah suna addua daga sun samu abin baza su Kara yi ba,musamman Zainab da Ammar da suke schl sai in zasuyi Exam suke Sallah da Addua.

   Zainab sabo da tana University ita da Soja suna gyara jikinsu,musamman Zainab Yar gayu ce,idan ka ganta a waje taci wanka kamar Yar gidan Gomna Amma da zarar kazo gidansu ruwa baza ka iya Sha ba.ko kawayenta Bata kawowa sabo da Kar a kure karyarta sabo da Yar Karyace ta gaske,Rahinatu Yar Ss2 ce itama akwai karya da rashin kunya ga rowa da son kayan wani, Shahid da Ummi kuwa a jss 1 suke Amma kullum sai Sunyi fitsarin kwance sabo da sangarta,gashi kazanta tasa ko yau ka wanke Kaya sai suyi maka fitsari ga fitsarin karnukan Soja sai suyi a dakina kan kayana shi yasa kullum zarnin fitsari kayanta sukeyi,shi yasa ta Ware kayan da take sallah dasu ta sakalesu a sama yanda ba abinda zai samesu.
  ko ta wanke kafin kwana daya Sunyi fitsari,gashi ba a bata sabulun wanki bare na wanka,Danma tana da karfi watarana Dole take daukan na Yan gidan tayi ayi fada Da ita Dole su hakura tunda itama tana iya masifa da fada bata Bari Ana mata abinda aka ga dama kamar da sanda tana yarinya lokacin taci wahala a hannunsu amma ta koyi fada da kokawa ta karfi Wanda ba halinta bane da can.

    Abinci Talatu ta bata Wanda ragowar Soja ne daya rage aka turo mata kamar karya,ta cinye tasha kazamin ruwansu sannan ta yiwa Zainab wankin da wasu aikace aikacen da aka sata,dare nayi ta tafi makarantar dare abinta.
  Kayan sawar Khairat Basu Fi Kala  biyar ba duk sun kode sun jeme wasu ma sun yage wasu da maho anyi musu sai slifas da take sawa gwanin tausayi.

   Washe gari kuwa Sunday Kawu yace Kauye zasu hau mota su tafi Tallan magani,Gaya Lga suka tafi cikin kauyuka suke zagawa ta kafa speaker a bakinta tare da Ware murya Waraka tazo,Ina Mata Ina Maza yau kakarku ta yanke saka ga dama ta samu,Me gani tazo ga Araha ga aiki.
   Yara suka taru suna binsu sunga sabon Abu mace da Tallan magani irin wannan,Dama ta dauko radio katuwa me speaker kawai ta dannawa Yara wakar Usaini Danko wacce taji kida ta yaudaresu da Haka suka Fara cashewa, idan sunji da yawa sai ta kashe taci gaba da talla, maganin Ciwon Sanyi yazo har gida,mace miji na saduwa dake kamar Dusa to Azo ga dama tazo,Warin gaba,mace mijinki yaji gabanki na bashi,doyi da hamami wannan zai zubar Miki da kimarki ta ya mace Azo ga Magani har gida...Waraka tazo...me gida baka da karfi kasala baka iya gamsar da matarka abin kunya nee gareka... Bayan ga Magani araha garabasa ku garzayo...ayi sauri Azo a siya ba Zama muka zo yi ba tafiya zamuyi,Makaho ya karbi speaker shima yace Mun gaji Wannan ingantaccen magani tun iyaye da kakanni...ku fito tafiya zamuyi...Kar mu tafi kuzo Kuna cizon yatsa...Nan take sai ga Yara ta kudu ta Arewa iyayensu sun turo su da kudi zasu siya,ganin harda zukekiyar budurwa sai abin yaja hankalinsu harda masu leke ta katanga,duk yaron da yazo siya sai a bashi speaker Khairat tace yaro ya sunanka? Sai ya fada,Bari ayi Maka Addua sai ta fara kwararowa yaro Addua kamar gaske Yara suyi ta tsalle da murna.

   Ganin Haka sai Kawu yasa Speaker yace idan da Wanda yayi niyyar bada sadaka ya samu Lada Ni nakasashe ne Makaho ne Ni Kuma bani da hannu daya a taimaka min ba sai na roka ba Sadaka Allah ya Kai muku gaban Annabi.
   Ganin Haka sai kowa yake Jin tausayin Kawu Sabiu ganin Makahon gaske ne hannu daya ya shanye sai sadaka ta ko Ina ake kawo Masa ga masu siyan magani suna yi Suma.Khairat kuwa taki karba taci gaba da talla kunya kawai take ji,tana kalmomin batsa gashi Kawu sai masifa yake mata Yana dukanta da Sanda,kuma idan sunje gida zai fadawa Matarsa da yaransa suyi Mata duka su hanata abinci.



  Kawu dai za muji Ina ya samu iya hada maganin gargajiya,Sannan maganin Yana yi da gaske ko karya ce.

 AsmaBaffa Fans club wannan page naku ne,son Kai zanyi ku Zan fara bawa.








            Sai kusan Magrib suka bar kauyen suka Shiga mota tare da  komawa gida lfy,sabo da rashin Imanin Kawu yau ma ko Awara kasa siyawa Khairat yayi,Babu irin rokonsa da batayi ba Amma yaki,sannan ya boye kudinsa tare da siyawa Talatu Matarsa da yaransa Kifi soyayye na dari biyar ya siya musu tare da kwai Dafaffe na Dari uku.
    Ganin idan sunje gida baza su ko sanwa Khairat ba sai ta faki numfashin Kawu tasa hannu a Jakarta ta dauki kwai guda daya da kifi guda biyu Manya suna tafiya tana cin abinta,Khairat duba min kiji kamshin kwai nake ji Dana kifi Kuma kamar an taba min jakata, Sai da Khairat ta Hadiye na bakinta da take ci tace Babu komai Kaine dai kawai hancinka yake jiye maka ba abinda ya faru.

   Bayan sun Karasa gida kuwa Talatu ta bude kifi da Kwai daga ita sai yaranta da Kawu suka ci ko kula Khairat basuyi ba aiki kawai take ta faman yi daga wannan sai wannan ko a jikinta dama ta Saba da halinsu Kuma taci ba tare da Kawu ya sani ba.

   Da dare Khairat yau ba Makaranta tana zaune Dogs din Soja suna kwance sun wani baje a gefenta wani Almajiri ya shigo Yana bara Wahidin...Iya Ni ban samu ba,Iya yunwa Bata da Hankali...ko Dan kanzo...takaici ya Kama Kawu sarkin rowa ya fito daga daki Yana dauke da sandarsa yace Kai Almajiri Ubanka Yana Ina?ko akwai kasonka a gidana?ko nauyinka a kaina yake?nace ka rataya a wuyana?ko hakki nane ciyar da Kai,ina ubanka ko uwarka ka kirasu a waya a kansu hakkinka yake,,Almajiri yace Baba Ni Maraya ne a taimaka min .
   Tsagal Talatu ta Nuna Khairat da yatsa wannan ma Marainiyace a hannun kanin babanta take ai kana da dangi ka tafi wajensu shegen yaro me suffar Yan ruwa.
   Almajirin Khairat ta kalla yaro karami ya bata tausayi tace Yi Hakuri ka tafi kaji,Rahinatu wacce Bata fi 15yrs ba ta gallawa Khairat Harara tare da cewa Iyayin banza.

    Khairat tace wlh sai na mike na Miki dukan tsiya ko Ni saarki ce Dan uwarki? Karki ga Ina kyaleki wlh Dan yarinya ce ke da sai na fasa Miki bak...tas Kake ji Soja Ammar ya buge bakin Khairat tare da cewa kafin ki fasa Mata Ni Bari nayi maganinki shegiya kodaddiyar banza, takaici yasa ta mike taje kofar dakinta sannan tace Kai Kuma Duna Dan Baki sari daddawa Baki wuluk da Kai sai kayan Muni jiki duk Dirty Wai Kai saurayi,wace zata so Ka kana tsami an cuci soja,tana Gama fadin Haka ta fada dakinta tare da Sa sakata ta kulle, Ammar Soja ya dinga bugun kofa kamar Zaki Yana yau sai na kasheki har lahira,Talatu tace kyaleta Dan Ubanta gobe zata fito ai,Kawu Makaho yace an cire Mata tallafin Abinci na sati guda shegiyar yarinya.

  Talatu tace wannan yarinyar da dama ta samu sai ta taka mu to Allah yasa munfi karfinta dama indai ta gaji uwarta sai Addua.
    Washe gari kuwa tana Fitowa da Asuba Soja ya mata shegen duka kamar zai kasheta ko Bari barinta tayi Sallah Bai yi ba,Haka suka je yawon talla kauyuka da kyar take motsi ga zafin dukan Rana tana Sha ga yunwa kamar ta mutu.
   Suna jikin wata bishiya a kauyen Kumbotso kawai ta bingire a Nan ta fara baccinta data saba,Kawu Babu tashin da Bai Mata ba yasan baza ta tashi ba kawai ya kyaleta yaci gaba da cinikin maganinsa.

    Sai da ta gaji da bacci ta tashi lokacin Ana sallar Azahar tayi Alwala tare da Shimfida Dankwalinta tayi sallah abinta sannan tace Kawu Bari naje wancan gidan nayi Fitsari,cike da masifa yace to kiyi sauri ki dawo,Tana Shiga gidan ta iske an sauke shinkafa da wake Ana rabawa yaran gidan,Suka gaisa da matar gida tace Dan Allah Zanyi fitsari,mutanen kauyen sunga bakuwa daga birni amma gwara na kauye da ita, Nan fa suka ji tausayinta suka nuna Mata Bayan tayi ta fito Matar tace baiwar Allah zauna a zuba Miki Abinci kici Mana, dama abinda ya kawota kenan kwadayin abinci,ai kuwa ta zauna aka cika Mata wata katuwar Siver ta cinye tas tare da kwankwadar ruwan rijiyarsu me sanyi ta musu Godiya sannan ta tafi,Suma kansu na kauye sunga rashin gata a jikin yarinyar.

  Yau ta koshi ko kula Kawu batayi ba kan ya siya Mata Abinci Haka da suka koma gida ma ko a jikinta tayi aikace aikacenta.
   Su kansu su Talatu Sunyi mamaki Basu bata Abinci ba Amma suka ganta lafiya Lau,da misalin 8 na dare sai ga yaro an Aiko yace Wai Khairat tazo inji Usy.
    Talatu tace Usy dai anyi asara ya rasa wurin wacce zai zo sai wata Khairat,Khairat Kuma Bata kaunar taji Namiji ya Kira ta zance,ta tsani maza su zo zance ganinta nawa take yarinya da ita za Ana damunta,duk wahalar da take Sha ya fiye Mata ta zauna Don har yau tana sa ran zata yi karatu,Kuma Usy ma wani gara dashi gaja kamar daga kauye yazo Haka yake ba Wanda zaice Dan birni ne sabo da a kauye ma akwai Dan birni a birni akwai Dan kauye, Talatu tace tashi kije shegiya wa zai soki in ba irin su Usy dinba,Hakan ma ai ke kika yi dacen miji kamar Usy,Rahinatu da Shahid suka sheke da dariya tare da cewa Usy hhhhh.
   Kawu yace jeki ko Zaki samo Mana Yan kudi Dole suka Kora Khairat ta tafi zance wajen Usy.

    A fusace Khairat ta fita wurin Usy tace Salamu alaykum gani ya akayi? Usy ya washe Baki sannan yace Sannu tawan,Khairat tace Fadi me ya kawoka? Usy yace shegen yaron Nan Muazu dana Aiko ya Kira min ke Amma sai da yace na bashi ashirin kudin Kira,takaici ya Kama Khairat sai tayi tunanin Usy Babanta Muaz daya rasu yake zagi a wayance,Sai itama tasan Sunan Baban Usy Kabiru tace Wlh kuwa kasan Kabiru makwafcinmu yaron Nan na can gidan Haka rannan na aikeshi ya kaimin shara yaki duk ranar Dana kamashi sai naci Uwar Kabiru,Dan uban Kabiru Ni zaiwa Haka,Tsam Usy ya Shiga tunani sai ya gano Babansa take zagi Akan ya Fadi Sunan babanta Bai sani ba,sai yanzu ya tuna Ashe Sunan Baban Khairat Muaz,ba shiri yace kutmar au da Babana kike?iyye....Khairat Ni din? Kwarai kuwa gobe ma ka Kara zagin me Sunan ubana ka gani idan ban zagi naka ba.

   Koda Khairat ta dawo gida Kawu yaga Bata samo ko sisi ba sai yace shegiya yanzu Haka ta koreshi,Rahinatu tace wlh Ina jinta Abba tana zagin iyayen Usy,Wai Dan yace Muazu..to Muazu an fada, da sauri Khairat tace Sabiu..Sabiu..na Kuma cewa Sabiu.
  Baki bude suke kallon Khairat Talatu tace lallai yar Nan Bata da mutunci Amma zanyi maganinki,Tuni Khairat ta gudu dakinta ta kulle ta window ta leko tana Talatuwa Yar Talatuwa me a daure a dinga wanka.

        Wace ce Khairat?

   Khairat Muaz Fulani cikakken sunanta,Yan Asalin Fulanin Taraba state ne, kasuwanci ya kawo Muaz Fulani Kano,Su biyu ne wajen iyayensu Wanda sun Dade da Rasuwa,Muaz sai da Ya auri Hauwau Babar Khairat kenan sannan ya dawo Kano Yana kasuwanci har Allah yasa arzikinsa ya bunkasa Bayan Matarsa Hauwau da yake matukar so ta Haifi Kyakyawan yarta Khairat ya jawo Dan Uwansa Kawu Sabiu Wanda dama tun Yana yaro yaje ya hau wata bishiyar kuka Aiko Aljanu suka makantar dashi hannunsa daya ya shanye magani ba inda ba aje ba Amma ba a Dace ba har ya girma ya Riga Muaz aure sosai ya Auri Matarsa Harira wacce ake Kira da Talatu itama Yar kauyensu na Taraba ce, tausayin Dan uwa yasa Muaz ya dauko Kawu Sabiu ya Gina Masa gidan da suke ciki a yanzu,tun asali Kawu Sabiu ba wani mutunci garesu ba daga shi har Matarsa,dake Muaz me dan kudi ne na rufin asiri sai Kawu yake Masa biyayya shi Kuma yaji Dadi yake Masa ko me yake so,sannan duk yaransa shine ya dauki nauyin Karatunsu har Ammar Soja da Zainab suka Gama secondary.

    Muaz ya Dade Bai samu Haihuwa ba kafin Allah yasa Hauwa ta samu ciki ta Haifi Khairat,ta taso cikin gata da Jin Dadi har aka yaye ta,Lokacin Hauwa ta sake samun wani cikin tazo Haihuwa Allah ya Mata Rasuwa,Muaz yasha bakin ciki sabo da Yana son Matarsa lokacin Kuma suna zamansu lfy da Kawu duk inda zasuje ko ziyarar dangi can Taraba tare zaka gansu Muaz Yana Masa jagora,sosai Shakuwa ce me karfi tsakaninsu, sabo da bacin Rai na rashin Matarsa Hawan jini ya kamashi da karfi Amma a Haka shi yake wa Khairat komai Yana rainonta ko shagon Kasuwa zaije da Khairat yake tafiya ga yarinya Fara Kyakyawa tayo babarta Hauwau tafi ma Babar Tata komai,Kawu sabo da rashin Imani ko Talatu Bata ce a Bata Khairat ta rike ba kafin Muaz ya sake aure,shi yaci fitsarin Khairat da kashinta.

   Bayan Shekara biyar Muaz Hawan jininsa ya tashi ya Shiga bayi zaiyi wanka ya Fadi dam, shike Nan ya sankame an kaishi asibiti Allah ya Masa rasuwa dattijon arziki,lokacin kuma Fafur Talatu tace baza ta rike Dan wani ba,Kawu kuma Allah ya Dora Masa son kansa sai abinda Matarsa da yaransa suka ce,mutanen Unguwar Gwale cikin birnin Kano suka Fara zagin Kawu da Matarsa ganin Khairat kullum tana makwafta wata Mata ta dauketa tace idan basa so ita tana so da na kowane, sai Kawu ya lallashi Talatu da ta daure ta dauki Khairat ta riketa idan ta girma sai ta zamar musu Yar aiki.
   Talatu tace Sam sai dai a siyar da gadon Khairat kaf data gada a Bata a matsayin kudin rainonta,baza tayi a banza ba,ba a aikin banza a Kano.
  
    Kawu ya hada komai har gonakinsu na gado na Taraba state ya siyar suka bude bushasha a matsayin kudin rainon Khairat.
   Dama Basu da iyaye sai Yan uwa na Taraba wasu sunji labarin me ya faru sai suka zo daukan Khairat Talatu da Kawu suka musu dadin Baki ai yarmu ce Kawu harda kuka Wai an nuna Masa Bai iya ba,kamar Dan uwansa ya kasa rike Masa ya daya Allah ya kiyaye.
   Bayan dangi sun tafi Sai Talatu tace mutanen Unguwa sun Sa musu Ido  a siyar da gidan na Gwale su koma Sheka can kusa da Zooroad, suka siyi wani tsohon gida Wanda kaf layin ma an San talakawa ne kukut a cikin wajen.
   
    Suna cinye dukiyar Khairat har ta Kare tas lokacin Khairat na karama ba irin azabar da Talatu Bata yi Mata watarana ma sai Su Zainab suyi ta mintsininta,dake tafi su karfi sai su cijeta mugunta iri iri,shi kanshi Kawu watarana mintsinin Yar yarinya yake,Talatu Kuma tayi Mata duka da carbi ko tsinkaken tsintsiyar kwakwa, tun Bata gane basa kaunarta har ta gane komai, tana Shiga jss2 suka cireta a schl Wai kudin rainonta sun Kare Kuma Hakan ma Primary kawai tayi Private Amma jss1-2 government schl tayi.
   Daga Nan Talatu take daura Mata talla iri iri har da kayan Miya etc.
  Kudin gadonta sun Kare nan Talauci ya addabi Kawu.

    Kawu yaje bara wasu wuraren Amma gaba daya kamar ya zagi sama ba Wanda ke bashi sadaka,sai ya tuna babansu kafin ya rasu Yana hada magungunan gargajiya Kuma yasan wasu da dama,shine yake Shiga daji cikin kauyukan Kano ya samo ganyayyaki da jijiyoyin bishiyu iri iri wasu ya hada dai dai wasu kuma shirmensa yake hadawa.

   Dansa Soja Ammar shi ke rakashi gonakin kauye ya samo tare da tambayar mutanen kauyen wannan itace bishiya kaza ne? Haka har su samo iri iri su dawo,tunda Khairat ta Gama jss2 yake tasa keyarta suje daji,su Kuma yaransa suna makaranta Yana so su Gama su Samu aiki su dinga rike gidan shi Kuma ya huta.
   Haka idan ya hada magani zasu bawa Khairat wasu ta Shiga gidajen mutane a samu ciniki Kuma,shine karshe ya siyi speaker ya dauki Khairat Yana sata Dole tayi tallan magani.

   Kawu da Talatu son Kudi ne dasu,ga son kayan wani,rowa harda rowar Abinci sannan yaransu kawai sune Yaya sune dolensu, basa hangen na kowa, Akan muguntar da suke yiwa Khairat ta Zama me Saurin fushi,zuciya da rashin barin ko ta kwana kullum a shirye take kana yi Mata zata maka,su Kawu sun zubar da girmansu Bata ganinsu da daraja ko kadan.
   Yaran Kawu biyar a duniya Talatu ta daina Haihuwa tana tsarin iyali,Ammar Soja shine Babba 28yrs sai Zainab 23yrs,sai Shahid 19yrs,Rahinatu 15yrs sai Ummi auta 12yrs.
   Kawu ya manta da abinda Muaz ya Masa yaci Amanarsa ya daya tal ya kasa rikewa sun cinye Mata gado Kuma suna azabtar da ita,ko sutura basa dinka Mata sai dai su Bata kwancen Zainab ko Rahinatu.
   Allah ya bawa Khairat farin jini kowa ya ganta sai ta birgeshi shi duk da kazantarta ta Dole domin basa Bata Sabulun wanka bare na wanki sabo da tsananin kyawunta da kyan diri,gashinta har gadon baya Baki sidik,idonta kadai ya Isa ya birgeka kamar Madara gasu Dara Dara kamar tana jin bacci fadin kyawunta zai cinye Mana time ma duk inda kuke zaton kyau to Khairat ta Kai,Hancinta ba me tsini bane can sannan round face gare ta gata da Masifar kyan diri ita ba ramammiya ba Kuma ba me kiba ba,sannan tana da tsayi Amma dai dai normal na dirarriyar mace duk da wahalar data ke Sha Bai Hana fatarta laushi ba,gata da son Tsafta Amma ba dama.
  Talatuwa kuwa duk yaranta munana ne shi yasa suke kishin Khairat.gwara ma Zainab tana shafe shafen sai ta Zama Fara shine ta danfi dama dama Kuma tana kwalliya sosai Yar wanka ce.
   Wannan kenan.

  Yau ma da dare kamar yanda Samari suka Saba yiwa Khairat tururuwa Haka Bata kulasu ko ta fita sai ta Kori mutum,a boye Talatu taga Dan gidan Kawarta Laure takarice a Makkah take rayuwa tana turo kudi ta siyi filaye ta bawa danta Hammad Kudi me yawa yake business Yana juyawa ya Zama me kudi,Talatu tasan bazai taba son yayanta ba,sai ta nemi Haj Lauren da tasa danta yazo yaga Khairat ya aureta sai ta samu kudi ta Nan sabo da kwadayi.
   Ai kuwa yau Laure ta bugawa Talatu waya cewar Yarta ta shirya Hammad zaizo ya ganta idan tayi Masa sai ya aura,Haj Lauratu duk tunaninta sabo da Allah take son hada alaka da ita sannan tayi Mata karyar cewa yarta ce ta cikinta,saura kwana Uku Hammad yazo Talatu ta zage tare dasu Zainab sukayi kwalima suka gyara gidan fes gida ya dawo kamar sabo,lokacin Soja Kuma ya koma schl tare da karnukansa Babu ko daya bare su Bata gidan sabo da schl yake kaisu su hade da karnukan makaranta masu gadi,kullum sai an gyara gida an kunna turaren wuta gida ya fito kamar ba shi ba,duk Kaya masu Dirty an wanke tare da killicewa,sannan Kuma kullum sai Zainab ta Kai Khairat Saloon an wanke Mata gashi fresh sabo da bako me kudi zaizo,Khairat Kam tana Jin dadin harkar Nan tuni ta Kara kyau ta fito tsaf Amma ko kadan Bata son Namiji ace ma tana da saurayi ko zata tsaya dashi zance.

   Yaune Hammad zaizo ganin Khairat,yau Kuma Talatu da kanta ta mike tace ai Khairat bakya wanke jikinki ya fita da kaina Zan Miki wanka,Khairat ta bude Dan bakinta tace wlh Ni bazan yarda ba Zaki jawo wlh idan yazo na zageshi ta uwa ta uba,Jin zata cucesu Zainab 
tace kyaleta tayi da kanta Ni dai burina na Samu kudin registration ta silar Khairat,Dan Allah Khairat ki taimake mu Za a rufe registration banyi ba zanyi asarar shekarata,Rahinatu tace muma wlh jibi za a Fara Kora Kuma ba a biya Mana schl fees ba,Dan Allah Khairat karki koreshi,Allah sarki Khairat sai suka Bata Tausayi duk da ita Bata karatun sai tace to idan ya bani Zan karba tunda kun San Ni bana karbar kudin samari in bana sonsa bazan karba ba,Amma wannan idan ya bani Zan karba sabo daku, murna ta Kama Talatu tace me kudine Khairat sosai,Khairat tace bazan roka ba Amma in ya bani Zan karba na baku.

    Suka dinga lallaba Khairat ta yarda da suka koma daki Kuma sai suka Fara zaginta shegiya tsinanniya mu lallaba dai ta karbo Mana kun San Bata da mutunci.
   Da yamma Zainab ta karbo sabon dinkin da suka yiwa Khairat Atamfa me kyau taji dinki Riga da skert Bayan tayi wanka ta shafa Mai me kamshi suka Bata,ta Sa subhannah kamar a jikinta aka tsara dinkin,Zainab da kanta ta tsantsarawa Khairat kwalliya ta kafa Mata dauri kamar Amarya suka Bata sabon mayafi da takalmi dai dai talaka irin kayanta tare da fesa Mata turare.

  Suna zaune suka ji Dirin mota,Zainab ta leka ta wata Yar kafa ta hango Kyakyawan matashi hutu ya ratsashi chocolate color dogo yasha shadda Yana zuba kamshi,Zainab taji Ina ma wajenta yazo da wlh sai ta aureshi wannan Kyakyawa Haka,ga kudi motarsa wata katuwa ta ba million biyar baya,a ranta tace ai kuwa Khairat Baki Isa na bar Miki wannan ba kina Gama Mana aiki Zan aureshi. Talatu ta tura Ummi da tayi Masa iso zuwa palonsu Wanda yake malale da carpet yasha gyara.

    Bayan sun gaisa da Talatu a mutunce sai ko Zainab ta Kai Masa ruwa da lemo tare da cewa tana Zuwa Khairat din,Yana Danna waya me tsada yace ok,Khairat ce ta shugo a nutse dauke da Sallama ya amsa Mata Yana Kare Mata kallo,wani dam gabansa ya buga sabo da tsananin kyan Khairat,tun a lokacin a ransa yace tayi ma wannan dai dai nice dama irinta nake nema a duniya Allah ya bani a ransa yace da kudi Zan siyesu a aura min ita da wuri,Matan yanzu da ka saki kudi sai su aureka ,durkusawa Khairat tayi tare da gaidashi ya amsa yana sakar Mata Murmushinsa me tsada,ita kanta Khairat Bata taba Jin Wanda ya Dan birgeta ba kadan sai Hammad.
   Magana ya fara da nasan kin San komai ma tunda Ummata da Ummanki sun Gama magana, Alhmdllh na ganki kuma na yaba kwarai da tarbiyarki da komai naki ma yayi min, Khairat sai kunya take ji tana boye fuska shi Kuma hakan ya Kara birgeshi Bayan sun danyi Hira sama sama yace sai Allah ya kaimu Nan da sati daya idan na Samu time Zan zo,ga wayata sa min number dinki Bayan na tafi zamu na gaisawa.

    Bani da waya Ni sai ko Nan gaba,kamarki Baki da waya idan Zan dawo Zan kawo Miki inshallah Khairat tace a'a na gode Kawu yace zai siya min,Dole sai na kawo Miki a kyale Kawu ya huta nauyin ya Masa yawa,Shuru tayi kawai tana jinsa ya zaro rafar dubu Hamsim ya ajiye Mata,Koda ya fito zai tafi sai ya bawa Talatu Dubu goma tausayin Kawu Makaho yaji ya bashi dubu Ashirin shima.
   Har kofar gida Khairat ta rakashi mukayi sallama.
   Lokacin sun cika gidan da ihun murna,dubu Hamsim din daya Bata ta mikawa Talatu gashi Nan kuyi abinda kuke so dasu,dubu daya kacal Talatu ta ciro tare da Miko wa Khairat tana hade fuska tace ga rabonki kayan sawa Kuma an bar Miki sabo da kokarin da kika yi kin biya a cikin kudinki,Baki Khairat ta tabe ta wullawa Talatu dubu dayan tace bana bukata bazan auri mutum ba bana sonsa ba ruwana da kudinsa,dan ku nayi sabo da masu komawa makaranta Kar su Samu matsala,Ni Ina da Imani,zuciyata Bata mutu ba kamar ku,Allah ya bani wadatar zuci,sannan Bari har kayan sawarku Zan baku dama badan Allah kuka yi min ba,Ni Kuma Dan Allah nayi Kuma sharrinku kanku zai koma,Nandai Khairat sarkin zuciya ta shige dakinta Wanda ake Tara kayan wanki ta cire kayan jikinta kaf da suka bata ta watso musu ta window tare da maida jemammiyar atamfarta.

    Shewa da ihu sukayi suka kwashe kayansu washe gari da Kudin Zainab ta biya kudin makaranta,Haka su Rahinatu ma,ragowar Kuma Suka dinga cin kayan Dadi iri iri,Khairat kuwa sai aikin tallan Magani suke zuwa da Kawu.

[10/18, 2:48 PM] Sis Asma: 🦚🦚ME MAGANI🦚🦚

By
AsmaBaffa





    
     Fancy Honey,Raliya Nura Lawal,Agas,Queen kk, Amatullah and Maman Ameer ga page naku.









       Washe gari kuwa Kawu yace Hutawa zaiyi sai munyi sati guda bamu fita ba,kudi sun samu sai sun Kare an ciye sannan mu koma,Talatu tace uhm Khairat an washe Baki za a huta to wlh Baki Isa ba kullum sai kin fita kuma da speaker har kasuwa kina tallan maganinki,Kawu yace ai Akan ta huta ma gwara na fasa Hutawa mu fita Dan ubanki tashi ki min jagora yau cikin manyan GRA zamu Shiga unguwar masu kudi tashi mu tafi,Kuka Khairat ta fashe da shi, ta kife a Nan tana ta Rusa uban kuka talla ai gwara a kauye Amma birni kowa Yana kallonta da ace tasan a Taraba Ina danginsu suke na uwa Dana uba da taje Amma Kawu yaki fada Mata,ita Kuma lokacin da iyayenta suka rasu Bata da wayo,sai hotonsu kawai take dashi kala kala,ba yanda ta iya Haka ta mike suka tafi Fara tallansu.

    Katafariyar GRA Khairat taje Kawu suka tafi fuskar Nan Tata kamar hadari yayi bakikirin Tana goge kwallar da take cika Mata ido Kawu ya fara dukan kanta kwas kwas ki fara Mana ya banji kina Tallan ba? Speaker katuwa ta Sa saitin bakinta murya na rawar Kuka tace...ku tashi ku nemi lfy... ,sai da Lafiya ake neman Duniya da lahira..,da lfy ake karatun Qurani....,ba sai na rantse muku ba sai kun gwada maganin zaku ga aiki...idan karya nake bance ku tsine min ba Amma akwai ranar da zamu tsaya a gaban Allah zamu tashi tsirara,Kawu na tsirara Kuma Haka....Allah muka roka ya bamu baiwar magani,Maganin Ulcer,Basir,sanyi,amosani,Ciwon Mara mace idan tana yawan Ciwon Mara Azo ga Magani,wani titi suka biyo Wanda Goslow ya Hadu sosai Karar jiniya suka ji kamar Gomna ne zai wuce motoci kusan guda shida ne rantsatsun gaske ba ta kasa da 20million.
  Ketowa sukayi Amma Goslow wata babbar motace ta mutu a tsakiyar titi,Kawu cewa yake kutsa ciki kiyi talla, Aiko ganin ba sarki sai Allah ta Ware murya tana tallanta ta jikin shegun motocin Nan tazo zata wuce kawai taga suuuuuu Glass din motar  data fi kowacce kyau cikin jerin motocin Nan masu jiniya sunsha tint wani Kyakyawan hannu ne fari Kar Kar kamar na balarabene dan Khairat cewa tayi Kawu ga Balarabe ya Miko Mana sadaka, Kawu yace karki karba Dan mafiya ne yaje ya sace Ni,Mutumin da ya zuro hannu ne ya Miko musu kudi ya gaji da jira basu karba ba,Gajiya yayi tare da Jan tsaki ya leko da kansa kadan kan uba kamar aljani cewar Khairat sabo da kyawunsa,wani kamshi ya cika wajen, tace Kawu Balarabe ne Ni dai Bari na karba Kuma wlh idan na karbo sisi bazan baka ba,Jikin motar ta Karasa tare da Sa hannu ta karba tana angode Allah ya Kara budi Allah ya biya maka bukatunka, Allah ya saka a Aljanna firdausi uban giji yasa kasha ruwan alkausara,in Allah ya yarda baza ka tabe ba a duniya da lahira,Allah ya rufa ma asiri duniya da lahira,Allah ya baka mace ta gari idan Kuma kana da ita Allah ya Kara dankon kauna ya Baku Yara masu albarka,Jin yanda yarinyar ta iya surutu Haka da yanda take ta faman Masa Addua me Dadi Haka wacce ba a taba Masa irinta ba a duniya sai yau.

  Hakan shi yaja hankalinsa ya bar karatun Magazine dinsa da yakeyi ya leko da kansa Dan ya ga wace wannan Haka,Abin mamaki sai yanzu ya kula ma yarinya ce karama ga Makaho Nan ko babanta ne oho ya furta ransa ita kuwa tuni tayi wajen Kawunta tana murna tace kawu wlh dubu goma ya bamu.
   Wayo kawun ya Mata yace laaa muji na taba su Aiko ta Sa Masa a hannu ya fisge da karfi yace Naira Hamsim Zan baki,takaici ya Kama Khairat ta jefar da speaker a kasa ta cakumi Kawu suka Fadi rigija,ta danne Kawu Iya karfinta suna kokawa Yana ihun neman agaji Amma Khairat sai da ta kwace kudin Nan,duk abinda sukeyi Akan idon Balaraben da ya Basu sadakar dariya abin ya bashi a fili ya Furta wonder shall never end, wannan yarinyar karfi gareta,Bai Gama tunaninsa ba yaga ta karkade jikinta tare da daukan speaker ta fara tallan maganin, yau Yaga abinda Bai taba gani ba a duniya mace ta Ware tana shararo karya maganin gargajiya,Kuma yarinya Haka har tasan su maganin sanyi Bai Gama Shan mamaki ba sai da yaji tace Kina mace bakya gamsar da mijinki sai da ya toshe kunnensa da sauri sabo da shi kunya ma yaji.
  Su sukeyi shi yake Jin kunya,a idonsa yaga Khairat tana talla Kuma ta fashe da kuka sosai a titi tana tafiya idan tayi Shuru sai yaga Makahon Yana dukanta da Sandarsa,Shi dai yasan ba wani tausayi ne dashi ba Amma yaji tausayin Khairat sosai,Hanya ta gyaru Nan suka ja motocinsu sukayi gaba abinsu.

    Yau Kuma Talatu ta yiwa Khairat dukan tsiya ta kwace dubu gomanta da Mutumin ya Bata,washe gari kuwa da zazzabi ta tashi me zafin gaske Amma da kanta ta lallaba taje ta siyo magani tasha,.
  Sati na zagayowa sai ga Hammad ya zo da sabuwar waya Infinix me tsada ya kawowa Khairat,yau ma Haka suka gyara gidan tare da Bata kayan Zainab me kyau tasa,ita kuwa Khairat da ya Bata waya taki karba ya damu ta karba taki Karba sabo da tasan ma Su Zainab ne zasu kwace,Amma daya takura sai ta karba a kofar gida ta Shiga makwaftansu ta bayar da ajiya a sirri,Kudi ya Bata dubu Hamsim taki karba,Gashi yau Bai bawa su Talatu sisi ba,sai suka ga Khairat ta dawo ba ko sisi,Talatu tace tsinanniyar tayi halinta na bakin ciki,Khairat tace kwarai kuwa Dole sai da Sa Hannuna zaku samu to daga yau na hanashi sisi baza kuci ba.

    Hmm kawai Talatu tace tana saka mugunta a ranta,Haka Hammad ya sake zuwa Bayan 4,days Bayan Nan yaci gaba da zuwa dake ya iya kalamai sai ya fara siye zuciyar Khairat ta fara sonsa abin sai gaba gaba yakeyi,ganin Haka Talatu Bata samun sisi sai tace da Usy Wanda Khairat ta tsana ya turo da iyayensa zasu aura Masa Khairat.
   Kawai sai Labari taji har an kawo kudin aurenta tare da Usy, sai shirye shiryen bikinta sukeyi,ita Kuma tuni ta tsara barin gidan Baki daya,Amma abinda ya daure Mata Kai sai taga Hammad yanzu wajen Zainab yake zuwa suyi Hira ya tafi,sai daga baya taji ai Zainab ce zata auri Hammad ita Kuma za a hadata da Usy, Khairat tayi ta Rusa kuka sabo da tsakani da Allah ta fara son Hammad, Kwalar Zainab taci tana kuka tace me nayi muku?me nayi muku...me na tare muku?..kun San bakwa kaunata ku kaini gidan rainon Yara mana,..ta jijjiga Zainab sannan tace wlh duk abinda Kuka min bazan yafe Muku ba,Kuma sai Allah ya bi min hakkina,kun San hakane Zainab zaku bashi ku hadasu tun farko Mana,ta Kara fashewa da Kuka ta Gama haukace musu da karfi ta kara shake Zainab me yasa Kuka Bari na fara sonsa,why..why...sai da kuka Bari muka shaku...kuka ta fashe dashi sosai tace Kuma kun San bana son Usy ba mutumin kirki bane shine sabo da kun tsaneni zaku daura Mana aure? Me kika fadawa Hammad ya daina ko kallo na?     Kawu ne ya fito da Sandarsa zai daki Khairat ta rike sandarsa tare da fisgeta Kawu ya tafi taka taka ya Fadi dabar,Tazo tayi jifa Da Sandar lokacin Kuma Talatu a fusace ta bude Baki zatayi magana kenan Sandar ta daki hakoranta na gaba dama wasu cako cako ne Aiko Nan take guda uku Hakoran gaba suka rushe tare da zubewa kasa Hakoran Talatu.jini yayi tsartuwa,Jin Talatu tana ta zubar min da hakora,jini...Kawu yace Khairat bar min gida bani bake Kuma na cire Hannuna a kanki,tsaki Khairat ta ja tace ka cire har kafar taka ba Hannu ba.

     Khairat kuwa tuni ta Shiga Makwaftansu ta karbi ajiyar kudadenta da take Tarawa idan Hammad ya Bata, sannan ta karbi wayarta sabuwa daya siya Mata Infinix ta fito ta shige Napep Bata San Ina zata nufa ba,sai zage gari ake da ita har suka zo Bakar number irin wajen gari suke a Kano ma daga su ba gida gaba ba gida Baya sai Daji.

    A Nan ta sauka ta rasa Ina zata nufa sai tayi hanyar Daji tayi nisa taji kukan yarinya karama a dajin,inda take Jin kukan ta nufa a tsorace sai ko ta iske wata yarinya za tayi 3yrs wata Kyakyawa da ita Fara Tasha Kaya masu kyau da tsada sai kamshi takeyi,Yarinya sai  Mama take Kira tana kuka,Tausayinta ya Kama Khairat ta rike yarinyar tace Mama ce ta tafi ta barki?, Yarinya ta daga Kai,daukanta tayi tare da goyata a bayanta,yarinya tayi Shuru kuwa ta rasa ya zatayi da yarinya,gashi taki yarda Khairat ta ajiyeta, giftawar wata mace ta gani taci wanka Yar gayu ta shige motarta me tsada ta bar wajen da gudu,Yarinya ta kwalla Kara ganin matar ta tafi ta dinga nuna motar tana Mama...Mama hakan yasa Lallai Khairat ta gane uwar yarinyarce ta jefar da yarta kuma ta tsaya ganin Wanda zai dauke ta, Gidan Mai Unguwa ta nema taje ta sanar aka fara bincike Amma ba a San Yar waye ba gashi ta nacewa Khairat kamar jela,Me unguwa da Police suka ce to za a bada sanarwa Amma Dole Khairat ta zauna da yarinyar a gidan Mai gari har na sati daya, Me unguwa yace tunda har taga uwar yarinyar ta gudu to tana sani kawai a rike yarinyar Uwarta zata nemeta da kanta.

    Me Unguwa dai akwai karamci da kirki Haka matansa ma,Khairat ta Zama uwar Dole ita take yiwa yarinyar komai,Ana gobe sati daya taji me Unguwa Yana neman Wanda zai bawa hayar karamin gidansa dake Gwammaja, me daki biyu da Toilet sai kitchen gidan toilet ne kawai da tiles sai kitchen Amma siminti ne ko Ina,Khairat tace wlh Me unguwa dama Ina neman hayar gida,tayi karya Ni karatu ya kawoni Kano Yar Taraba ce,Yarinya kinyi Dace kuwa domin gidan Yana da shago a kofar gida wani Dattijo ne ya Kama shagon Yana Kasuwanci Kinga Namiji a kusa dake Security ne ba Yan iskan da zasu shigar Miki gida da niyyar cutarwa.

    Murna ta kamata tace nawa ne kudin Haya na Shekara?         Hunaif Mahmood Kuwait cikakken sunansa,Mahaifinsa Dan Asalin Kuwait ne Wanda ke kasuwanci a garin Makkah,Mahmood Attajiri ne na gaske,Wanda shi kadai iyayensa suka Haifa Wanda sun Dade da Rasuwa, Hajiya Fatima itace Mahaifiyar Hunaif wacce Bafulatana ce yar Jigawa state can kauyen fulani,Babanta shima ya rasu sai Mahaifiyarta wacce har yanzu tana Raye Kuma tana Makkah tana auren wani Dattijo Dan Sudan, tun Farko da Fatima ta tafi Saudiya acan take zaune suna kasuwanci Har ta auri Dan Sudan,lokacin ita kuma Fatima Bata son zaman Makkah tafi son Nigeria,Wanda acan Kuma ta samu mijin aure balarabe Mahmood Dan kasar Kuwait,tana sonsa ta aureshi ta zauna dashi a garin Makkah,Danginsa ne suka takura basa kaunarta su saidai ya auri Balarabiya Yar uwarsu,hakan yasa suka dinga samun matsala har Allah yasa ta Haifi Hunaif lokacin sun koma kuwait da Zama,Bayan Hunaif Yana da Shekara biyar Mahmood ya saki Fatima Allah yasa ta dakko danta Hunaif ta gudo Nigeria,Mahmood Bai so hakan ba.

   Amma Dole ya hakura ya kyaleta gashi Yana son dansa,sabo da yasan yanda Nigeria take sai ya siyawa Fatima gida a Kano state me kyau ta zauna da dansa Kar yasha wahala,duk watan Allah zai turo Mata da kudi masu yawa Kan ta kula da rayuwar dansa,sannan idan ya samu time Yana zuwa yaga dansa jefi jefi ya koma kasarsu Haka kuma Yana daukansa suje yayi hutu ya dawo dashi Nigeria,Sosai Hunaif ya taso cikin gata,Naira da Hutu ga kyau,Bayan ya Gama Primary Maman Fatima dake auren Dan Sudan ta Mata waya Lallai tayi aure.

  Bayan wata Uku Fatima ta auri wani Alhaji Umar Wanda yayi aure aure da dama Amma baya Haihuwa matansa duk gudunsa sukayi suka auri wasu,sai Bayan auren Fatima ta gano baya Haihuwa sannan baya son Haihuwa Kuma Allah yasa ma baya haihuwar, Alhaji Umar rikakken Dan boko ne,baya kaunar Haihuwa baya son Yara ko kadan,sannan yayi Dace Allah yasa baya Haihuwa,aiki yake a ministry of education,tun sanda Hunaif yana yaro ya tsaneshi sai yayi ta hararsa,Yana zaginsa,ya takura Masa sannan baya son ci gabansa,ganin hakan yana secondary masu tsada a Nigeria sai Fatima ta yiwa Mahmood  magana ya kai Hunaif karatu London inda zai karanci kasuwanci,Unguwarsu daya da Musaf a Kano,tare suka taso shi da Musaf talakawa ne sosai,Haka Hunaif yasa Babansa Dole ya biyawa Musaf makaranta me tsada sukeyi tare tun daga Primary har University a london,Ita Kuma Maman Musaf sabo da taimakonsu da Hunaif yakeyi take mugun kaunarsa Haka ma Baban Musaf,abinda Hunaif yake so take dafa Masa idan yaje gidan kamar zata goyashi,shima Baban Musaf Haka abin gwanin Sha'awa.

   Sai yamma ta farka tana tashi lokacin sallar laasar yakeyi tace na tafi gida sir,na gode Allah ya Kara budi.

  Office din ta kalla tsaf tace Ni dai Banga komai ba jibeshi tsaf, Ina magana kina yi?    Tunani ta katse Masa tace Sir ai mu inda kasan a kauye muka taso Haka muke I'm serious ban taba ganin wannan abubuwan ba sai anan,sannan Ni Tea ma idan bana kaninfari da citta ba ban iya hada komai ba sai dai kawai ka kwankwadi barasarka daka Saba sha zunubi kuwa kayi ta Tarawa kanka ba ruwana.
 
      Ko ka Kira arniyarka ta hada maka amma Ni Nan da kake gani na banza ce ba wayewa nayi ba,Naga Alama ya Furta sabo da magana sai Dole yake yinta.
   Ta gaji da tsaiwa tace to nidai Zan tafi gida Naga yarana,Wani yaron kika Samu again?    Tana fita ya saki Murmushi dimple dinsa ya loba,shi Kam tana bashi dariya wannan yarinyar wacce ko sunanta Bai sani ba,tana fita gefen titi Mararta ta rike again ta rike Mararta tana zaga wurin tayi gabas ta dawo yamma ga Napep Bai samu ba,da gudunta ta Kara yin gaba tana ta falfala gudu  gudu hannunta dafe a cikinta, wani katafaren Hotel ta gani ta shige ciki da gudu,su kansu maaikatan sun tsorata wani Namiji yace lfy madam? Tace Dan Allah ku taimakeni ku bani aron Toilet da daki daya Zan Dan huta,Baki bude suka ce Kudi kwana daya dubu Hamsim da biyar,Baki bude tace bani da ko kwandala sadaqa zaku taimakeni,ta sake rike ciki tana kara, Kamar Aljani taga Hunaif Driver dinsa ya kawo shi Hotel din Wai Yana da Meeting a nan da wasu turawa.

    Bai gane Khairat bace sai da yaji rokonta tana Dan turancinta data iya wani ma Shirme take fada,Tana joyowa taga Hunaif yasha wani wankan daban ba irin na dazu ba,kamshi kawai yakeyi,Magana yayi da Maaikatan da su Bata abinda ta bukata zai biya,da gudu ta shige tana murna,Bayan sun Bata dakin tayi abinda zatayi ta fito tana tafiya a hankali tana rike da mararta,Hunaif a ransa yace sabun Shiga Yan mata an fara period sai iyayi harda Shiga Hotel Wai a Bata  toilet.

    Baki ya tabe an kawo Masa fruit salad ya Mika Mata ta karbe tana godiya ta shanye tace Kai wannan yanzu Zan warke idan har Zan shanye Kofi uku,Wai wayo tayiwa Hunaif Dan ya Kara Mata,Murmushi yayi a ransa yace a karo Mata tana tsaye taki tafiya,Ana kawowa ta karbe tana Murmushi ta shanye kwat kwat tace har na Fara Jin sauki da Zan Kara Kofi daya shike Nan na warke ma,dariya kamar zata kwace Masa yasa aka Miko Mata wani ta shanye,tace yawwa naji Ras Ras yanzu Amma da ace zansha Mango juice to gobe aikin da zanyi a Office Allah ne kadai ya sani.
    Mamaki ya Kama Hunaif Bata koshi tana ta durawa cikinta ruwa,yace a kawo Mata fresh mango juice, aka kawo Mata a wani Dan Glass cup ta karbe tare da Furta ku dinga cika mudu bayin Allah ba kyau wlh,ku sa Babban Kofi sai Kuna saka irin wannan karamin ai salon cuta ne Abu kadan sai tsada ta shanye,Hunaif Yana gefe Yana kallonta tace yawwa yanzu naji dai dai tace na gode na tafi gida Sir fatan dai kasha man mota da yawa yau?     Gabantane yayi mugun bugawa Dam Dam har sau Uku ganin Hunaif tsaye a bakin kofar ta ya gaji da Haduwa cikin kana Nan Kaya wando pencil white da Riga irin ta kamar mawaka doguwa ta sauka cinya silver color da tof a sama Yar pencil dai dai shi me dogon hannu marar nauyi Fara,sumar Tasha kyau ya gaji da haduwa, askinsa kawai da aka yiwa sumarsa abin kallo ne.

    Ko baza ki bani hanya bane ya Furta a nutse? Da sauri Khairat ta gigice tace Uhm...ahm...wuce ...sannu da zuwa Sir,Allah Sa dai ba laifi nayi ba, Baki ya tabe ya kalli gashinta Yana mamakin tsayinsa dama Yan Nigeria na da Natural gashi Haka,Ba tare da ya kalleta ba yace da Daren Nan gashinki a bude a wannan kangon gidan naki me cike da aljanu,kallonsa tayi tace Ni dai Dan Allah Kar kasa na kasa bacci Gidana ba Aljanu,Meenal da Mohd sun ganeshi suka zo wajensa ta janyesu da sauri tace ga abincinku ke Meenal wanne iskanci ne wannan nasa Miki Riga ki tube ki jefar kunki cin Abinci sai magana kuke sani,idan Baku ci ba yanzu wlh bazan tashi cikin dare na Baku komai ba.
   Ta kalli Mohd tace Kai zo Nan Kaci naka Baki bude take kallon Mohd ya kwaso Vaseline dinta a hannunsa da yawa Yana ci,bakin ciki da rashin sabo da rainon Yara kawai Khairat ta Fara Hawaye,tace Ni dai na Shiga uku,na Shiga Uku da wannan Yara kasheni zasuyi kawai su huta.

   Dariya tayi mugun bawa Hunaif ya harde Hannayensa Yana kallon Ikon Allah, Sai ga Meenal ta fito da gudu ta karyewa Khairat Kan janbaki tayi kaca kaca da jikinta.
   Idon Khairat jage jage da hawaye tace ku kashe Ni ki huta kawai,ta jawo hannun Meenal tasa a wuyanta tace shakeni kasheni ki huta,Meenal tunaninta Wasa Khairat take Mata sai ta Fara goga Mata jambakin a jikinta,Khairat ta Dago ta kalli Hunaif tace ka gani ko ka gani ko yanzu Ni ya zanyi dasu ta fashe da kuka tana Yan yaran Nan Basu da mutunci ko kadan so suke su sa min Hawan jini.

     Kallonsu kawai yakeyi suna bashi dariya Kujera ya jawo ya zauna,ita  Kuma Khairat tace Haka zaku yi bacci Ni bazan sake muku wanka ba Dazu Nan nayi muku Dan kuji dadin bacci, Bedroom ta turasu tare da kullesu sabo da Kar su fito,dawowa tayi tace Sannu fa na kyaleka,plate din dake hannunta na danwake yake ta faman kallo har ya kasa daurewa ya kalleta kadan yace wannan abin kika yi? Kai ta daga Masa dazu naji Ina Shaawarsa ko kana ci ne na kawo maka? Da sauri yace ae Amma idan da Egg da tumatir zanci,Allah ya taimaki Khairat tana da kwai guda goma da ta siyo yau zata dinga soyawa su Meenal da safe,tace akwai sai ka Dan jira kadan na dafa Kwan,Ok ya Furta Mata kawai yana zaune Yana latsa wayarsa ta daura a karamar Gas dinta data siya irin Wanda Yan Hostel suke tafiya da ita,minti kadan ta yanka Masa tumatir da kwai a wani Dan karamin Plate na roba,ta zuba Masa danwaken a plate daban me yawa kuwa ta kawo Masa Yajinta me shegen Dadi da Mai har Maggi ta ajiye a gabansa tace gashi Nan, tnx ya Furta Da kansa ya zuba yajinsa Mai da magi sannan ya zuba egg da Tumatir Yana ci,Dadi kamar ya cire Masa kunne Yana kaunar danwake.

    Bai taba jin danwake me dadin na Khairat ba,a hankali yace da me kika yi danwaken dashi? Tace Flour da Garin rogo sai kuka da Kanwa Amma in kana so yafi Dadi to garin Rogon yafi flour yawa.
  Kai ya jinjina yace Zan fadawa Ummi na,Khairat mamakinsa da Dadi ya Gama kasheta Bai kyankyameta ba,har yake cin abincinta duk kudinsa Kuma yazo har gidanta gaskiya Bai da girman kai.

   sai da ya cinye abinsa tas tana gefe a zaune tana kallonsa farin ciki kawai take ji mutum kamar Hunaif yaci abincinta tana ganin ita ba kowa bace,Bayan ya Gama ci tace mu Pure water muke Sha na kawo maka? Kai ya girgiza Mata baya bukata,dama tasan shi sai ruwan roba.
    A hankali yace kin San me ya kawo Ni gidanki?    Da sauri Khairat tace au ci min fuska kazo Yi kenan, to kaje ka auri type dinka ba Ni ba,kawai zaka zo kana ci min mutunci,Ni nace Ina sonka ne.

   Knocking yayi lokacin Khairat an Gama Danwake da kwai yanda yake bukata,harda siyo Masa ruwan Roba Faro da juice na kwali da fresh yo an shirya komai gidan Nan ta gyarashi sai kamshi ko Ina yake,su Meenal sunci Abinci yau da wuri ma suka yi bacci,tayi wanka tasa sabuwar doguwar rigarta ta gwanjo me kyau kamar sabuwa black da adon Golden a jiki tayi rolling gyalen a kanta ga acuci anyi,Maroon jambaki ta shafa,sai Powder tasa kwalli a idonta abinka da fara sai tayi kyau sosai.
    Sai faman kallon mudubi takeyi tana yabon kanta taji knocking sai da tayi yanga sannan taje ta bude, tabarma ta Shimfida Masa ya zauna sai kunya take ji.

     Abincinsa ta kawo ta jere a gabansa da kayan Sha,a ransa ya yaba Mata kwarai yanda tana cikin talauci ta iya kashe Dan kudin nata,yace zauna muyi magana,duk kwalliyar da tayi taga ko kallonta baya yi bare har tasa ran tayi kyau ko ta birge,labarinki Zaki bani kaf,sannan Nima Zan Baki nawa,Khairat ba Bata lokaci ta bashi tarihinta tas,yaji tausayinta matuka sannan yayi Allah wadai da halin Kawu da iyalansa,shima Ya Bata tarihinsa har Dana Musaf Amma a yanda ya fada Mata Sam Bai gane Tuggun Musaf ba,sannan baya zarginsa,gashi duk matar daya aura sai Musaf ya aureta,to Allah ya kawo karshensa a ranta tace sai tayi maganin Musaf zata gano ko ma mene, tunda itama Bata San da wacce zuciyar yake zaune da Hunaif ba,Amma taji tausayin Hunaif tabbas Musaf ke Masa zagon kasa Amma Bai gane ba sabo da bashi da zargi.

    Abincinsa ya fara ci,tace to ya za ayi da Kawu? Ki barshi zanje gareshi Dole kafin auren Sai kin koma gidansa da Zama kinyi hakuri har ayi biki a Gama,karki nunawa kowa ba auren so zamuyi ba,kawai ya Zama sirrinmu daga Ni sai ke.nan da ranar Sunday Zan kaiki wurin Ummi na zaku gaisa,Khairat tace Allah ya kaimu,Danwaken yayi Dadi kuwa? Kallonta yayi kadan yaga Ashe dai tana da kyau matuka,yayi Dadi Mana,da baiyi Dadi ba ai bazan ci ba yarinya.

   Dan lips dinta ta turo ka gani kullum kana ce min yarinya katuwa dani,ba tare da ya kalleta ba yace mike tsaye Naga tsayinki idan har katuwar ce,Mikewa tayi kalla fa kamar Ni ga tsayi kallonta yayi yaga baiwa iya baiwa yace zauna to yarinya ce ke Banga girman ba Ni, ya Saba da ac sai zufa yake hadawa,Mufici ta Mika Masa ba tare da ya karba ba yace ki min fifita Zaki bani da wanne hannun zanyi kina gani daya waya nake Amfani da ita daya Ina cin abinci ya Furta da Shagwaba yanda yakewa Umminsa,dariya Khairat ta Shiga yi shi Kuma Yana kallon yanda dariya ke mugun Kara mata kyau.

  Khairat tace Dan gata ne Kai Allah tana Masa fifita fiii fiii da Mufici,wani Question daya Bata kunya ya zabgo mata marar naki ya daina ciwo ne? Shuru tayi tana kasa da Kai, Hunaif yace wacce kunya Kuma matar da kike talla a titi magani har da na maaurata,ai dai na baka labari Kawu ne ke sani Dole, Uhm ya Furta to kin warke? Ae mana na warke,kwana nawa kika yi? Wai Ina ruwanka ne ban Gama ba to,Baki ya bude yace Lallai Idan kika yi aure na gaskiya Mijin sai ya karo Miki kishiya da wuri,Akan me? ta tambaya sabo da Bata gane me yake nufi ba, Bai Bata amsa ba har ya Gama cinye abincinsa sai satar kallonsa takeyi yanda yau ya Kara kyau sosai, Mikewa yayi yace Zan wuce,to baka bani takar dar rules din auren ba? Zo muje mota ki karba,ok tace ta fito Yana gaba tana bayansa suka je har jikin arniyar motarsa, ya bude Bayan mota ya fito Mata da wata katuwar ledar shopping mall yace gashi  ki bawa su Meenal,ya dauko kyautar Ummi ya Bata gashi inji Ummina tace a gaidaki,mamaki ya kamata tace Ashe dai abin nayi ne.
   Ashe da gaske kake dai  ko?yace kwarai kuwa bana zuwa Abu da Wasa Ni.
   Gaban motar ya bude ya dakko takarda ya Mika Mata an wani bugata yace da Hausa na rubuta miki rules din yanda Zaki Fi ganewa,abinda Baki gane ba ko kina da tambaya to ki bugo min waya Zan ki shirya bikin baifi Nan da wata daya ba,sannan ba wani Event da za ayi frnds na baza su sani ba sai Musaf kawai.
   Zanzo da Ummi mu dauki yaran Nan su koma hannunta, ok tace amma zanyi missing nasu,ke kika sani Ni dai baza kizo Gidana da ko yaro daya ba.

   Sallama sukayi ta koma gida,tana ta murnar kyautar kayan tana Zama ta baje kaya,na yaran chocolate sweet dasu biscuits ne gasu Nan,sai nata Kuma dogayen riguna Ready made kala hudu da mayafansu da takalma da jaka masu tsadar gaske,ga Kuma cosmetics iri iri,taga turaren Ummi ai kawai sai ta mike ta fara taka  rawa tana ta tikar rawar murna,katsam sai ganin Hunaif tayi a tsaye a kanta dama a tsakar gidan ta baje kayan,Sai da ta tsorata sai ta tuna ai kofar a bude ta bari.
   
   Yace wayata na manta tana duba bayanta inda ya zauna dazu sai taga wayar tasa ita murna tasa Bata duba ba,Yana dauka yace Ci gaba da murnarki sai da safe,kunya taji tace na gode fa,ka cewa Ummi na gode.

   Yana fita ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace nayi abin kunya.
 Washe gari da wuri Hunaif ya kwashe labarin Khairat ya sanarwa Umminsa taji tausayin yarinyar tace gwara data bar gidan Kawu wlh ka kaini jibi na dauko yaran dake hannunta ita Kuma taje gaban Kawu Haka ta zauna kafin ayi bikinku,Hunaif yace to Ummi,zamuje ki ebo yaran Amma ita dai sai Nan da 2wks zata koma gaban Kawu sabo da akwai Shirin da nakeyi idan ta koma ko harararta Basu Isa Sunyi ba.
   Ummi tayi Murmushi tace Lallai kana son Amaryar taka din Nan,Babu macen daka damu da ita Haka a duk Wanda ka aura,share zancen Ummi yayi kawai ya fita,sabo da yasan Auren ba na so bane.
    Washe gari ma Khairat Bata je aiki ba,da safe Bayan ta Gama aikinta  komai su Meenal suna wurin Sadiya makwaftansu zata kaisu yawo, Takadar rules ta dakko ta Fara karantawa kamar Haka....

       Rule din farko ba shagalin biki,aure za a daura kawai a Kai Amarya,baza mu kwanta 1room ba,zakina min girki kullum abinda nake so,girmama juna,gaskiya,rikon Amana,Banda boye boye,Ummi na sai kinyi Mata biyya sosai,sannan kullum kece Zaki dinga tashina daga bacci da Asuba nayi Sallah,Haka baza kiyi bacci ba da dare sai Kinga nayi bacci, duk yanda za ayi karki Bari Ummi ta gane bama kwana tare ko akwai matsala a aurenmu,Haka mutane ma,sannan Dole sai kinyi karatu kin Zama me Ilmi Zan dauki nauyi,wannan sune abinda nafi bukata kawai a aurenmu,idan kinyi Haka zamu zauna lfy,idan Baki ba Zan iya Sallamarki da gaggawa,ki guji batawa Mus'af sabo da close frnd nane bana son abinda zai Bata masa.

    Khairat ta bude Baki tace wlh Bai Isa yace bazanyi bacci ba sai yayi sannan Zan tafi na kwanta,Kuma da Asuba kullum sai na tasheshi yaro ne shi ko me,zumbur ta mike da takardar a hannunta ta saka hijab dinta me hannu tayi kyau ta kulle gidan ta fita.bata tsaya ko Ina ba sai a Building din Hunaif Company,da sauri ta wuce fiya fiya kamar zata tashi sama,Allah yasa taga motocin Hunaif Maana yazo Office kenan.
   Aminu Yana Mata magana tace Ina zuwa sauri nake da Sauri ta haura sama.

   Sai da taje bakin kofar Office din Hunaif sai Kuma tsoronsa ya kamata,tasan yanda yake da kwarjini,tsoronsa ma take ji Taya zata iya Masa musu? Amma Bari ta daure suyi magana,Kwankwasawa tayi taji muryarsa me dadin masifa yace come in a gajiye,a hankali ta tura kofar ta Shiga,Yana zaune Yana jujjuyawa a kujerarsa Yana Kora ruwan giyarsa me tsadar gaske.

    Hankalin Khairat ne ya Kara tashi tunawa da tayi yana Shan giya fa,Amma mamakinta idan suna Sha da Musaf Bata bugar dasu sai ka gansu Ras dasu suna komai a hayyacinsu, a ranta tace to sun Saba tabi jininsu,Jin shurun yayi yawa Bai kulata ba kawai waya yake latsawa Yana Kora barasarsa ta katse shurun da ajiye Masa takardarsa a saman table ta Fara magana Morning sir, wannan dokar taka bata yi min ba, guda biyu a cikin bazan iya su ba,tun kafin ta fadesu ya gane wanne take nufi,yaushe Zan iya Zama Dole sai kayi bacci zanje na kwanta jariri ne Kai? Sannan na tashe ka da Asuba ai Kai ya Dace ka tasheni Kaine namiji.

   Hmm yayi Dan guntun Murmushi kana ya kalleta da idonsa me tsananin kyau yace Ummi kike so na Nemo ta min? Ni da kike ganina Haka Ummi take min Bata bacci sai ta tabbatar nayi bacci tana kusa Dani tana min adduoi,idan nayi bacci ta kashe min light ta tafi,sannan da Asuba ita ke tashina nayi Sallah,ai Lada ma Zaki samu idan kuma auren ne bakya so to sai ki zauna a Haka Baki San danginki ba,yanzu Kinga Ni har nasan inda suke a garinku Taraba.
   Jin abinda yace sai Khairat ta turo lips dinta gaba tare da daukan takardarta ta rules tace Haka Zan auri Dan shaye shaye? Nan take idon Hunaif ya koma red yace watch ur tongue shaye shayen me nayi? Tsoronsa ya kamata tace Allah baka hakuri ai ruwa nake nufi ba giya ba,ka fiye son ruwa, tayi waje da sauri.
    
    Tana fita tayi kicibis da Musaf zai Shiga Office Din Hunaif ya bigeta da karfi takardar dake hannunta ta Fadi da sauri ta dauka ta tafi da sauri, shi Kuma yaja kwafa ya tsaneta,me yake kawo ta Office din Hunaif ne shine abinda ya kasa ganewa Kenan Amma a ransa ya kudurce sai ya gano gaskiya.

     Hunaif washe gari da wuri yayiwa Ummi magana suje a kwaso Meenal da Mohd Yaran da Khairat ke rikewa lokacin Kuma Kan Ummi Yana ciwo tace Bazan iya ba Hunaif kaje ka kawo min su kawai.
    Already ya rigada yayiwa Khairat waya Amma yace kayansu kar ta Basu ko tsinke Ummi zata siya musu sababbi masu tsada,Da Kansa yake driving zuwa gidan Khairat,jiki a sanyaye Khairat ta fito da yaranta harda Hawaye Bata son rabuwa dasu,Baba Isyaku ta sanarwa Yace mashaallah kin huta kema Allah ya taimakeki,Khairat tace ai aure zanyi,Shi kanshi Baba Isyaku yayi mamakin ganin Mijin da Khairat zata aura ga kyau ga Naira,su Khairat sun Saba da ganin Hunaif sai Basu yi kuka ba suna ta dagawa Khairat Hannu suna wasansu a mota har Hunaif ya bar unguwar.

    Bayan kwana Uku tsakani Hunaif ya tura Driver ya dakko Khairat tare da kayanta kaf wasu Kuma ta bawa Baba Isyaku,sukayi Sallama da me Unguwa Wanda take haya a gidansa da makwaftanta ta shige mota suka tafi sai gidan Kawu Sabiu Makaho,lokacin Kuma ta bawa Hunaif Address yaje kofar gidan da jerin motocinsa securities na take Masa baya.

     Talatu Jin motoci Sunyi yawa suna ta tsayawa a kofar gidansu sai ta leko tunaninta mutanen Zainab ne ko Kuma wurin Rahinatu suka zo,to ita dai Zainab Bata da matsayin da zata kula irin wannan bare Rahinatu,Talatu taga Hunaif sai tace La balarabe ne to ko Service din Mtn ne ya Fado a gidanmu za a siye gidan? ai ko da munyi kudi,da gudu ta koma gida,tana bawa Kawu Sabiu labari,yaranta sukayi ta lekowa,Lokacin Soja yazo Weekend gida,Zainab tana Nan tana girki zatayi bakon saurayinta daga Zaria.

    Khairat ce sanye cikin doguwar rigarta sabuwa dal wacce Hunaif ya Bata yace tasa,Tasha makeup kowa yaga Khairat zai  rantse Yar gidan wani Hamshaki ce harda sa Takalmi me tsinin gaske tana taku dai dai.
    Gidan ta Shiga da Sallama kwas kwas,Talatu tana ganinta ta rafka salati tana Malam fito kaga Khairat,Kawu yace Ina Naga idon da Zan ganta me tayi? Ta Zama Yar dagwas,Yar gayu,Ashe ita ce tare da me kudin Nan Dana ke baka labari,ai sai su Zainab suka fito da gudu suna kallon Khairat da Hunaif sun jero ga securities suna take musu baya.

    Da sauri Zainab ta Shimfida sabuwar tabarma sai kallon Hunaif sukeyi,Bayan mun zauna ya sallami securities cewar su jirashi a waje,a mutunce ya gaida Talatu ta amsa da sauri tana washe Baki,Kawu ma da baya gani Yana gefe suka gaisa yace duk da bana gani kamshinka kadai ya Isa a San Kai babban mutum ne,Hunaif ya daure fuska ba mutunci yace abinda ya kawoni na dawo da Khairat gidane zata zauna kafin ayi bikinmu,sabo da kyan ya Mace gidan Ubanta ko mijinta,ta bani labarin yanda kuke Mata Kuna zaluntarta,gata na dawo da ita kafin ayi bikinmu ta bar muku gidanku,Wlh wlh kunji na rantse kallon banza kuka yiwa Khairat masoyiyata sai na daureku ko waye ba ruwana,ku Fadi kudin da kuke so na zamanta a gidanku Zan biya ko nawa ne,ba kyauta zata zauna ba,Ammar Wanda duk ya gigice ganin me kudi Haka yace ai ba ko kwandala ma ta zauna sabo da ai mu Yan uwanta ne Kawu ma Babanta ne.

     Zainab tace wlh kuwa ai gidansu ne,Kawu Sabiu yace Wai Kai waye ne Malam,da Sauri Zainab tace wlh Kawu Bin Mahmood ne Wanda ake ta zancensa a radio da gidan tv,Kawu ya ja baya a tsorace wanna yaron Dan balarabe me kudi dai? Talatu tace shi fa,Kawu ya jinjina yace Khairat da samun irin wannan tab Allah kenan.
    Khairat tana iyayi tace ku Fadi kudin zamana a gidanku How much? Talatu tace iyye nasan Zaki aikata Khairat,to ka bamu dubu dari Uku,Hunaif yace kacal? Baki bude Talatu tace kacal duk wannan uban kudin,Yace ga Dubu dari biyar Zan baku check,sannan Kawu bani address na family dinku dake Taraba da Dangin Maman Khairat, jiki na tsuma ya fara musu bayani,Khairat tana rubutawa a paper har ya Gama Basu Address.
    A hannun Kawu ya damka check din kudi Hunaif ya Kara da cewa Khairat kema kamar gidanki ne kudi aka biya su, duk Wanda ya Miki ko Harara ki fada min wlh kunji na rantse sai na daure mutum,aiki ba abinda zata yi muku,Abinci Kuma safe rana da dare.
   Talatu jiki na tsuma tace ba abinda za ayi Mata Abinci ma sai ta barshi,Bayan Hunaif ya mike zai tafi Yace Muje Sweetheart ki rakani mota,kiyi hakuri kiyi manage a wannan gidan da abincin kafi a daura aure,kamar gaske Khairat tace Babu damuwa Honey Dan Allah karka damu da tunanin Ina wannan gida marar kyau Zan jure, Murmushi yayi kawai Yana kallon ikon Allah wurin Khairat yanda take ta yanga da iyayi tana lankwashe murya.

    Talatu tace ai yaro indai Khairat ce zaka Sha iyayi wannan da gidan kudi ta taso to ba a San me zatayi ba sai ta taka mutane,ba Wanda ya kula Talatu sai ma gani sukayi Hunaif ya riko Hannun Khairat suna magana kasa kasa sun fice kofar gida, Zainab ji take kamar ta hadiyi zuciya,Ina ma itace ta samu Hunaif,Rahinatu ma Haka take jin inama itace,Soja yace Alhmdllh na Samu kudin komawa schl,gobe sai makaranta,Rahinatu tace muma a biya Mana kudin waec da neko dama an kusa rufewa,Zainab ta karbi check tace zanje na Ciro kudin Nima gobe Zan koma Hostel.

   Khairat kuwa suna fita ta kwace hannunta wani shock take ji a jikinta Wanda shima hakan Yake ji, dariya sukayi sannan Khairat ta dauki Jakar kayanta da Wanda Hunaif ya siyo Mata sababbi da Wanda ya dinka Mata atamfa,shadda,laces etc,ya siya Mata sabuwar waya katuwa me tsadar gaske,sannan ya Bata 50k tayi amfani dasu.
  Ciki ta Shiga da kayanta sukayi Sallama Kan Next wk su Abbinsa zasu zo daga Kuwait Zasu kawo kudin aure da lefe sai a tsai da Rana.
 
   Khairat tana komawa gidan kowa sai wani Nan Nan akeyi da ita suna lallabata,Kawu yace Khairat Yar Dan uwana,Khairat yata zo Nan muyi hirarmu,yanzu Khairat sai ki gudu ki barmu ko tunawa damu Baki yi ba? cewar Talatu,Khairat sai kallon ikon Allah takeyi.
   Ko tsinke Hana Khairat dauka sukayi sabo da suna tsoro Kar Hunaif ya daure su,duk da Haka Khairat sai da ta Taya Talatu aiki Bata bar gidan da kazanta ba sai da ta gyara ko ina.dakin Khairat ma Talatu kwashe komai tayi na shirgi da suke Tarawa a ciki,Khairat ta gyara abinta.
 
    Saura Kwana Uku dangin Hunaif na Uba suzo neman aurensa yana Kan Hanyarsa ta komawa gida da yamma likis sai motarsa ta tsaya ,Driver yayi iya yinsa taki tashi,sai Hunaif yace jeka hau Napep ka dauko Me min gyara Ni Bari na Kira wani Driver yazo ya tafi Dani,Driver yace to sannan ya Shiga Napep ya tafi,Hunaif yana Kiran Driver Amma taki Shiga,ya fito gefen titi Yana tsaye Yana gwada Kira sai ga wani abokinsu Farouq da mota ta saya hannun Opposite ya tsaya Yana ma Hunaif horn,Hunaif ya daga Masa hannu Yana Shirin motoci suyi sauki ya tsallaka titi kawai wata mota Ta taho da Masifar gudun gaske direct dama Kan Hunaif ta nufa Aiko kafin ya farga motar ta kwashe shi yayi sama ya Fado dam a kasa shi kuma me motar ya take da matsiyacin gudu kafin kace me ya bacewa kowa.

    Babu inda Hunaif yaji ciwo sai a kansa,jini Yana malala a kasa Kuma Yana yashe a kasa,abokin nasu Farouq da gudu ya fito a gigice ya tsallako titi tare da karasowa wurin, mutane sun cika makil a kansa,Driver ma daya dawo da bakanike Kuka ya saki,A motar Farouq aka sashi zuwa asibitin Private,Ummi ma an sanar Mata sai kuka takeyi tun kafin ta Isa asibitin,Musaf shi ya fara zuwa a gigice Yana hawaye, ganin Halin da Hunaif yake ciki da kyar idan zai tashi,kansa ya bugu,a jikinsa Haka lfy Lau Bai ji ciwo ba sai iya kansa.
   Ummi tunda ta ganshi take kuka kawai kamar zatayi hauka.
  Iyayen Musaf ma tuni suna can asibitin,Ummi tace waje zata fitar dashi,Nan tare da Farouq sukayi shige da fice sukayi visa ta Germany kwana Uku suka daga zuwa Germany tare da Farouq da Ummi Mus'af ma ya bisu a baya.

     Meenal da Mohd Kuma Ummi ta kaiwa Yar uwarta Haj Amina ajiyar su Meenal taci gaba da kula dasu kafin su dawo,Su Meenal har sun Saba da kowa harkarsu sukeyi.

  Ummi Hawaye takeyi kawai har suka Isa Germany Hunaif Bai farfado ba,likitoci suka fara aikinsu a kansa Ana ta gwaje gwaje,Doctor ya Kira Ummi ya Sanar Mata cewar Hunaif ya samu matsala a kwakwalwarsa,ko idan ya farka zai iya farkawa da Ciwon Hauka,ko Kuma ya kasa tuna rayuwarsa ta baya,sannan Kullun ko me yayi a ranar idan yayi bacci ya farka bazai tuna abinda yayi a jiya ba,Babu abinda Memory dinsa zai ajiye, kullum idan ya tashi a bacci to fresh zai tashi ya manta abinda yayi na jiya bazai dinga ajiye komai a kansa ba.
    Ummi ta barke da kuka,Dr yace karki damu ko Ciwon hauka ne ko Memory dinsa baya ajiye komai na wani lokaci ne kadan zai warke Baki daya ya dawo normal,sai dai za a dan dauki dogon lokaci,Zan hada ku da babban Dr a Abuja take aiki zaici gaba da kula da magungunan Hunaif sannan ko ya kuka ga canji Hunaif yaje Yaga Dr a sanar mana,sai lokacin Ummi ta Danji sanyi Jin zai warke,dama tashin hankalinta ace bazai warke ba.

     Khairat Bata San me ya faru ba taji duk wayoyinsa basa Shiga har sati guda Shuru ba shi ba alamarsa sannan Bai turo dangin nasa ba,yau Monday da wuri ta shirya taje Building dinsa Company Aminu duk Basu San me ya faru ba su dai sunga ba Musaf ba Kuma Hunaif,Aiki ya tsaya cak,sannan Musaf Kwana Uku yayi kacal a Germany ya dawo Kano Yana zuwa aiki Amma yaki fada musu komai Ina Hunaif yake babu Wanda ya sani,tunanin kowa Hunaif yayi tafiya ne maybe tunda ya Saba.

    Abin takaici Khairat bat a San kowa na Hunaif ba sai Musaf Wanda ya Gama tsanarta,Haka Bata San gidan su Hunaif ba,Bata San Ina su Meenal suke ba,to Taya zata nemi Gidan su Hunaif,zuwanta Company sau uku Musaf ya Mata cin mutunci yace ya koreta idan ma aiki take zuwa ya sallameta,Ummi kuwa tana ganin Halin da Danta yake sai tasa aka rufe a accnt dinsa Baki daya,sannan tabi Companies nasa da sauran Abubuwa da kadarorinsa kaf ta hada kansu ta kwashe takardun komai ta hada su wuri guda ta Adana yanda ba me sanin inda suke Dan ita hankalinta Bai kwanta da Musaf ba,Duk tabi ko Ina ta daura mutane masu Amana data sani suke kula da Business din Hunaif da komai,iya Company biyu kacal ta barsu a hannun Musaf na kano Dana Rivers state, Wanda dama a hannunsa suke,Dalilin Haka yasa Mus'af ya Kara Tsanar Ummi Yana tunanin daukan mataki a kanta mummuna.

   Farouq kuwa mutumin kirki shine ya tsaya sosai yake jinyar Hunaif har Ummi ta dawo Germany suka ci gaba,Kuma Farouq cikin frnds din su Hunaif yafi kowa hankali da nutsuwa Kuma shine Wanda ma Hunaif Bai damu dashi ba baya wani Shiga harkarsa sosai Amma sai gashi Farouq shine yayiwa Hunaif Rana fiye da kowa.
   
    Wasa Wasa Khairat ta Fara damuwa an kwashe 3wks babu alamar Hunaif,tana ta faman sintirin zuwa Company Amma Babu Wanda yake da labarinsa,Koda Musaf yaga ta dameshi ma sai ya fara tunanin mene tsakanin Hunaif da Khairat data dameshi Haka kullum sai tazo Office tana rokonsa Kan ya fada Mata Ina Hunaif yake,ba irin wulakancin da Mus'af baiwa Khairat ba Amma sai yaga ta jure Kullum sai tazo,sai yayi tunanin akwai wani Abu a kasa Bari yayi Amfani da wannan damar ya gano gaskiya a wajen Khairat.
   Katsam yau ma da Sassafe sai ga Khairat tazo da wuri tana ganin Musaf ta dinga binsa tana rokonsa har Office.

    Zama yayi a nutse ya kalleta sannan ya kunna sigarinsa ya zuka tare da feso hayakinta ta hanci ta Baki sannan yace kina so na fada Miki inda yake? Khairat tace ae da sauri,Murmushin mugunta yayi sannan yace fada min mene alakarki dashi? Wanne Abu ne tsakaninku da kika damu kanki sai kin San a Ina yake Bayan ke ba kowansa bace face Yar shara da goge goge?
    Khairat tayi niyyar fadawa Musaf gaskiya sai ta tuna halayensa,sannan ta tuna yanda baya kaunarta sai tace Wani agogonsa ne na Diamond me tsadar gaske yace na ajiye Masa a Hannuna zai karba,Kuma a kalla yace zai Kai Million Talatin,shine Zan bashi abinsa Kuma ban ganshi ba,Musaf yayi Murmushi yace karya kike baki da matsayin da Zaki San sirrin Hunaif ko kadan,kin San zurfin cikinsa kuwa?.
   Bari na fada Miki Khairat kike ko wa Ki daina Bata kafarki kina zuwa Hunaif ya koma kasarsu Kuwait da Zama idan kina da kudin binsa bismillah sai ki bishi Amma wlh baya kasar Nan Kuma ba yanzu zai dawo ba hasali ma ya Gama Zama a Nigeria Baki daya, kajifa mugu.
   Khairat ta yarda Hunaif baya kasar ga yanda taga da gaske Musaf yake fadar Maganar,sai tace to Ba damuwa ta tafi gida jiki a sanyaye tana goge kwalla.
