[10/18, 2:50 PM] Sis Asma: 🦚🦚ME MAGANI🦚🦚





         

                   21-25









Official









By
AsmaBaffa







   Sweet Mum,Ayshertuh,Zee I.G, Queen of Shebah, Hadiza Hussain,Maman Humaira,Mmn Moustapha.
       page dinku ne na hannun dama.






         Jiki ba kwari Khairat ta fito tana Hawaye sabo da tsakani da Allah Dan muamular da sukayi da Hunaif sonsa ya kamata,ta rasa ya akayi ta fada sonsa me zurfi Haka,yanzu ya zata yi,dama karya yake ba aurenta zaiyi ba,gashi yayi tafiyarsa ko sallama Babu,ya rabata dasu Meenal dinta gashi Bata San Ina suke ba,gashi ya dawo da ita gidan jaraba wurin su Talatu Bata aikin komai kuma,duk ranar da su Talatu suka gano ya gudu ya barta Allah kadai yasan azabar da zasu gana Mata,ga Son Hunaif Yana cinta a zuciya,da kuka ta dawo gida,Talatu suna zaune a tsakar gida Khairat ta shugo bako sallama tana Rusa kuka,Bata kula kowa ba ta shige dakinta,Talatu suka Fara kallon kallo da yaranta suna gulma kasa kasa lfy? Ita Kuma me ya sameta? Rahinatu tace oho ko fada sukayi da Mijin yace ya fasa?Zainab tace maybe ciki yayi Mata ya gudu,shewa sukayi da dariya idan tayi wari maji cewar Talatu.

       Hunaif kuwa ya farfado lfy Lau Kuma yasan kowa Yana gane komai daga Sanda Khairat ta samu aiki a Company dinsa zuwa yanzu baya iya tuna komai,Haka kuma duk abinda ya faru yau da zarar yayi bacci ya tashi to ya manta shi,gashi a Haka lfy yasan kowa Banda shekarar data wuce Wanda a lokacin Khairat ta samu aiki a Company baya iya tunata,har hatsarin da yayi baya tuna komai.
    Duk abinda ya faru a ranar kullum kafin Hunaif yayi bacci sai ya rubuta a littafi idan ya tashi a bacci sai ya karanta yaga me ya faru,Ummi in Banda tausayinsa ba abinda takeyi,sai da suka kwashe wata biyu cir a Germany ya Gama Shan Magunguna Dr yace suci gaba da jira watarana zai dawo normal,Amma duk abinda ya faru ko chanji suka gani su sanar Masa a waya,Hunaif shima ya tausayawa kansa halin daya Shiga,Nigeria suka tattara zasu dawo Hunaif yace shi bazai zauna a Kano ba ya Gama Gina katafaren gidansa a Abuja Haka kuwa Suka sauka a Abuja,sannan Ganin zai iya Business dinsa sai ta damka Masa komai,sannan tace ya kula duk abinda yayi Kar ya sake ya kwanta bacci bai rubuta ba.

   Da Farko Hunaif baya rubutawa sai Frnds nasa suka dameshi da karban bashi Yana kwanciya bacci sai ya kasa tuna komai sai su cinye kudin,ganin Haka Ummi ta matsa Masa kullum sai yayi rubutun abinda ya faru kafin yayi bacci, yayi iya yinsa Kan ya samu ya tuna ko wani abune ya kasa,Haka Yana so ko bacci ya kwanta ya tashi yaga ya tuna wani abin Amma ko kadan Baya tunawa,sabo da Haka sai gaba daya Hunaif Rayuwarsa ta canja ya koma so silent sosai baya Magana,Bai son a takura Masa,Ya Zama Masifaffe me bacin Rai da kunci baya faraa ko kadan yanzu.

   Tunda Allah yasa Mus'af ya gano shike Nan ya nacewa Zuwa Abuja wurin Hunaif ko yaushe sai ya shato kudi Wanda zasu Kai million goma sai yace Hunaif ya ranta Masa zai biya, shi Kuma Hunaif ganin Mus'af ne sai yace ka tabbatar ka biyani bashin sai suyi dariya sai shi Kuma Hunaif ganin Mus'af ne Frnd nasa sai yaki rubutawa tuna ninsa zai bashi Kuma baya biyansa shi Kuma baya iya tuna komai.

   Ummi Bata da sukuni ko kadan kullum tana dawainiya da Hunaif ya zata yi taga ya warke burinta kenan.ta manta Kuma Sunan budurwarsa da zai aura tunda Hunaif sau daya ya taba fada Mata Sunan Khairat,Ga yaran tuni Yar uwarta Amina tace ita a bar Mata su sun shaku hakan yasa Ummi ta barwa Yar uwarta su Hajiya Amina kuma tana rike dasu Meenal lfy a garin Katsina da take auren wani me kudi.
   Ummi da kanta ta Nemo Mus'af Kan ya fada Mata Sunan budurwar Hunaif tunda tasan abokinsa ne Dole zai sani, Mus'af yace Ummi wlh ban San Yana da wata budurwa ba Ni,kin San Hunaif da zurfin ciki ba komai yake fada ba,Ummi tace Ni na manta sunanta Amma ya fada min sau daya ko Khausar ko Karimatu tsakanin dai haka,Mus'af sai yayi zargin ko to Khairat ce a ransa,a fili sai yace Babu wata me suna Haka da Hunaif ke muamula da ita,Ummi tace wayyo Ina ma nasanta da Haka za'a daurawa Hunaif aure da ita ko zai samu kwanciyar hankali,bana Jin dadin ganin Hunaif a Haka kullum cikin kunci.
  Harara Hunaif ya watsawa Ummi a boye,a fili kuma ya kwantar Mata da hankali da kalamai masu dadi,kwanansa days suna tare da Hunaif ya tafi Kano abinsa, Farouq kuwa Allah sarki mutumin kirki kullum Yana Kan hanyar Abuja duba lafiyar Hunaif,Har ganin Likita kusan idan lokaci yayi da shi ake tafiya.

     Farouq ganin irin Su Musaf suna ta cutar Hunaif sai bawa Ummi Shawara kan Karawa Hunaif matakan tsaro duk inda zaije da masu take Masa baya gudun matsala,in kaga Hunaif ba karamin kyau da haduwa ya Kara ba sabo da yanda yake samun hutu da kulawa.
  Su Meenal kuwa gani Ummi ta sama musu matsugunni gurin Yar uwarta ba ta damu ta dakko su ba,Ummi sai takaici takeji Bata San wacce Hunaif zai Aura ba bare ta wuce gaba ayi musu auren haka.

    Ummi tana zaune watarana katsam ta tuna Sunan Budurwar da Hunaif yace zai Aura Khairat,tace kwarai sunanta Khairat.
   A waya ta Nemi Musaf ko yasan wata Khairat? Musaf ya sani sarai Amma sai yace Mata Bai sani ba ko daya, Ummi ta gama bincikenta Babu labari sai ta hakura taje ta karbo su Meenal suke zamansu wajenta,tace baza ta bawa Yar uwarta ba ta fasa tunda ita tana da Yara da yawa, Koda Hunaif yaga Ummi tare da Meenal da Mohd Sam Bai sansu ba sai ma tambaya da yayi Ina ta samo Yara? Tace kawai a gidan Raino ta karbo su zata rikesu.

    Khairat kuwa su Talatu sun Fara ganeta,musamman ramar da tayi kullum kuka ne aikinta,gashi an wuce 3mnths Hunaif Shuru kawai sai Talatu ta Fara kokarin dawo da halayyarsu ta Baya Kan azabtar da Khairat,Khairat tana daki a kwance zazzabi me zafi ya Kama ta,Wata kawar Talatu ce tazo daga Abuja suna Hira kawar Talatu Hajiya Abu tace Wai Talatu Ina yarinyar da kuke rikewa ne wannan kyakyawar? Talatu ta tabe Baki tare da cewa tana Nan da ta samo wani attajirin Matashi balarabe Amma munji Shuru.
   Hajiya Abu tace kina zuba Mata Ido ke Kuma yarinya me kyau Haka Talatu ai jarice a wajenki,da kin min magana ai da tuni kin Zama me kudi,Talatu tace Dan manzon Allah?, Kwarai kuwa cewar Abu,ki bani ita na tafi da ita Abuja na kaita gidan wata Hajiya uwar Karuwai ce,Kinga manyan sanatoci,Yan majalisu da manyan masu fada aji ake kaiwa su suna biyan kudi,idan ta samo kudin Rabi naki ne,Uwar dakinsu tana da quarter itama yarinyar tana da Quarter.
   Shewa Talatu tayi tace na yarda,Abu ta ce ai ke kawata bugu da Kari sai dai kiga Kuna zuwa Makkah,motoci sai kun zaba,to yarinyar taurin Kai gareta da kyar zata yarda,Hmm ai karya za ayi Mata kice aiki za a kaita birni tana kula da wata yarinya albashinta dubu Hamsim Kinga taji kudi sannan Bata son Zama daku Kinga zata Amince.

   Hmmm Abu yarinyar Nan addini gareta ko an kaita baza tayi karuwanci ba,ke irin wannan sunfi kowa iskanci ki Bari a kaita ki gani Bayan Haka ma idan Bata son maza akwai Matan Alhazawa da suke neman Mata kyawawa suna amfani dasu Zaki Zama me kudi Ni Nan duk wata Zan karbo miki kudin na kawo Miki ko na Aiko Miki dasu wlh,ki lallaba ta Sigar dabara mu samu kudi ta hanyar wannan zukekiyar budurwar,samun irin Khairat sai an tona kowa sai ya sota.
   Talatu tace an Gama Dole ma ta biki zanyi duk yadda zanyi Dole ki tafi da ita Nima na Zama me kudi,ai yanda take da kyau sai dai kiga Gomnoni na binta cewar Abu,Talatu tace shegiya sai kugu kamar na babbar mace ga kirji me kyau.

    Bayan sun Gama maganganun su Khairat Bata San me suke cewa ba taji dai kawai suna ta faman shewa, washe gari Talatu har daki ta samu Khairat,ita kanta Khairat tayi mamakin Talatu yanda take wani Magana a hankali da lumana,tace Khairat ba wani Abu ne ya kawo Ni ba face Hanyar arziki da Zan Miki,me zai Hana kibi Hajiya Abu zuwa Abuja Zaki samu aikatau Yan share share da kula da Yara a gidan Attajirai Kuma suna biyan kudi me tsoka ko ya kika gani?
   Baki Khairat ta tabe tace me yasa Baki tura Zainab ko Rahinatu ba ai kinfi sonsu a kaina sannan kinfi son ci gabansu Dani.

    Baki bude Talatu tace ai gani nayi kinfi Zainab da Rahinatu nutsuwa da hankali,gaki da hakuri Zaki jure ko wanne aiki,Khairat tunaninta baza ta sake ganin Hunaif ba kawai mayaudari ne,sannan idan ta zauna dasu Talatu tabbas sai ta koma Tallan magani,gwara ma taje aikin share sharenta ya fiye Mata,gashi ko banza zata zauna a Abuja capital city,Murmushi Khairat tayi tace na Amince yaushe Abu zata koma Zan bita,Farin ciki ya Kama Talatu zatayi kudi taje Makkah itama a Fara kiranta da Hajiya Talatu.
  Da sauri tace gobe goben Nan Zata tafi sai ku tafi kawai ki shirya kayanki.

   tun dare Khairat ta Gama shirinta tsaf da Sanyin safiya Abu tazo tace Khairat ta fito Su tafi,Zainab,Rahinatu da Talatu dariyar mugunta kawai suke wa Khairat,Kawu ma tunda yaji kudi za a samu yace Allah bada sa'a.

    Khairat ansa Doguwar Riga dark blue and white cikin kayan da Hunaif ya siya Mata masu kyau da tsada Allah sarki sai Murna Khairat takeyi Bata san Karuwanci za a kaita ba.
   Tasha suka je Khairat da katuwar wayarta da Dan ragowar kudinta dubu biyar tasa a jaka,Abu ta kalleta kawai tana dariyar mugunta a ranta,Khairat anyi tsuru a mota Ana kallon Hanya a zuciyarta Kuma in Banda tunanin Hunaif ba abinda take yi, har sukayi nisa tafiya ake ba tsayawa Ana zarara gudu.

     Wani nishadi Khairat takeyi Bata taba tafiya me nisa ba sai yau, har Waka Khairat take rerawa sabo da Jin dadin hanya tafiya mabudin Ilmi duk ta takurawa mutane a motar tana Danna waya tana wakarta Kuma ba a hankali ba,akwai wata Yar sanda a motar a dauketa zata koma wajen Aiki a Abuja take aiki Masifaffiya ce ta kalli Khairat da katuwar Muryarta tace Dan Allah yarinya ki Mana Shuru kin hana mu sakewa,sauri muke zamu koma aikinmu ke Kuma kin addabi mutane da wake wake a Haka kamar Yar birni,Khairat ta kalli Yar sanda tace yo Kya fada Mana aikin yi,tunda sauri kike wa yace ki fito yanzu ai da Asuba Zaki fito shine Zaki nuna kin San darajar aikinki, Dan kina Yar sanda sai kice baza muyi abinda muke so ba.

   Yar sanda ta Fara masifa kaga yarinya marar mutunci,da Alama Yar kwaya ce ki kalli Uniform ne jikina zanyi maganinki,Khairat tayi banza da ita ta canja salon wakarta ma yi take ba ji ba gani,Haka Yar Sanda ta hakura ta kyaleta,Driver Kuma dama Dan Gulf ne kawai ya kunna wakar Yan Wiwi Khairat ta iya da yawa,Driver har dukan sitiyari yake sabo da dadin wakarsa da yake ji shi da Khairat sun takurawa kowa ita kanta Abu yau tasan Khairat data dakko za a Sha fama da ita.

     Sun Shiga garin Abuja Wani katafaren gida taxi ta tsaya gidan ya Hadu katon gaske part-part ne fadin tsaruwar gidan Bata Baki ne,Khairat Yar kauye ta koma tana kalle kalle,sai da suka Shiga gidan Khairat tun daga bakin gate taga motoci wannan tana wane wannan da Alama tunanin Khairat gidan siyar da motocine Amma sai taga Yan Mata tsala tsala cikin Shiga kusan tsirara suna Fitowa ko wacce tana Hawa motarta suna fita,akwai Wanda Kuma Alhazawa ke saukesu.
   Khairat tun tana yin Shuru ta gaji da gani tace Abu wannan Amma gidan yawa ne Naga mutane Kuma kamar Yan bariki, Abu ta kalleta kawai tayi Murmushi tace Family House ne.

    Me gadi ne ya musu Iso har babban Palon Uwar Karuwai Hajiya Baturiya,Palon ma Yan Mata ne da Shiga tsaraici a waje,Shekeke suke kallon Khairat da Abu,wasu cikinsu har toshe hanci sukeyi,Hajiya Baturiya ta sakko daga sama cikin Shiga ta Alfarma,Dattijuwa ce ta Gama kwarzane fatarta da Mai farin har yayi yawa ba kyan gani,tattijuwa da ita Amma Tasha kitson attach ta Dame sosai tana faman tauna chewgum Fuskarta kwayar kwarjinin musulunci Babu ko digo.

   Zama tayi saman kujera ta Kalli Hajiya Abu sannan tace da Yan Matan dake palonta suna ta faman dannan waya tace ku bani waje,ficewa sukayi Baki daya,Abu tace Hajiya ga wata maaikaciyar na kawo Miki,wannan da kike gani sai kin Sha fama Bata iya komai ba,Murmushi Baturiya tayi tace gaskiya tunda ake kawo min Maaikata ba a taba kawo me kyan wannan ba gata yarinya sannan duk gidan Nan Babu wacce ta Kama kafarta a kyau da cikar zati,Fara Kuma natural wow gaskiya Abu kin kawo min hanya Babba kudin Sallamarki dubu dari Zan Baki cash,Abu tayi guda ayyiriri nanaye tace na gode Hajiya ai yarinyar akwai Shiga Rai mata da maza kaunar ta zasuyi.
   Khairat tana zaune ta kasa gane me suke nufi da maganganunsu,rafar Yan dubu ta mikawa Hajiya Abu,sannan ta kawo dubu Talatin tace ki kaiwa uwar yarinyar,Yarinyar Dole tayi tsada Mata da maza zasu so ta cewar Baturiya a zuciyarta.

   Hajiya Abu da murna tayiwa Khairat sallama tace ta tafi gida sannan ta bawa Baturiya Accnt number din Zainab Wanda za a dinga turawa Talatu kasonta duk wata,tace dubu Talatin din Nan ma gashi Hajiya ki tura musu kawai ta accnt din Zainab yayar Khairat ce,Nan take Hajiya Baturiya tayi transfer Yana Shiga Hajiya Abu Nan take ta Kira Talatu da Zainab suna ta ihun murna kudi sun Shiga,sannan Abu ta tafi abinta ya rage daga Hajiya Baturiya sai Khairat wacce tayi mutuwar zaune ta kasa gane me suke nufi da ita,Fuska Khairat ta kwabe zata saka kuka,Hajiya Baturiya tace No..no..Kar kiji tsoro fa ba abinda za muyi Miki ba cutar dake zamuyi ba,ki saki jikinki,Khairat tace wlh indai kuka min abinda zai cutar Dani na gane sai na Kone gidan Nan Baki daya,Talatu ta zaro Ido waje tace Kone mu zakiyi? Khairat tace da gudu ma kuwa.

     Sama taja Khairat suka tafi,nanfa Baturiya tasa aka kawowa Khairat lafiyayyun abinci taci ta koshi Tasha ruwa da lemo,bacci ya kwashe ta a nan,.
    Washe gari da safe da wuri Khairat ta farka tayi Alwala da sallah cikin dakin da aka Bata a matsayin nata ne,Sabo da Hajiya tana son samun kudi da Khairat sai ta Bata daki kusa da nata Wanda ko part Bata hadawa da sauran Yaran nata sai Khairat.
   Da Asuba Khairat ta Ware Murya tana rera Karatun Qurani ka rantse a radio aka kunna,Hajiya kasa bacci tayi Khairat ta dameta,har dakin Khairat tazo tace Dan Allah ki rage Murya Mana wanne iskanci ne wannan kin hanani bacci,a Nan gidan ba a wannan karatun,Hajiya ai sai kice ku arna ne ba Wai kizo kina min tsawa ba cewar Khairat,Baki bude Hajiya take kallon Khairat, Khairat tace kiyi hakuri Hajiya na manta Ashe Baku da addini gidan Maguzawa ne na kiraki da Christain, duk yaranta Babu wacce ke iya Kallon ta ma bare ya iya Mata musu sai Khairat ma  bakaken magana take fada mata.
   Hajiya tace ke karki yi tunanin Wai ke wata ce da har Zaki fada min bakar magana wlh zanyi maganinki Naga waye ubanki a kasar nan,bani da mutunci ki kiyayeni Ina da Marasa mutuncin da Zan turo su Gyara min ke.

    Qur'ani Khairat ta rufe tare da ajiyewa gefe tace Hajiya kija mutuncinki Ina girmamaki ne a matsayin ke Babba ce,Marasa mutuncin naki ki turo su mana ai Ni irinsu nake nema, bana son zaman lfy Ni Nan da kika ganni,abin ya ba Hajiya mamaki Wai duk rashin kunyar da yarinyar tayi Mata Ashe Nan girmamata tayi,Ashe za ayita cewar Hajiya tace to mu zuba, ta fita sai kitchen tace Kar a sake a bawa sabuwar bakuwarta ko ruwa.
    Khairat Misalin 11am yunwa ta Fara damunta ta fito tana neman Hajiya ta ganta a Palo,tace Hajiya Ina kwana ko kallonta Baturiya batayi ba,Khairat tace Hajiya a nuna min aikin da Zan Miki su goge goge da share share me zanyi a ciki? Dariya Hajiya tayi da wasu Yan Matan Dan sun San aikin Khairat,Hajiya tace jeki huta sai zuwa dare Zaki ga aikinki.
   Khairat tace to yunwa fa nake ji ya kamata a bani naci na koshi Zan Fi Jin karfin aikin, Nayi me kyau,Hajiya Baturiya tayi Murmushin mugunta tace ai Nan gidan kowa ci da kansa yakeyi,idan kina da kudi ki kawo a siyar Miki da binci plate daya dubu biyu,Ido Khairat ta zaro Ni da Zan Miki aiki Kuma Ni Zan siyi Abinci?.
   Hajiya tace ga Yan Mata Nan tambayesu kiji komai a gidan Nan na kudi ne,ai ko sai Khairat taga Yan Mata suna ta bada kudin Abinci idan kin biya kudi sai ki Fadi me kike so Sai Hajiya tasa Yan aikin Abinci su dafa Miki a Baki.

    Khairat tace ban fa gane ba Hajiya ya kuke rayuwa kamar ba bil'adama ba? Baturiya ta kalli Khairat kawai ta dauke Kai,Wata budurwa Yar kwallisa tace in Zaki kawo kudin Abinci yarinya ki kawo ba a aikin banza a nan Yar kauye kawai,jahilar Ina ce ke baza ki gane ba,ko iyayen naki Basu sanar Miki me ya kawoki Nan ba? Khairat tace Ni Marainiya ce ku taimaka min,Yar budurwar tace wannan jaka ce gaba daya Bata ganewa, Khairat tace nice Jakar? Ae da mece ai ke kinfi jaka jakanci ma,Tasss kake ji Khairat ta kwashe Yar budurwa me ji da kanta da mari tare da cin kwalarta ta makata da bango ta shaketa Kam.

    Hajiya Baturiya ta fara tafi raf raf...tace Wannan kin dace da gidan Nan wlh irin wacce nake nema ce.
  Nan take Hajiya tace a bawa Khairat abinda takeso taci kyauta,me aiki ta tambayi Khairat me za a kawo Miki,Khairat tace soyayyen kwai,chips,bread,shayi hadin kauri.
   5mnt aka kawowa Khairat taci ta koshi tace Kwan da aka soya yayi kadan ta shige kitchen da kanta ta soya kwai wani me Fadi fakaka ta karo bread taci abinta ta tafi dakinta tayi wanka,Hajiya ta fito tace Khairat tazo zasu je Shopping,Kamar me Hada Lefe haka Hajiya ta hadowa Khairat kaya na gani na fada readymade ba abinda Babu ga kayan kwalliya,wasu Kuma laces,atamfofi da shadda masu tsada suka tsaya aka bada dinki.

    Tunda Khairat tazo gidan ba a Zama lfy da ita kullum sai anyi fada da ita,cikin kwana Uku kacal ta buwayi kowa sabo da Babu wacce ta Isa ko kallon banza tayi mata sai ta Rama Har Hajiya Baturiya tasan Khairat ta Gama sabawa da masifa da rashin son Zaman lfy ga karfi, Amma Kuma duk yawancin Karuwan gidan daga kauye suke Khairat kuwa daga birni take idonta a bude Kar yake,Dan ma yarinyace shi yasa wani abin Dole ake Mata wayo.
   Bayan kwana Uku Hajiya Baturiya da kanta ta karbowa Khairat kayan  sawarta wurin tela,Murna Khairat take kamar me,tunaninta a banza aka siya Mata Kaya kamar lefe komai akwai har akwati Uku,ga gyaran jiki kullum yanzu Sai Hajiya Baturiya ta kaita kamar Amarya,Gashinta yasha gyara,skin dinta kamar daga engine aka fito da ita,sai kamshi take ta ko Ina,Nan fa Yan Matan gidan suka Fara kishi da Khairat sun San zata kwace musu Customers.

    Khairat Kuma ta Fara zargin ba sanaar arziki akeyi a gidan Hajiya Baturiya ba,da dare sai taga Yan Matan gaba daya suna ta fita a motoci wasu Kuma Ana zuwa daukansu manyan masu kudi,duk kusan basa kwana a gidan,wasu ma idan suka tafi basa dawowa sai Bayan 1wk,Sannan ko wacce ta dawo zata kawowa Hajiya Baturiya naka kason makudan kudaden,ga maza Alhazawa suna sintiri a gidan Nan ma suna bawa Hajiya kudi,sannan kullum ba a zaman lfy a gidan Yan Matan fada sukeyi harda wukake da kwalabe kamar zasu kashe kansu,ga shaye shaye na kayan maye.

    Hajiya Baturiya tunaninta Khairat Bata da wayo Bata San Khairat tayi sanaar tallan maganin gargajiya ba har da maganin Mata,sai ta kawowa Khairat maganin tsumi na Mata Wanda zai sa Khairat Sha'awa da son maza tace ta shanye,tana fita sai Khairat ta juyeshi a toilet ta Kora ruwa ya tafi,sai ta koma tace gaskiya Hajiya maganin Nan da Zaki a Kara min, Hajiya Baturiya sai Dadi take ji tana bawa Khairat tana zubarwa ita Kuma.

     Yau Kuma Saturday Hajiya Baturiya sun Gama Magana da wani Senator yau akwai budurwa sabuwa dal me tsada zata tayashi kwana su Sha weekend me Dadi da Khairat,Hajiya Baturiya tace yarinyar me tsada ce Haka Senator ya biya Hajiya makudan kudade yace yaronsa zaizo ya dakko Masa Khairat zuwa Katafaren Hotel din  da zaiyi weekend. 
   Da dare misalin 9pm Hajiya tace Khairat taso maza ga me kwalliya tazo Zaki fita aikinki yau zai Fara,Khairat Ita dai wanka tayi kawai ta Gama gane nufin Hajiya Baturiya,me kwalliya tazo ta shirya Khairat kamar zataje gasar sarauniyar Kyau,wata Gown me Masifar kyau aka sa Khairat tasa,kowa ya ganta sai yaji kamar ya hadiyeta gashin Nan yasha gyara,ga takalmi me tsinin gaske da Yar pose hadaddiyar gaske,su kansu Yan Matan gidan sakin Baki suka yi suna kallon Khairat.

    Yaron Senator Yana gidan Yana jiran Khairat,Har mota Hajiya ta raka Khairat ta Shiga arniyar motar yaron yaja Khairat sai Hotel,a hanya Khairat tace ya tsaya zata siyi paracetamol a chemist,Wani katafaren Chemist Khairat ta Shiga,duk Wanda yaga Khairat sai ya rantse ko jini Bata hada da musulmi ba,a sirri ta siyi Magunguna wurin me Chemist ko na mene oho Sannan ta fito ta Shiga motar suka tafi Hotel.

         Katafaren Hotel din suka tsaya,yaron Senator sai wani yabon Khairat yake, Yana wlh kin Hadu Hajiya,irinki Ogana yake nema,komai yaji Har Room din Alhaji Senator ya raka Khairat yace Hajiya asha weekend Lfy a fito lfy,bana dake Alhaji zai tafi aikin Hajji.
    Khairat ta Shiga daki sai taga shirgegen Alhaji yaci kudin talakawa ya koshi Yana kwance saman makeken bed Yana kallon News,Tsoro ya Gama Kama Khairat sai karkarwa takeyi,Alhaji ya saki Salati yace Baturiya Bata taba hadani da irin wacce nake mafarkin samu ba irinki,ki saki jikinki Maganar Kudine kin samu an Gama,ko me kike so Zan Miki a duniya ,Fadi me kike so Yan Mata,gida? Mota? Ko kudi Fadi million nawa? Dabara ta fadowa Khairat tace jikina yafi karfin a siya ko ba sisinka Zan baka.

  Alhaji ya washe Baki yace Amma kina da aji Yan Mata sai kin Fi cin kudina wlh,Khairat ta zauna gefen bed ta tsiyayi lemon data ga Yana Sha ta kurba tace je kayi wanka so nake nayi bacci da wuri.

    Alhaji ya Gama susucewa ya rude yace nasan Baki sunana ba,nine senator Mudassiru,Khairat tace Mashaallah Ka ganka kuwa kamar yaro Dan 35yrs,Dadi ya Kama Alhaji Mudassiru shi Bai yarda ba yaro ne gashi tsofai tsofai dashi.
    Yana Shiga wanka Khairat ta zaro maganinta ta zuba a lemon Alhaji Mudassiru ya narke,Bayan ya fito daga Wanka ta Mika Masa yasha lemonsa suna Hira tana ta zugashi Tane kiransa da Baby,Sai bacci ya kama Alhaji ya kwanta sai munshari kwarrrrr kwarrrrr kamar Ana Jan rago za a kaishi kasuwa,Yar karamar wuka Khairat ta zaro ta samu kirjin Alhaji kamar ta samu Kwaryar Yan fulani Haka ta Zane kirjin Alhaji tatas jini na tsatstsafowa a wajen ba kyan gani, ta Haye Saman bed ta dauko Reza sabuwa ta samu gashin Alhaji da yasha gyara da aski me kyau ta zauna ta askeshi tas tayi masa kwal kwal sannan ta bar Masa wata Suma a tsakiyar kansa tayi wani toluwa kamar askin yaran Fulanin daji,kowa yaga Alhaji sai yasha dariya, kwashe kayan sawarsa tayi ta cire Masa ATM card da kudi etc ta ajiye a gefen bed ta zuba kayan sawar Alhaji a bakar Leda sannan ta rubutawa Alhaji short note a paper kamar Haka: Dattijon banza nafi karfinka,Ni ba Fasika bace,jikina yafi karfinka,in kana da duniya baza ka samu budurcina ba,Allah ya shiryeka da masu Hali irin naka, ta ajiye Masa gefensa tayi waje tare da barin Hotel din.

    Taxi ta Shiga ta koma Gidan Hajiya Baturiya,Hajiya tayi mamakin ganin Khairat ta dawo,tace Lfy na ganki shi da yace weekend zakuyi tare,Khairat tace Kira ya samu na gaggawa zasu je Dubai meeting da shugaban kasa, Number dinsa Hajiya Baturiya ta Kira yafi sau goma Alhaji Yana can yana baccin maganin Khairat data Sa Masa da tsagaggen Kirjinsa.
   Khairat ta Kalli Hajiya tace ai na fada Miki baza ki sameshi ba,Hajiya tace ya Alhaji zai min Haka,Amma Bari zai sameni gobe akwai wani Danmajalisa Already ya biya kudinsa ma wajensa Zaki tafi gobe, Khairat tace Allah ya kaimu,Kinga kayan Alhajin ma nace Dole sai ya bani sheda na kawo Miki kar kice ko karya nake Miki banje ba,Hajiya ta karba tace tabbas kayansa ne,na yarda dake Khairat,Amma Banda Shirmenki ya Zaki sa Alhaji Dole sai ya Baki kayansa,Khairat ta turo bakinta kadan tace ai sabo da Zaki Fi yarda Dani ba Wai naci amanarki bane ko?
   
   Farin ciki ya Kama Hajiya tace Haka nake son mutum me gaskiya da Amana,jeki ki karbi Abinci abinda ranki yake so kici kyauta,Khairat ta tafi a ranta tana yawwa saura na gobe Kuma zanyi maganinki.
    Khairat ta Gama shiryawa su Talatu Mugunta tunda ta gano cewar Karuwanci suka kawo ta,Sai cikin dare ta dauki waya ta Kira Number Zainab,Zainab tana dagawa Suka gaisa da Khairat tace Dan Allah bawa Ummanki waya,Talatu tana kusa Jin Khairat ce tace Alo...Alo Kharait tawa Talatu ce mene ne Khairat wani abin Alheri ne ya samu? Khairat tayi Murmushi tace Umma ki fadawa Kawu Allah ya kiraku bana,Talatu tace Allah ya Kira mu Ina Khairat? Umma Ashe Kiran da Allah ya muku da wuri zai tabbata, Nifa ban gane ba cewar Talatu, Khairat ta Furta Makkah fa nake nufi Umma Allah ya kiraku bana,wani mashahurin me kudi ne ya bani Kujerar Makkah guda uku shine nace na baki daya na bawa Kawu guda Daya kawai kuje kuyi International passport Zan zo mu tafi tare mu uku.

   Haukacewa Talatu tayi da ihu da murna ta gigice,da gudu ta fada Dakin Kawu tana bashi labari,ya fara murna,su Zainab Nan suka Kara Kiran Khairat tana dagawa Zainab tace Hajiya Khairat Dan Allah Nan gaba ko Umrah ce muma ki samo Mana kujerar Makkah ko ni da Rahinatu ce muje Makkah muma, Khairat tace karki damu Ni nake sa Alhazawa masu kudi damun Kujerar Makkah wajena ba komai bace,Allahu Akbar mashaallahu cewar Zainab.
   Suna Gama waya Khairat ta dinga sheka dariya a dakinta,Hajiya Baturiya ta samu a bedroom tace Hajiya Dan Allah ki ranta min dubu Hamsin kiyi min transfer ta accnt Dina kafin zuwa gobe Inshallah idan naje wajen Alhajin da Zaki hadani dashi Zan biyaki, Hajiya Baturiya Dadi ya kamata Khairat ta dauki Darasi zata Fara samun kudi da ita,sabo da Khairat taji dadin Yi Mata aiki sai tace tsakanina dake yanzu babu Rance Zan Baki kyauta ma,burina kawai ki taimaka ki Nemo mana kudi masu yawa yanda kike me kyau Haka Babu Wanda bazai so ki ba,kin ganki kuwa Khairat,ko Na hada ki da Mata ne masu bukatar irinki Nan ma mu samu kudi?

   Khairat a ranta ta dinga tsinewa Hali irin na Hajiya Baturiya a fili Kuma tace Ina so Hajiyata ai Ni duk inda kika ce Haka za ayi,Hajiya tayi dariya tace an Gama yata,nan take Baturiya tayiwa Khairat Transfer,Khairat tana ganin Alert itama sai tayiwa Zainab transfer ta kirata a waya tace kudin International passport ne ki bawa Kawu da Talatu suje suyi Passport kwana Nan zasu tafi,Nan suka Kara tabbatarwa Khairat abin nata da gaske ne,murna ba a magana Kawu harda kukan murna.
  
Alhaji Mudassiru kuwa Yana farkawa daga baccin kwayar da Khairat ta Sa Masa a lemo ihu ya saki ganin Kirjinsa a tsatsage ko Ina jini ya dankare har ya fara bushewa,Bai Gama firgita ba sai da ya shafa kansa yaji wayam sai toliyar gashi a tsakiyar kansa,a fili ya Furta na tabbatar yau Aljanna Hajiya ta hadani da ita,Nan take ya nemi wayar Hajiya Baturiya tana dagawa ya ci Mata mutunci yace kinzo kin hadani da Aljanna zata dauki raina,Hajiya na bashi Hakuri yace wlh Dan kina min abin arziki ne kadai yasa na daga Miki kafa Amma da wlh sai naga gatanki a kasar Nan,kamar Ni Senator ki kawo min yarinya Yar iska duk ta keta min kirji ta Mai dashi kamar atamfa ko yadi,yanzu da wanne idon Zan kalli yarana, da Kyar ya karbi tuban Hajiya Baturiya sannan ya Kira babban yaronsa ya kawo Masa kayan sawa da Shaver gashin data bar Masa a tsakiyar Kai ya Karasa askeshi,sannan yayi wanka tare da gasa Kirjinsa da ruwan zafi Yana kwala ihun zafi Toilet.

    Hajiya Baturiya ta samu Khairat tace ke Dan ubanki me kika yiwa Senator Mudassiru? Khairat gabanta ya Fadi ta daure tace Ni ban sani ba yace min kawai Yana da Meeting zai tafi Dubai,Ni ban San abinda akayi Masa ba,Baturiya tace wlh kika sake na bincika na gano gaskiya wlh sai na sa an kusa halaka ki a gidan Nan,Khairat tace yo Ni kawai kyaga laifina ni ba ruwana, kwafa Hajiya taja tare da ficewa a fusace,Khairat taja tsaki tayi kwanciyarta tana tunanin Hunaif dinta.
    Da wuri Talatu da Kawu suka je Office din Immigration aka musu Passport na tafiya aikin Hajji,suna ta murna ba ruwansu da tunanin Khairat ko kudin Bata hanyar Halak bane kawai su dai suje Makkah.

    Ummi da Hunaif suna zaune lfy sai dai rayuwar Hunaif yanda ta canja kawai abin baya yiwa Ummi Dadi,kullum cikin kunci yake,Masu aiki a karkashinsa ma yanzu basa Jin dadinsa gaba daya ya canja ba mutunci ba ko Murmushi,frnds Dinsa baya muamula dasu sai kawai dai Musaf sai Farouq dake kula dashi sosai.
    Ummi na zaune da yamma ta gama shiryawa Danta Abinci lafiyayye sai ga Musaf ya zo daga Kano,Ummi tana ganin Musaf yazo ranta ya baci Amma Bata nuna Masa ba suka gaisa yace Ummi Ina Hunaif? Yana samansa,yanzu kazo? Ina su Mama fa?suna Nan lfy sunce a gaida ki,jeka wajensa sai kuzo kuci abinci.
   Part din Hunaif ya nufa,Yana zuwa ya iske Hunaif a palonsa Yana kallon News ya Kara wani azababben kyau da Yar kiba sabo da hutu, Mus'af bakin ciki ya kamashi ganin kullum Hunaif ci gaba yake Kara yi,Harara ya watsawa Hunaif ba tare da ya gani ba,suka tafa yace mutumina kyau kake karawa,Allah ya baka lfy dai ka warke, Hunaif yace Ameen Ni mamaki nake Musaf Wanda ta ya bana tuna abinda ya faru na last year sannan ba abinda zai faru yau gobe idan na tashi komai bazan tuna ba Musaf,yanzu kaga dai muna tare to Wlh gobe Ina tashi a bacci Zan manta komai, Farin ciki ya Kama Mus'af a fili Kuma ya nuna kalar tausayawa harda hawayen Kuka yace kayi Hakuri in Allah ya yarda zaka dawo Normal,naso ace Naga uban waye ya kadeka a mota ya gudu wlh da sai na daureshi har abada,Ni ban yarda da mutumin ba turoshi akayi ko dama haushinka yake ji ko waye ma. 

   Murmushi Hunaif yayi tare da cewa kaddara ce kawai Allah ya saukar bana zargin kowa,nanfa suka barke da hirarsu ta abokai daga Nan suka ci abinci tare suka je masallaci tare,washe gari Mus'af yace jirgin karfe biyar zai bi ya koma Kano,Hunaif yace me ya kawoka Abuja ne naji kace China zaka je a week din Nan,Musaf yace wlh kuwa Hunaif kudi ne Banda su Kuma Ina so Na Fara shigo da Kaya kasar Nan Ina Kara fadada Business dina, Hunaif ya manta da Yana ta rantawa Musaf kudi different time kawai yace million nawa zata maka? Yace Million Bakwai ma ta isheni,Nan take Hunaif ya Masa transfer sannan ya rakashi har Airport ya dawo gida,Ummi Bata San me suke ciki ba,yau tayi sauri tun kafin Hunaif yayi bacci ta sameshi tare da tambayarsa me Musaf yazo yi? Ummi ba komai fa,Bata Rai Ummi tayi tace wlh idan baka fada min ba Hunaif sai na Saba maka, kiyi Hakuri Ummi kudi yace na ranta Masa million Bakwai,Baki bude Ummi ke kallonsa,tace Hunaif rannan fa naji ka bashi million goma,Hunaif yace yaushe? Ni bani bane kin San bana iya tunawa,Ummi tace bani wayarka Hunaif, Mika Mata yayi ta canja Masa sabuwa da sabon layi tayi Masa copying numbers na layikansa ta bashi gashi Nan kayi amfani da wannan Babu wani rancen da zaka sake bawa kowa,Kuma daga yau ko nawa zaka karba Ni Zan na baka da kaina tunda Kai Mus'af yafi kowa a wajenka, Saman Cinyar Ummi ya kwantar da kansa ya Mata shuru, ta Gama fadanta ta kyale shi ta koma lallashin abinta Kuma.
   
    Hajiya Baturiya yau tasa aka tsantsarawa Khairat kwalliya cikin wani danyen Material me azabar kyau da tsada,Riga da skert Tasha kyau Amma sun fito da surarta Haka tasa Driver tace ka kaita gidan Hajiya Bara'atu matar Ambassador Safiyanu Maharez, Khairat tace Hajiya an fasa Dan majalisar ne? Harara Hajiya ta watsawa Khairat tace ae Bara'atu ce ta bani kudi me yawan da yafi na Dan majalisar yawa shi yasa nace kin fasa zuwa wajensa yau sai Gobe yanzu wajen Bara'atu za a kaiki ki tayata kwana saura kuma kiyi Mata wani abin wlh sai kin gane kurenki idan Baki Bata hadin Kai ba.

   Khairat tayi Murmushi ta kalli Hajiya tace ko Dabbobi Hajiya basa neman jinsinsu sai Dan Adam da Allah ya musu daraja,kalli fa Duk abinda nake dashi tana da shi,iri daya ne fa idan ba kwakwalata zata yi ba me zata iya min ta gamsar Dani?
   Rankwashi Hajiya ta zubawa Khairat tace kije haka ai Business ne,Driver ya Kai Khairat hadadden Guest House din Hajiya Bara'atu Wata me aiki ce tazo tayiwa Khairat iso har cikin gidan,katafaren gida ne na gani na fada,Ga bedrooms na Alfarma ko Ina Yan Mata a cikin gidan tsala tsala ko wanne room free to enter ne Mata suke cin karensu Babu babbaka.
   Ko wace taga Khairat sai ta hadiyi yawu suna kallonta kamar mayu,Hajiya Bara'atu taga Khairat tun kafin ta karaso ta Fara Lashe Baki ganin irin budurwar da Bata taba samun ko shigenta ba.
   Na take ta Kira Hajiya Baturiya ta Kara Mata dubu dari biyar kyauta sabo da Jin dadin kalar budurwa irin Khairat da aka Bata,Hajiya Baturiya sai Murna takeyi.
   Khairat ta zauna a kujera tana tauna chewgum Hajiya tace sannu da isowa Babyna.

   Khairat ta kalleta kawai fuska ba rahma tayi kas kas da Chewgum tace yawwa sannu Iya,Iyata barka da hutawa,Ido Bara'atu ta zaro Iya fa kika kirani yanzu ki kalleni Sweetheart kice min Iya nayi Kama da tsohuwa?
   Khairat tace to da mece Gododo dake tsofai tsofai ki bar mijinki kina neman Yara Mata ai gwara ki nemi Maza,tunda Haka kike so ai shike Nan Ni ba ruwana iyaka ci na Miki abinda kike so na tafi.
   Hajiya Bara'atu tayi Murmushi tace indai Zaki min yanda nake so ai ba damuwa wlh ko nawa ne Zan iya biyanki matukar Kika bani farin ciki an Gama,Khairat tace a kawo Abinci naci yanda Zan Fi Jin dadi,Hajiya tana wani fari da Ido tana yiwa Khairat kallon so tasa aka cikawa Khairat gabanta da kayan alatu iri iri,Khairat taci ta koshi ta kalli Hajiya tace ya kike kallona ne kamar mayya ne? Idan ban kalleki ba wa Zan kalla kin hadu da yawa khairat, dare ne yayi Khairat duk tayi sallolinta har Isha sannan tace Hajiya ki kwanta sai tsakiyar dare zamu yi harka,Hajiya taci kwalliya ta hade cikin kayan bacci,tayi tayi Khairat ta Sa kayan bacci taki yarda.

    Khairat ta Haye Saman bed ta kwanta tayi lambo kamar me bacci,Hajiya ta  yi tunanin Khairat bacci take ta tube tayi tsirara sannan ta haura saman bed kusa da Khairat ta makalkale Khairat a jikinta,Khairat tace Wai mene Haka nake Jin Kirji kamar Slifas Wanda akayi da fatar Giwa a jikina,gefe ta matsa tace Abu kamar gugan Danko na ebo ruwa a rijiya,Hajiya dai Hankalinta ya tashi sai ta ja Hannun Khairat ta daura a kirjinta,takaici ya Kama Khairat tace Wai mene Haka kina yakushi na, ganin za a samu matsala sai Khairat tace Darling Bari dai na Miki kiji Dadi,kamar gaske Hajiya ta fara Murna Khairat tace kwanta ki baje,Hajiya tayi dai dai a saman bed,Da dabara Khairat ta dakko dakakken Yaji ta zuba ya Kai Rabin spoon a farjin Hajiya Bara'atu,Mai makon Hajiya taji Dadi sai Balai ya biyo baya,Ihu ta kwarara Wanda ya gigita Yan iskan gidan Baki daya,sai ko Khairat ta dire a kasa ta kwashi takalmanta da Jakarta da komai nata ta rike a hannu ta fice da gudun tsiya.

   Hajiya tana ihu da birgima a kasa ta fito tsirara tana ku Kama min shegiyar yarinyar can ta kasheni,wuka ta caka min a kasana na,wayyo karfe ta zurkuda min,Nan fa Hajiya ta Fadi tana ihu tana neman agaji,da kyar Yan aiki suka jata toilet suka hada Mata ruwan sanyi a baho ta zauna a ciki,Haka suka dinga canja ruwa Hajiya na Zama,har yajin zafin ya ragu ta samu sauki ta kwanta ta wangale ta kunna fanka da ac tayi shanya tana tsinewa Khairat kwando Kwando sannan tace wlh sai taci uban Hajiya Baturiya ta biyata kudin data kashe Akan Khairat.

    Khairat kuwa da gudu ta bar gidan ta mike titi tana gudu saida tayi nisa ta tsaya ta huta tare da da gyara kanta tana tafiya a hankali tana jiran ko zata samu taxi Amma ba Taxi dare yayi titi ba kowa wurin 11pm har 12am na dare Bata samu taxi ba sai mazan banza masu tsayawa a titi daukan Mata.
   Khairat tasan idan ta koma Gidan Baturiya ta Shiga uku sai kawai ta Nemi wani asibiti katafaren gaske ta Shiga ciki da niyyar Wai tazo Yar zaman jinya ce,tana ta zagaye zagayenta a asibitin kawai tana tafiya da baya da baya a tsorace tayi Karo da mutum Jakarta ta Fadi kayan suka watse a kasa, wani turarene me azabar Dadi ya daki hancinta rabon taji mutum me kamshi Haka tun suna tare da Hunaif.

    Wayarta ya take da arnen takalminsa me kyau da tsaya ya wuce abinsa,Khairat ta mike a masifance tace Malam mene Haka wannan ai wulakanci ne,yaransa da suke take Masa baya Suka yi shuru,a hankali ya juyo sukayi Ido Hudu da Hunaif da Khairat.
   A hankali yace malama kina rike kayanki da kyau kina Bata min lokaci,Jin Muryar me Maganar ce yasa ta dago da sauri a firgice ta kalleshi,Mutuwar tsaye tayi ganin Hunaif ya Kara wani Kyau da Haske,shekeke ya kalleta  ya bi takan wayar ta ya wuce Yana Jan tsaki.
 
    Khairat da sauri ta mike tsaye tare da kwala Masa Kira Hunaif ganin ya juyo da mamaki Yana kallonta Ina ta sanshi ita Kuma shi da baya hurda da Mata,ganin Yana Mata kallon banza yasa Khairat ta gano ko dama can yaudararta yayi Bata san yayi accident ya samu matsala ba,sai tace Kai Malam ya zaka watsar min da Kaya Amma ko Sannu ko tunaninka irin Yan matanka ne daka Saba yaudara? Mayaudari kawai,Da mamaki Hunaif yake kallonta yanda take Masa tsiwa,yace a Ina kika sanni ko kin sanni ne? Baki Khairat ta tabe tace Dole kace Haka Mana tunda Kai babban mayaudari ne,sannan ka fasa min waya da kayan kwalliyata me tsada,Abin ya daurewa Hunaif Kai da take ce Masa Mayaudari ko budurwarsa ce gashi tana kiransa da Mayaudari,dama Ummi tace ya taba soyayya to ko itace,a ransa yace karya ne yaja tsaki ba wani Bata lokaci yayi gaban abinsa,Khairat Baki bude take kallonsa har ya bacewa ganinta.

    Hawaye ne suka wanke Mata fuska sabo da tana Masifar son Hunaif Amma ya ganta ya nuna Bai ma santa ba,wani haushinsa taji ta kwashe kayanta tana mamaki Wai Bai nuna ko alamar ya santa ba,wurin Zama ta samu a Hospital din ta zauna ka rantse jinyar wani takeyi,a zaune a wurin bacci ya kwasheta Bata farka ba sai da gari ya washe yayi tangararan,Ana ta zirga zirga Ana wuceta,pampo ta nema a can Bayan Compound tayi Alwala tare da gabatar da Sallah sannan ta fita ta Shiga taxi ta wuce gidan Hajiya Baturiya.
 
 Hunaif tunda ya koma gida yake ta faman tunanin Khairat da abinda ya faru tsakaninsu,tunda cutar Nan ta sameshi Abu Bai taba faruwa ya tuna ba sai Akan Khairat,Koda dare yayi ya kwanta bacci Mafarkin lokacin kuruciyarsa shi da Mus'af yayi suna yara,Sannan Yana farkawa daga bacci sai gashi ya tuna abinda ya faru tsakaninsu da Khairat jiya,ya tuna yafi sau a irga abin ya bashi mamaki da yake tuna Abinda ya faru dashi jiya da Khairat,sannan rabon da yayi mafarki ma ya manta sai gashi a Dalilin Khairat yayi Mafarki jiya,farin ciki ya kamashi,ko wanka baiyi ba ya fito da sauri Yana kwalawa Ummi Kira,tana kitchen ya fada ciki yace Ummi na tuna abinda ya faru jiya Ni da wata,wlh nayi mafarki jiya ma lokacin muna Yara da Mus'af,sannan Ina farkawa a bacci jiya naga wata Yarinya munyi fada Kinga yau na tuna komai,Ummi farin ciki ya kamata tace da gaske yace yafi Sau goma ma na tunata,Kinga yanzu Ina ganinta a kwakwalwata Memory na ya ajiyeta.

   Ummi tana dariya tace wannan wacce yarinya ce Haka wacce ta samin yarona farin ciki Nima ta sani ya kamata a nemota ko a Ina take,Hunaif yace  Zan Kara nemota muyi fada na gani ko Zan sake tunawa, Good cewar Ummi,Waya Hunaif ya dauka ya Kira Farouq ya bashi labari,Zai Kira Mus'af Ummi tace ka Bari tukun a samo Kan lamarin kawai kayi Shuru shi Farouq kadai zaka sanarwa tunda shi ya damu da lafiyarka, jeka yi wanka muyi Breakfast sai mu tafi wurin Doctor a sanar Masa an samu chanji.
   Koda Hunaif ya fara wanka in Banda tunanin Khairat da maganganunta jiya ba abinda yakeyi Yana Jin wani Nishadi, Haka suna Break ma,Hospital sukaje Doctor ya Gama Jin Bayaninsu kaf sai yace Hunaif You are In love with her tun tuni,sonta ya Dade da kamaka Wanda Brain naka bazai iya mantawa da ita ba.

   Ummi tace to Dr yanzu mene shawara,? Lallai a Nemo yarinyar ita zata taimaka ya iya dawowa Normal,Hunaif ya tabe Baki yace wannan Yar Baby din Zan zubar da mutuncina Ni wlh bazan nemota ba,Babu yanda Ummi batayi da Hunaif ba Amma yace Sam baza a Nemo yarinyar ba zai warke a Haka.

    Kwana biyu tsakani ya kasa mantawa da yarinyar kullum tunanin Khairat yakeyi maganganunsu tana kiransa da Mayaudari,Cikin securities dinsa ya nemi Wanda suka yi escorting Nasa zuwa Hospital yace Lallai a Nemo Masa yarinyar da suka hadu da ita a Hospital ya bangajeta.
   Yaronsa yace an Gama sir,Nan suka bazama neman Khairat.



       
    Godiya da Jinjina gareki UMMI GARKUWA.

[10/18, 2:51 PM] Sis Asma: 🦚🦚ME MAGANI🦚🦚

        Hadiza Hussain,Khady Chafe,Hassana Usman,Aisha Ad,Nomah Zinatu,Jameelah Abdullahi,Zinatu Aliyu,Rukayyatu,Ummu Hanan,Mmn Tasleem,Mmn Labyb.

         Yaran Hunaif ke aikin neman Khairat lungu da sako, Khairat kullum sai anyi fada Da ita a gidan Hajiya Baturiya kowa rashin mutunci take musu ba abinda ya dameta,Suna Zaune a Palo Khairat ta fito cikin zaratan Yan Matan Nan dankwali ta tsigoshi gaba sannan ta kallesu daya Bayan daya ta tabe baki tare da Jan tsaki, jira kawai take wata tayi magana suyi fada, sabo da sun San Masifar Khairat Babu wacce tayi ko tari,Hajiya Baturiya ce ta fito da sauri dauke da akwatunan Khairat ta watso su waje tana huci ta nuna Khairat da yatsa ..

    Tashi ki fitar min a gidana tunda Kika zo ban a Karuwa dake sai asarar Customers da kike min,kina hadani Fada da manyan masu kudi Dan ubanki Dan Uwarki bar min gida, dariya Khairat tayi tace an fada Miki Ni Karuwa ce? Ina tsoron Allah Baki Isa kisa na sabawa Allah ba,Kuma Dan na bar gidan Nan sai me,gidanki din banza an fada Miki Allah bazai tallafa min ba, Ni har Ina neman yabawar Dan Adam ne.
   Hajiya Baturiya kallon Khairat kawai takeyi har ta Gama sannan ta kwashi akwatinanta da Babba da karama ta kalli Baturiya tace gidan da aka Gina da Haram,ake ci da Sha da Haram me zanyi da Zama a cikinsa, taja tsaki tayi ficewarta ta bar gidan Hajiya Baturiya Baki bude suke jinjina Rashin kunya irin ta Khairat.

    Khairat tunani takeyi Ina zata je,idan ta koma Gidan Kawu wata Masifar ce,tana zaune jikin Wata bishiya sai wayarta tayi Kara kirrrr..tana dubawa taga Zainab,dagawa tayi tace Zainab ya akayi? Umma ce da Kawu suka ce na tambayeki yaushe zasu tashi zuwa kasa me tsarki? Khairat a ranta tayi dariya a fili tace sai an fara iban Alhazai Nan da sati Uku kice su shirya.
   Zainab ta fadawa Talatu me Khairat tace ai kuwa suka fadawa Yan uwa da abokan arziki zasu tafi Makkah kwana nan,Ana musu Allah Sanya Alheri,Talatu harda shiri taje gidansu ta sanar bana dasu za a tafi aikin Hajji.

     Bayan tafiyar Khairat Talatu ta Fara abincin siyarwa Amma tunda taji zata je Makkah tace ai Sunyi kudi tafi karfin saida Abinci ta kusa Zama Hajiya.
    Khairat ta yini a jikin bishiya karshe ta mike da kayanta ta Shiga Taxi tace a kaita suleja inda masu karamin karfi ke Zama,Bayan taje Suleja ta dinga zaga Tasha wurin Yan tuwo tuwo tana neman wacce zata na tayasu aiki a Bata wurin kwana,Babu wacce ta saurareta sai wata Bahaushiya Ana kiranta da Ladi,Ladi tace Yan Mata Zan Baki wurin kwana ganin ke Bahaushiya ce Amma Zaki dinga tayani aikin abincina a Tasha shine taimakon da Zan iya,Murna Khairat tayi tana faman godewa Ladi,Ladi tace shigar da akwatinki shagon cin Abinci zuwa dare idan na tashi sai mu tafi Gidana gaba daya.
   Khairat ta dinga Godiya sannan ta zage ta Shiga Taya Ladi aiki sosai,Ladi taji Dadin Ganin Khairat Bata da kuya ga Tsafta.

     Wurin Magrib Ladi ta Gama siyar da abincinta ta kulle shagonta suka tafi gidanta tare da Khairat,ba nisa da tashar Khairat taga Dan gidan karami Amma Yana da Dan kyansa ko Ina tiles,Daki biyu da Palo ne sai toilet da kitchen,Khairat tace Aunty Ladi gidanki ne ko na haya? Ladi tayi Murmushi tace Gidana ne na Kaina Kuma da kudin Sana'a ta na siya,Khairat ta jinjina Kai,Ladi tace yanzu tunda muna tare Ina saida katin waya su Mtn,Glo etc sai ki dinga siyar min da shi a gefen titi Ni Kuma sai naci gaba da girkin abincina ko ya kika gani,Khairat tace ba damuwa ki Saro katin da yawa kawai Ni Zan siyar.
   Daki guda me dauke da Katifa karama Ladi ta bawa Khairat tace ga dakinki,Khairat tayi murna ga Ladi akwai Tsafta har da ta masifa ma.

   Khairat Bayan tayi wanka suka danyi Hira Da Ladi sannan Suka tafi makwancinsu,Khairat a fili tace wato Ni a talla Zan Kare a rayuwata ba ci gaba,ba yanda ta iya Haka zatayi Dole tunda Allah ya taimaketa ta samu wurin kwana.

   Washe gari da wuri Ladi ta tashi Khairat sukayi Sallar Asuba,Shayi ta hada musu suka Sha sannan suka kwashi tarkacen kayan aikin Ladi sai Tasha,Ladi ta tambayi tarihin Khairat ta Dan Bata a takaice itama Ladi tace Ni Yar Asalin Kebbi State ce Allah Bai taba bani Haihuwa ba sai tarin Yan uwa,Aure ya kawoni Suleja,Allah yayiwa Mijina Rasuwa,wannan gidan da nake ciki na Mijina nane Allah yasa Ina da zafin nema,Bayan anyi rabon gado yaransa suka ce zasu siyar,Ina da kudi na sai na siya naci gaba da Sanaa ta,da ita nake ci nake Sha.

    Khairat ta jinjina Kai tace Anty Zan tayaki sanaarki indai Zaki bani wurin kwana,Ladi ta kalleta tace ba damuwa Allah shige Mana gaba abinda nake so dake ki rike mutuncinki Kinga dai a Tasha zamuna siye da siyarwa Dole sai kinyi taka Tsantsan da Bata gari,Khairat tace inshallah ba matsala.
    Katin waya iri iri Ladi ta bawa Khairat ta siyar Mata,Khairat tana gefen titi tana bin motoci tana mikawa idan ta gaji ta koma inuwa ta zauna ta huta,a Haka ta dinga ciniki sosai, Ladi sai farin ciki takeyi,2pm Bayan Sunyi sallah a tashar sai Ladi tace Khairat ebi abinda kike so kici ki koshi ga ruwa pure water.
   Washe gari ma Haka Khairat take zabga cinikinta.
   Har ta kwashe kwana Uku lokacin Kuma yaran Hunaif sun bazama suna ta neman Khairat ko Ina,Bayan sun Gama da cikin garin sai suka koma wajen gari, katsam suka Shiga Suleja Khairat na ta siyar da katinta,A cikin yaran guda Daya ya gane Khairat yace wannan ce,Khairat Bata sani ba suka dauketa hotuna da video tana ta faman bin motoci tana tallan katin waya sai tsalle tsalle takeyi sabo da kuruciya ko gajiya batayi.
   Yaron Hunaif ne yayi parking da motar ya siye Katin wayar Khairat gaba daya ragowar na dubu Bakwai ne a hannunta,Khairat sai Murna takeyi an siye Mata Kati.   

    Da murna yaran Hunaif suka sameshi a katafaren Office dinsa dake birnin tarayya,Yaron ya dakko katuwar wayarsa yace Sir ga yarinyar nasan wannan itace,Video na Khairat tana tsalle tsalle ya nunawa Hunaif shi kanshi Bai San sanda yayi Murmushi ba ganin yanda take tsalle tsalle Akan siyar da kati,Pics dinta yayi zoomin tabbas itace Nan take ya jika yaran nasa da kukade yace ya za ayi tazo inda nake Ina so muyi fada da ita na gani ko Zan iya tunawa again I think Memory na zai iya ajiyeta .

    Babban yaronsa Usman yace ai Zuwa zamuyi muce muna bukatar Kati na dubu dari oganmu Yana nema Amma idan ta Saro tazo da kanta ta kawo maka sai mu Bata Address da Number wayarka Kuna magana.
   Murmushi yayi cikin Isa da Izza Yana wani juyawa a kujera sanye cikin hadaddun kana Nan Kaya Yana rike da biro a hannunsa yace Good Idea aje ayi hakan Ina son ganinta gobe.

    An Gama sir cewar Usman suka fita suna Jin Dadi yau sunsha kudade duk da cewar Yana musu kyauta ko yaushe Bayan albashinsu Amma na yau yafi na kullum,Nan take suka koma Suleja lokacin Khairat tana cin abinci a runfar Ladi,Usman ya Karasa har gabanta inda suke zaune tare da Ladi,Khairat taga wanda ya Mata ciniki yau ta washe Baki tace Ina yini? Yace lfy tare da gaisar da Ladi sannan yace Ogana ne yake bukatar Kati na dubu dari idan har zaku siyar Masa,da sauri Khairat tace me? Yace Kati na dubu dari Kinga idan kika Saro sai ki siyar Masa ki samu riba,dazu na siyi katinki naji dadi shi yasa na kawo Miki hanyar Karuwa,Khairat tace dubu dari fa kace,Ladi tace to yaro siyarwa shima zaiyi? Usman yace a waya zai sa ko kudin Sunyi kadan a Kara dubu dari biyu? Khairat tace Sunyi yawa sai Gobe idan na siyo Taya zaka Karba to? Number ya Bata yace gashi number Ogana ce ki nemi number sai ya Baki Address ki Kai Masa,Khairat taji kudi Bata ji tsoron komai ba ta karbi Number sannan ta Basu Tata number din suka tafi.
   Ladi murna takeyi tace Bari anjima naje banki na Ciro kudin gobe da wuri zamuje mu Saro katin sai a Kai masa.

   Washe gari kuwa 11am Khairat ta Kira Number Hunaif,Wanda tuni yaransa sun bashi number Khairat yayi Saving,Yana Office ya ga kiranta sai da yayi Murmushi sannan ya daga ba tare da yace komai ba,tace Hlo Good day Sir, me siyar da kati ce, katin ko a maka Transfer kawai a waya? Murya ya canja yace no Haka nake sonsa a takarda Yan 1k a kawo min inda nake,Khairat tace to sai ka tura min Address naka, Alright ya Furta tare da datse Kiran, Khairat tace wannan wanne irin mutum ne da baya Jin kudi? Ta bawa kanta amsa da Maybe wani shugabane a kasar nan.

   Sanye take cikin doguwar Riga red and Golden da Dan Hijab dinta me hannu madaidaici ta yiwa Ladi Sallama ta Shiga taxi tana bin Address din Office dinsa daya bata har ta je katafaren Building dinsa dake Asokoro,ta kirashi a waya gani a Office din naka,yace ki shigo ga yarona zai Miki Iso,Ok tace ta kashe wayar ta Shiga sai kuwa ga Usman ya fito da fara'a yace Hajiya me Kati biyoni a baya,Khairat tayi Murmushi ta bishi suka Shiga lifter sai gasu a bakin Office din Hunaif.

    Knocking Usman yayi daga ciki suka ji yace Come in,Usman yana bude Office din wani kamshi da sanyi ya daki Khairat ta lumshe Ido tana kallon katafaren Office din kayan Alatu da gani kasan na Yan gayu ne.
    Sanye Hunaif yake cikin farar shadda Kal Tasha dinki me azabar kyau na Yan zamani,sheki da kyalli kawai yakeyi ya Kara wani Masifar kyau.
   Juyowa yayi lokacin tuni Usman ya fita,Khairat kawai sai taga Hunaif ne Ashe,Haushinsa take ji baya tunawa da ita ya yaudareta,yanzu Kuma me yake Shirin Yi Mata,Fuska ta hade ta Mika Masa katin da yawa a wata Yar jaka,kallonta yayi Yana mamaki to wannan a Ina ta sanshi ne? ga katin ka karba Zan tafi Ni ta Furta da Shagwaba,Murmushi yayi tare da kallon katin yace Kije dashi kawai,Khairat ta kalleshi ban gane ba? Dama rannan Ina Jin haushinka ka fasa min Powder me tsada yanzu kasa na kawo maka Kati baka biya kudin ba,kudin Powder nawa ne? ya Furta tare da Mikewa tsaye ya matso kusa da ita, tana turo Baki tace dubu biyu ce ehe Nan take ya zaro Bundle na 1k da dubu Ashirin a Kai yace gashi har kudin Powder da kudin mota 5k,Khairat mamaki ya kamata baya Jin kashe kudi dama tasan shi tuntuni,Katin ta Mika Masa yace Kije ki bayar kyauta ko ki siyar ko ki zubar duk abinda kike so kiyi dasu,Khairat ranta ya baci ya sata wahala a banza a wofi, kamar zatayi kuka tace amma ka sani wahala nazo har cikin gari? A fusace ta fita ta bar Office din tana goge kwallarta wani son Hunaif ya Kara taso Mata,ace Wai baya iya ko nuna alamar yasanta ma.

  Hunaif Kam yace to fushin me takeyi? Baki ya tabe yaci gaba da aikinsa, Khairat Kuma tana komawa Gida ta sanarwa Ladi me ya faru ta cire dubu Ashirin dinta kudin mota Dana Powder ta bawa Ladi dubu darinta sannan suka siyar da katinsu riba biyu Ladi taji dadin wannan harka.

    Tunda Khairat ta bar Office din Hunaif ya kasa komai sai tunaninta yanda ta Bata Rai tana Masa masifa da Shagwaba,har Murmushi yakeyi shi kadai,Haka daya koma gida ma,Ummi taga canji yau Yana farin ciki taji dadin hakan domin ta Dade Bata ga ko Murmushin Danta ba,ta tambayeshi me ya faru yaki sanar Mata yace ba komai kawai.
   Washe gari daya tashi daga bacci kawai sai ya sake tuna Khairat kaf abinda ya faru dashi jiya tare da Khairat ya tuna Amma baya tuna na komai sai na Khairat,Haka yaje wurin Doctor ya sanar Masa,Likitan ya sake gwaje gwaje yace yarin Yar Nan Zata taimaka kwarai wajen dawowar memory naka.

    Tunda Zainab taji Khairat tace su Talatu sun kusa tashi zuwa kasa me tsarki kullum ta damu Khairat da waya yaushe zasu tashi, Khairat ita kanta taji Zainab ta dameta kawai sai yau tana ganin Kiran Zainab tace Su Talatu su shirya su tafi Airport yau jirginsu zai tashi.
    Talatu ta gigice ta Shiga makwafta tace to jama'a a yafi juna mu Allah ya kawo tashinmu,abinda Kuka yi min na yafe muku Kuma ku yafe min,Su Rahinatu harda kuka za a rabu da iyaye,Talatu an Nemo Taxi sun shirya da jakarsu Kawu ya fashe da kuka ya rike Hannun Rahinatu yace to Rahinatu ko mu dawo a raye ko ba mu dawo ba ku rike zumunci,ku kaunaci junanku,Talatu tana goge Hawaye yace ke Zainab ki rungumi kannanku  kafin mu dawo,Bayan Sunyi Sallama da juna suka wuce airport, Bayan sunje Airport sai Talatu ta Kira Khairat ta sanar Mata,Khairat tana ta dariya tace yanzu za a zo a daukeku za a kaiku wurin Screening,Aiko sai ga wani mutum me Gulf yazo duk cikin aikin Khairat ne,yace Kune Talatu da Kawu?,da Sauri Talatu tace ae mune,yace ku Shiga Mota mu tafi inji Khairat,Sai da Talatu ta shigar da Kawu sannan itama ta Shiga mota suka tafi,kawai Bawan Allah ya mike hanyar Niger,gudu yake tsalawa tun su Talatu na tunanin an kusa zuwa suka ji Shuru.
   Kawu yace Kai yaro ko Makkah zamu a mota ai sai Haka wannan irin nisa Haka,Driver yayi banza dasu gudu yake shekawa kawai har suka Isa Katsina suka wuce katsina state suka dauki Hanyar Niger.

   Sai da sukayi tafiyar 5hrs lokacin sun Shiga kauyukan Niger can yankin Sahara,ba gida gaba ba gida baya,sai tarin Sahara da Rana kwal ba ko ruwa kusa Babu bishiyu ko wani koren gayye Babu,Talatu ta fashe da kuka,Kawu yace lfy a Ina muke? Talatu tana kuka tace Bangon duniya ya kawo mu,Malam ka taimakemu,cikin Dajin ya gangara sannan ya fito ya kwace wayar Talatu da Kawu ya jefar musu da jakarsu yace ku fice min a mota, Bayan sun fita yaja motar Sa yayi tafiyarsa ya bar Talatu da Kawu Makaho a wajen,Talatu tace ya zamuyi? Kawu yace kwadayi mabudin wahala Yi min jagora mu tafi ko zamu ga wani kauye sai muje a samu a hanya mu koma Nigeria, Talatu ta Fara tsinewa Khairat,Kawu yace wannan yarinya Allah wadaran Halinta,wlh idan muka koma gida sai nasa Soja ya harbe ta.
   Talatu taja Hannun Kawu suka Kara nausawa cikin Dajin Sahara suna tafiya,yunwa da kishirwa kamar zasu mutu.Talatu ta rushe da kuka Kawu Kam ya rasa abin cewa ta kansa yakeyi kawai.
    Khairat kuwa tace Nayi maganinku Talatu kafin ku dawo sai kunyi nadamar halayenku.

   Hunaif ya gaji da tunanin Khairat, kawai ya Umarci Usman Daya binciko Masa gidan da Khairat take sannan wanne time suke komawa Gida Bayan sun Gama sanaarsu.
   Usman ya sanar Masa da Address din gidan sannan yace sai 5pm suke komawa Gida, ba tare da Hunaif ya nemi Driver ba da kansa yake Driving ya tafi gidan su Khairat 7pm na dare,so yake yasan Taya ta sanshi,sannan me yasa indai sun hadu sai ya tunata da safe,baya tuna kowa sai ita,me yasa Memory dinsa yake tuna Khairat kadai.

    Lokacin Khairat ta fito siyen Maltina a wani kanti ta tafi gida wani Dan wiwi marar mutunci ya tare Khairat a hanya yace ke marar kunya ke wato kinfi karfin kowa ko Akan ance Ana sonki har wani Shan kamshi kike Mana ke Wai Dan kina da kyau ko? Harda wani siyo Maltina guda biyu Zaki Sha ke ba maaikaciyar Gomnati ba ba komai ba,ke ba Yar kowan kowa ba harda wani Zaki Sha Maltina,karuwar banza ai duk mun San irinku Sumi Sumi a hijab, shekeke Khairat ta kalleshi ita dariya ma ya Bata Wai Maltinar ma da zata Sha bakin ciki yake mata,tace to bana sonka ko Dole ne,duk mazan duniya na rasa wa zan so sai irinka Dan wiwi,Kuma Ni ba Karuwa bace Kaine babban Karuwi tunda Ni Karuwa ce Kai kuma fa Karuwi ne?

    Hannu ya daga da niyyar zabgawa Khairat Mari saiko wani zukeken hannu me laushi ya rike Hannun Dan Wiwi Wanda ake kiransa da Me Dawa,Khairat ganin Hunaif ne sai ta Fara kuri ai da ka kyaleshi ya taba fuskata ya tabowa kansa bala'i da Jarabar duniya,da ka barshi ya jawa kansa barin Suleja ba tare da ya shirya ba,Da yatsa ta nuna Me Dawa tace ka kiyayeni nafi karfin Wanda ya fika ma,ba a ja dani,Baki Hunaif ya bige Mata tayi sauri ta rufe bakin ta tsuguna a kasa tana Yar Kara taji zafi, Kudi ya zaro Wanda Bai San ko nawa Bane ya mikawa Me Dawa,Me Dawa ya samu kudin wiwi ya dinga murna Yana sai Oga Allah bar Mana Oga,wannan kanwarka ce? Hunaif yace ae,shike Nan na kyaleta Amma ayi Mata fada Bata da kunya Zan iya take Mata wuya watarana,Khairat day sauri ta dago da kanta tace ka take Mana.....kafin ta rufe Baki Hunaif ya rankwasheta,Kara ta saki  da salon Muryar Shagwaba tace Wai me na maka ne? Ka daina takura min,me ya kawoka gidanmu ka daina Bina Hawaye ne ya zubo Mata na tunanin irin son da takewa Hunaif.

   Fuskarta ya leka ta matsa baya tana boyewa Dan kar ya gani,kuka kikeyi? Tace a'a Ni ba kuka nakeyi ba,Akan me zanyi kuka tana magana tana goge Hawaye,Murmushi yayi kawai yace a Ina kika sanni ya akayi kika sanni?Mene a tsakaninmu da?
   Takaici ya Kama Khairat Yana Raina Mata hankali duk yanda ya santa ya nuna wani Bai taba ganinta ba,shi Kuma Hunaif ya kasa fada Mata Accident din da yayi,ita Kuma Bata sani ba,ganin Yana Raina Mata hankali kawai sai ta dauki ledarta tayi gaba,Yana binta a baya suna tafiya har cikin gidansu.

    Ladi taga Mutum kawai a gidanta,a mutunce suka gaisa,tace Malam lfy? Hunaif yace wurin yarki nazo Taki tsayawa ta saurareni,Ladi ganin me kudi Haka tace Khairat jeki Mana ki saurareshi,Maltina ta ajiye ta fito a fusace ta bude Masa Kofa Malam fitar Mana a gida,ganin Yanda yarinya karama take Raina Masa hankali sai ya fita kawai,Khairat ta rufe kofa sannan ta zauna tana hawayen son Hunaif,sai da ta gaji sannan ta Shiga ciki ta kwanta bacci ya kwashe ta.

  Hunaif kuwa Bai San ya akayi ba idan yaga Khairat  sai yayi ta faman tunaninta sannan Yana Jin nishadi da farin ciki a zuciyarsa,Haka washe gari ma gidan su Khairat da yaje Yana tashi a bacci ya tuna,memory nasa ya ajiye Masa.
   Khairat Kam harkan gaban ta takeyi,yau ma sai ga wayarta ya Kira cewar ta kawo Masa Kati na dubu Dari zai siya,ya tura Mata Address na guest House nasa,Yana son ganin fadanta da masifarta tare da Saurin fushinta,Khairat Kuma Ladi ta fadawa Anty kinji Wai a sake Kai Masa Kati Wanda ya siyi Kati rannan,Ladi ta washe Baki tace Wanda ya biyoki gida jiya Zaki ce,mu Ina ruwanmu tunda riba muke ci ai shi yaga duhu maza jeki Saro ki Kai Masa,idan Bai karba ba ya biya kudi mu siyar da abinmu riba biyu kenan.

    Sanin Hunaif ne mutumin kirki ne sai Khairat ta siyo Kati ba ko kwalliya ta tafi inda yace taje Guest House nasa.
   Gidane na Alfarma wani me gadi ne ya Mata Iso har ciki,tana kallon yanda gidan ya tsaru,a Palo yake daga shi sai 3qtr da Riga t-shirt me azabar kyau,remote a hannunsa ga Magazine Yana karantawa,ya harde kafa daya Kan daya,ga wata katuwar tv plasma a jikin bango Yana kallon wani American film.

      Kamshi da sanyi ne kawai ke tashi ta ko Ina,Juice dake glass cup ya dauka tare da kurba Yana kallon Khairat dai dai,tana tsaye a kansa daga shi sai ita,katin ta Mika Masa a wata Yar wallet tace gashi,yace Ok Yana kallonta kasa kasa Yana so ya gano Ina ta sanshi,sai yace bazan biya ba sai kin gyara min Palon nan, Dan karamin bakinta ta turo tace ba abinda ya kawoni ba kenan ka bani kudina Zan tafi,Zaki kwana anan Ashe matukar Baki min abinda na saki ba,Harara Khairat ta watsa Masa,yayi Murmushi kadan,ta juya a Shagwabe tana tafiya irin ta sangartattun Nan, ya nuna Mata inda kayan aikin suke tsintsiya,Mopper etc,Khairat aiki yasa ta cire Hijab T-shirt ce a jikinta Fara ta kamata daf Bata da wani kauri rigar, sai skert din atamfa sai dankwali a kanta Baki karami ta daura,Hijab Kuma Yana saman kujera Ana ta aiki,duk ta gaji,Bra dinta ta goce ta koma cikinta,shi Kuma kirjin gashi Nan Ana kallon komai har nipple dinta,Abu dagwas dagwas, Hunaif ya mike zai Shiga kitchen tayi sauri ta tareshi tace na Gama Ni ka bani kudina na tafi,juyowa yayi ya kalleta karaf idonsa ya Kai Kan kirjinta,gabansa ya Fadi,yarinya da abubuwa haka, ganin bra dinta ta koma cikinta abin ya bashi dariya,ya daure da kyar,baya so Kuma yace ta gyara taji kunya ko ta fassarashi, Khairat ta Kara matsowa tana gyara tsaiwarta tace Dan Allah Zan tafi, kirjinta ya kurawa Ido kadan ya dauke Kai yace ga kwaro Nan a cikinki,da sauri ta kalli cikinta da kirjinta.

Kara ta kwalla tare da durkushewa a kasa ta kankame jikinta,kunya ta kamata,ganin yanda tayi ya bashi dariya ya dinga dariya da kyar ya danne wata,ya juya bayansa yace gyara to,da sauri ta mike ta gyara kanta ta jawo Hijab dinta tasa sannan ya juyo tare da Bata kudinta da katinta tayi tafiyarta da saur ga kunya ya kalle Mata kirji.

    Har tayi Nisa taji Muryarsa yace Dan tsaya,Ashe Yana biyota a baya,sai da ta tsaya ba tare data juyo ba,yace Pls a Ina kika sanni? Wani bakin ciki ya Kara rufe Khairat Wai Dan rainin wayo ita zai ce Bai gane ba,mutumin da yace zai aure ta,Yama raina Mata hankali, Hunaif har yayi tunanin fada Mata rashin lafiyar dake damunsa sai Kuma ya fasa yaji bazai iya fada Mata ba sirrinsa ne,Yana tsaye yaga tayi tafiyarta a fusace Bata ko saurareshi ba.





Ina matukar Godiya gareku masu Sharhi da masu kirana a waya,da masu min magana,Novel din Nan Yana da masoya.

[10/18, 2:51 PM] Sis Asma: 🦚🦚ME MAGANI🦚🦚
