     FATIMA IG,UMMU HANEEFER,MAMAN SAUBAN,SUMMIS BEB,UMMU MUS'AB,HAFSAH,HAFCY,SILENT QUEEN,MOM SALEEM,SIS NERNAH,MAMAN RUKAYYA,MRS ABUBAKAR.
    Ga page naku Yan albarka.







        Hakura yayi kawai ya Shiga dalleliyar motarsa ya bar unguwar tasu,Yana komawa Gida Ummi ta tareshi da Ina kaje Hunaif hankalina ya tashi,nasan baka Driving Amma sai yau Kuma kasan baka da lfy Ina escort naka duk baka tafi da ko mutum daya ba?
   Murmushi ya saki yace Ummi kamar wani yaro wani Meeting naje shi yasa,Baki Ummi ta tabe tare da cewa to sai ka sakko kaci abincinka kasan bazan wahalar banza ba ka sani na maka Abinci ka fita,Zanci ai Ummi Bari nayi wanka ya Furta Yana haurawa sama.

    Tunda Khairat ta bar gidan Hajiya Baturiya take tunanin me zata yiwa Hajiya Baturiya ta gyara Mata Zama sannan ta Rama cin mutuncin da tayi Mata, tunowa tayi da Me Dawa Dan Wiwi ta Gama sake sakenta.
    Washe gari Khairat ta Nemi Me Dawa,Tunanin Me Dawa kanwar Hunaif ce Wanda ya jikashi da kudade,yace ya akayi ne marar kunya,Khairat tace haba ai mun shirya dama Kaine kake tsokanata,Me Dawa yace na yafe Miki sabo da Yayanki,me kike nema? Khairat ta kalleshi sannan ta fadawa me Dawa aikin da zasu yi Mata shi da yaransa guda Biyar,Me Dawa yace kawo kudi,Khairat ta Mika Masa Dubu Ashirin din da Hunaif ya Bata da ta Kai Masa Kati a farko.

    Me Dawa yace Ki shirya muje dake,Khairat tace an Gama,dare nayi Khairat Tasha katon Hijab da Nikaf suka Shiga Mota tare dasu Me Dawa sai gidan Hajiya Baturiya.

    Katanga Me Dawa ya Kama tare da haurawa gidan yaje ya fara daure me gadi ya like Masa Baki sannan ya bude musu gidan suka Shiga har Khairat, tiryan tiryan Khairat tasan ko Ina ta Kaisu part part suka Fara daure Yan Matan gidan kaf suka kullesu a daki daya suka musu daya Kan daya kamar Kifi sadine,Khairat tace ko wacce ayi Mata bulala Talatin Talatin,ai ko su Me Dawa suka zanesu tas sannan Khairat ta bude fuskarta,basuyi mamaki ba sun San zata aikata,tace na Baku 2wks ko wacce ta koma Gidan ubanta sannan ta ja su Me Dawa har part din Hajiya Baturiya.

lokacin wasu Matan sun tafi sanaarsu,Har dakin Hajiya Baturiya suka Shiga Baki daya tare da rufe dakin suka Sa key,Hajiya Baturiya Ana ta kwasar bacci Khairat ta zaro katuwar bulalar Danko ta dage iya karfinta ta Fara Tsulawa Hajiya Baturiya,a firgice ta farka tana ihu jama'a Yan fashi,Khairat ta Shiga Tafkar Hajiya Baturiya kamar Allah ya aikota,idan tayi magana Kuma Me Dawa su daka Mata tsawa,tari ma sun hanata,Me Dawa ya karbi bulalar a hannun Khairat ya Shiga Tafkawa Baturiya,yana Baki da Karfi karfi ai sai maza,tana tsala ihu da birgima,Mutanen gidan duk matane tsorone ya kamasu Babu Wanda ya ceci Hajiyar tasu Suma ta kansu sukeyi jikinsu duk shatin bulala,ga dakin su Khairat su rufe.

    Hakuri Hajiya ta fara basu,Khairat tace ki tabbatar gidan Nan kin tashi daga shi kafin Nan kafin sati daya,sannan ko wacce Karuwa ki maidata gidan Ubanta,idan muka samu Baki aikata hakan ba sai mun harbeki,Baturiya a gigice tace wlh zanyi Bazan fasa ba,sabo da zafin dukan sun farfasa Mata jiki ko gane Muryar Khairat Bata yi ba har suka Gama karshe Khairat ta bude fuskarta, Baturiya tace Khairat dama kece? Zaki aikata Allah ya Isa tsinanniya, Dariya Khairat tayi tare da Furta zagi da cin mutuncin da kika min na rama,Kika dinga zagin iyayena Kika wahalar Dani wurin zuwa Hotel da gidajen Mata Dan ki gurbata min rayuwa,Kuma Ina Nan dawowa idan Baki gyara halayenki ba zamu dawo,Khairat tace dasu Me Dawa muje kafin sati biyu mu dawo.
    suka bar gidan Baki daya,Khairat ta koma gida tana Jin dadin cin Uban Hajiya Baturiya da tayi dama haushinta take ji yanda ta tozarta ta tana Zagar mata iyayenta da suke Lahira.

    Zainab Ana gida tare da Soja da sauran kannensu duk tunaninsu su Talatu Ana Kasa me tsarki,abinda ya damesu shine rashin samun wayar Iyayen nasu,Sannan Shuru Basu nemesu ba har an kwashe kwana Uku,gaba daya sun Shiga damuwa.
   Talatu da Kawu kuwa Tafiya suke cikin Sahara wahala ta ishesu tun suna magana har bakinsu ya mutu Babu me magana,Talatu Hannun Kawu kawai take ja,Kawu yace Dan Allah ki Jani a hankali kawai Dan Allah yayoni bana gani sai ki dinga min abinda kika ga dama,Da fada itama ta hayayyako Masa Duk abinda nake maka baka gani wlh sai na sakeka na kyaleka kabi ka isheni,Tsaki Kawu yaja yace karki jawo na Sakeki Talatu,to Ka sakeni Mana sai me aikin banza tsoho kabi ka gallabeni,zagi Kawu ya kundumawa Talatu Nan Fada ya kaure a tsakaninsu,Talatu tace Hanci kamar an taka Kashi,ai gwara Ni dake matsiyaciya an cuceni daga ji an San Talatu ke ba kyaune dake ba cewar Kawu,Baki Babu hakoran gaba,Yarka ce tsinanniya ta cire min su,Khairat tsakaninmu dake Allahumma Tafatsinini cewar Talatu,Kawu ya amsa da Ameen.

   Suna Tafiya da kyar suka Karasa wata Yar rugar Fulani,Talatu ta rokesu da su sanmata ruwan Sha,Rijiya suka nuna Mata Talatu ta jawo ruwa Tasha ta cika cikinta jinin jikinta ya dawo sannan ta ebo ta bawa Kawu ya koshi sannan suka koma jikin wata bishiya suka zauna,Bayan sun Huta suka roki Fulanin da su San musu Abinci, Haka aka kawo musu tuwo suka ci hayam hayam kamar Mayu Bayan sun koshi suka sake Shan ruwa sannan aka nuna musu hanyar da Zata kaisu babban titin kwalta suka tafi,Tafiya me nisa wahala ta ishesu.

     Zainab kuwa Khairat ta Kira tace su Talatu Shuru ba labarinsu,Khairat tayi dariya a ranta,a fili tace zasu kiraku ai Ni jiya ma na Kira Amirul Hajj nasu ya hada Ni dasu,suna Nan lfy cikin Jin Dadi sunce na gaida ku har Sunyi Umrah saura aikin Hajji, Wayar Talatu ce ta fadi Amma zuwa jibi tace zata siyi sabuwa ta neme ku,Zainab da murna ta fadawa Yan Uwanta abinda Khairat tace sai Murna sukeyi, Khairat tace ai Ummanki Tasha zam zam ta koshi tace shinkafa kaza ma ta gaji da ita,su Zainab sai Ihu Ana dariya,Rahinatu tace nasan Umma wlh sai tayi kauyanci.

   Bayan Talatu sunje Bakin titi sai ga wata mota katuwa zata wuce,da sauri suka tsaidata suka ce Kano,Me mota yace ku Shiga,ga mutane Nan a ciki cike da mota, sai dai Kamar kiftawar Ido sai sukaji Driver ya tsaya wani yace a Nan Zan sauka,Driver ya juyo da kansa Yana kallon su Talatu yace daga nan baza mu sake tsayawa ba sai a birnin sin,Baki Talatu ta bude tace Birnin sin can kasar China karshen duniya? Driver yace ae, da sauri tace a Nan zamu sauka,da Sauri taja Kawu suka sauka,sai taga motar ta Bace bat ba ita ba alamarta,Ashe dai Talatu motar aljanu ta suka shiga hhh.
  Mutane suka gani kalarsu daban,Ana ta wani yare da Basu sani ba,Talatu ta samu wata mace Allah yasa tana Dan tsintar turanci Jin su Zainab suna yi,Talatu ta Fara turancinta na gwari gwari tace Me..From...Nigeria....where? Tana gwadawa da hannu tana turancinta na Yan koyo,Da kyar wani mutum ya gane me take nufi,yace You are In Kenya,Talatu ta fashe da kuka tace Sabiu motar Aljanu muka Shiga kamar kiftawar Ido har sun kawo mu Kenya, Kawu Hawaye ya kwararo Masa yace shike Nan sai gawar mu,Talatu Kenya fa kikace?

   Kawu yace Kai Khairat Allah ya kwashe Miki albarka,yanzu ya zamuyi? Talatu tace wasu zamu nema a sanarwa hukuma sai a dawo Damu gida,Haka suka Fara garari a cikin kasar Kenya gashi a Kenya dinma can Kauye aka sauke su ba cikin birni ba sai wahala suke Sha,Har ga Allah Khairat Bata San su Talatu Haka zata kasance dasu ba,tana da tausayi baza ta so hakan ba,sannan ba kowa yasan Ana Shiga motar Aljanu ba,Khairat tayi tunanin Dan Niger ai zasu iya dawowa.

    Hunaif da Ummi suna Dining sai tuna abubuwan da suka faru tsakaninsu da Khairat yakeyi,wayarsa ta Fara ruri Mus'af ne ke kiransa,dagawa yayi suna gaisawa irin ta abokai, Mus'af yace Hunaif akwai matsala a Company dake Rivers State jiya naje kudade da dama ban san ya akayi ba sun bace naje na Gama bincike na ban San ya akayi ba,Hunaif yace kudin masu yawa ne? Mus'af yace zasu Kai 90millions na yanke shawarar korar maaikatan baki daya matukar kudaden Basu fito ba,Hunaif yace Amma Taya za ace kudi Haka sun bace dare daya? Ummi tana jinsu tasan Mus'af ne ya shirya komai makaryaci ya sace kudade, me yasa su sauran masu Amana ba a asarar sisi Amma shi komai matsala a jikinsa ta Kare,daga yace wannan sai yace wancan, Bayan Hunaif ya Gama waya Ummi tace a rufe Company din kawai,Hunaif yace to Musaf din Kuma Ina zai samu kudin da zai inganta rayuwarsa Dana danginsa?  Ummi ta kalli Hunaif kawai tace shi ya sani sai ya nemi aiki a wajen wasu Amma ka sani bazan Rufe Company din ba Amma Zan Dora sabon Manager both har na Kano.
   Hunaif Ummi yake roka data bar Mus'af Amma Ummi tuni ta canja Shugaban Company daga na Kano har na Rivers, Mus'af Yana Office Sai takarda yagani an Mika Masa cewar an saukeshi daga matsayinsa an maida shi karkashin wani Wanda Ummi ta kawo,yasan ba Hunaif bane Aikin Ummi ne,bakin ciki da Tsanar Ummi ya Kara darsuwa a ransa,a fili ya Furta Dole nayi maganin wannan uwar Banzar, sake Sake Musaf yakeyi kawai yanda zai kassara rayuwar Ummi wacce ta shige Masa hanci da kudundune.

   Yau Ladi ta bawa Khairat dubu Ashirin kyauta Kan taje ta siyi kayan kwalliya,Yau Bata yi tallan Kati ba,Da yamma kwalliya tayi sosai tayi Masifar kyau cikin ready made Doguwar Riga light blue da baki, takalmi da jaka duk Black ta shirya ta Shiga Taxi sai cikin garin Abuja,ta shiga katon Mall na gani na fada na manyan masu hannu da shuni Amma Iyayin Khairat da Dan kudinta tace Nima na masu kudi Zan Shiga Kar a barni a baya, komai ta daga sai taga tsadar masifa, tunda ta Shiga ta kasa ko zabar Abu daya komai tsada,sai zaga wurin takeyi,karshe taje layin cosmetic ta dauki wani jambaki maroon taga an rubuta dubu Bakwai,ta hangame Baki tana kallon jambakin, Hunaif ne ya shigo Mall din shima zaiyi siyayyar da kayansu na maza.

    Khairat ya gani tana ta daukar Kaya idan ta kalla sai ta mayar ta kasa daukan Abu ko daya,ta dauki wata powder 15k Yar karama da ita,Khairat tace kai Ana tsada a kasar Nan,ba Imani ba tsoron Allah,Yar wannan Powder har 15k to baza a siya ba din aikin banza barayin mutane,Hunaif Yana gefe Yana kallonta Yana dariyar maganganunta ita kadai,karshe yaji tace an fasa siyayyar ma,tana fita ya fito,duk abinda yaga ta dauka sai da ya siya Mata har ma da Wanda Bata duba ba,Kaya sosai ya siya Mata iri iri masu tsada,yaransa suka zuba a motarsa ya karbi Key yace zai je shi kadai,sauran motocin suka koma gida dasu shi Kuma ya nufi garin Suleja wurin Khairat.

  Yayi nisa a Hanyarsa wayarsa tayi Kara Farouq ke kiransa Yana dagawa yace Ina Abuja gani a palonka Ummi tace ka fita kana Ina? Wani wuri zanje can Suleja wurin yarinyar da na baka labari Ina iya tuna ta ita kadai,Farouq yayi Murmushi yace ko dai so ne ya kamaka? Tsaki Hunaif yaja tare da cewa Allah ya kiyaye wannan Yar yarinyar karama ko 19yrd Bata Kai ba, Dariya Farouq yakeyi yace wait for me zanzo muje na ganta,Hunaif yace ok Bari nayi Parking sa Driver ya kawoka petrol station na Total, 10mnt sai ga Farouq Driver ya saukeshi ya shige motar Hunaif suka tafi,Hunaif ya Shiga bashi labarin Khairat ga kida na tashi a motar tasu,Yace Wato Farouq Ina fada maka yarinyar baiwa gareta,Farouq dariya kawai yake kwasa,Yana biyewa Hunaif yace Allah mutumina ai tunda naji kana iya ajiyeta a memory naka nasan Yar baiwa ce,Hunaif ya karo Sautin kidansa Yana wani nishadi har kada kai yakeyi Yana Murmushi yaci gaba da cewa Farouq yarinyar Nan gata Masifaffiya ce fa kullum idan muka hadu fada mukeyi,gata tana da kyau shegen iya Shagwaba ne da ita,Farouq ya sheke da dariya yace tab Lallai ta hadu to, Hunaif ya Dan kalli Farouq sannan yace Kai fa Dan iska ne Ina baka labari Kuma kana min Dariya,Farouq ya matse dariyarsa yace na daina to.

    Hunaif yace baka ga Dan bakinta ba idan tana masifa Ni kaina ta rainani,idonta idan tana Harara har wani spark sukeyi,sai naji zuciyata ta Fara wani Das..Das...Das..sai kuma tace Dit...Karshe sai dai naji zirrr...a cikin jini na,Farouq kasa danne Dariyarsa yayi ya dinga Kyakyatawa har Hunaif yayi Fushi yace ya daina bashi labarin ma.

    Lokacin da suka shigo Unguwar su Khairat ta talakawa Me Dawa Hunaif ya fara gani suna tsaye tare da Khairat,Me Dawa Kiran Khairat yayi Kan shifa da gaske son Khairat yakeyi,ganin ta kulasu sunje gidan Hajiya Baturiya shine yake tunanin zata so shi,Khairat ta Kalli me Dawa tace Dan Allah kayi hakuri wlh Ina da Wanda nake so,idan kudin Wiwi kake bukata Zan na San maka watarana.

    Me Dawa ya Hasala dake shima Saurin fushi ne dashi,Haka Khairat ma akwai Saurin fushi sannan basa son rainin hankali,Me Dawa ya daga Murya Dole ki Soni Wai ke Baki da Imani ne Ana miki magana aikin banza,Khairat tace kaci darajar yau Birthday na, ba komai na yafe maka, ta juya ta bar Me Dawa a tsaye,tsaki shima yaja ya juya ya tafi,Hunaif Yana kallonsu sai yaji ransa ya baci ganin Khairat tare da wani, Farouq kuwa Bai ma kula da komai ba,har Khairat tazo ta jikin motarsu ta wuce,Ashar Farouq ya saki tare da cewa Hunaif kaga wata hadaddiya kuwa? Gaba daya ta haske unguwar Nan,Talliya Sunan wata Kai ban taba ganin me kyan wannan ba.

     Hunaif yace itace yarinyar Dana ke fada maka to,Lallai ta hadu,Hunaif ya balle murfin mota ya fita yabi Khairat a baya, yace Ke..da sauri ta juyo Jin Muryar Hunaif,Farouq Yana kallonsu dake haske ya wadaci layin,Cike da masifa ta dawo baya zuwa wurin Hunaif tace nifa tsakani da Allah ka dameni kuma,Tunda baza ka iya tunawa Dani wace ba ka Sarara min,ka sakar min Mara nayi Fitsari, na Sakar Miki mararki tsula fitsarinki cewar Hunaif,Shuru tayi sai data gaji tace to Mene? Shuru yayi Mata Dan Bai San Me zai Mata ba face ya tsokane ta suyi fada,Yace mamaki nakeyi da kika ce nasanki kina mummuna Haka kamar Ni Zan ko kula irinki? Fada min" Haka dama muke soyayya dake kullum fada? Ga Yan Mata Nan hadaddun Taya Zan kula irinki,Jin cin fuskar da yayi Mata sai zuciyarta ta baci Amma ta danne,Sai baya ta juya Masa da sauri tana goge hawayenta ance Bata da kyau,irin son da take Masa Amma muninta yake gani Taya zai so ta.

   Juyowa tayi ta kalleshi idonta yayi jajir ta rasa me zata Masa kawai sai tace ka cuceni maye kawai,Wai Dan shima ta bashi haushi.
  Dariya ta bashi ma.

   Kallonsa tayi tace Maye me farin zabiya,tsoho kawai Dattijo, Ni sai Dan yaro Dan Shila,Farouq Yana gefe Yana kallonsu Yana dariya,Baki Hunaif ya tabe yace to Ni me zanyi da ke kin min yarinya,Hannunta ya rike tare da shafa tafin hannunta yace Kai yanzu wannan ace hanun mace ne,hannu duk kaushi kamar Bayan crocodile,Ba shiri Khairat tayi dariya tace wannan Kuma ko hassidin bazai ce min Haka ba,yaro anji hannu kamar auduga Kai fa? fa dogo zankala koki kafi kowa tsayi zamarke ,ta nuna Farouq tace frnd naka ya fika kyau shi nake so,Murmushin dake Kara Masa kyau ya saki,Khairat tayi dagalolo tana kallonsa a duniya tana kaunar Hunaif.

   Manyan Ledoji ya fito Mata dasu yace gashi Nan yau kinje Shopping kin kasa siyen komai talaka dake kawai,Mamaki Khairat tayi yaushe ya ganta ita bata sani ba,Amma taji dadin kyautar tasa,ba Bata lokaci ta karba tace nagode badan halinka ba,Kuma Dan na Isa aka siyo min sai ni Khairat me sa mutum yayi kyautar dole ba tare daya shirya ba.
   Mota Hunaif ya Shiga Yana Dariya,Farouq suka gaisa da Khairat sannan taje jikin motar saitin window Hunaif dake mazaunin Driver ta Dan matsa da kanta ciki ta kalli Hunaif tace Yaro na   Dolenka ka siyo min, kwanan Nan zaka Fara kirana da Aunty ta dole.
   Dariya yake kawai yayi sama da glass dinsa yaja mota suka tafi Yana wani nishadi,Khairat ma ta kwashi kayanta tayi Gida tana murna Dadi ya Gama rufeta.
   Farouq ya kalli Hunaif Akan hanyarsu ta dawowa yace Kai Hunaif wannan love Haka da kuke Sha,tsaki Hunaif yaja ku fa Hausawa komai naku kuce soyayya,kawai Ina Jin dadin yanda muke fada Memoryna Yana ajiyewa that's all.

    Mus'af ganin yanzu baya wani samun kudi kawai sai ya tattara ya koma gida ya daina zuwa Office kudin daya Tara su ya zauna ya Sa agaba ya bude duniya yana tsikararta da tsinke,Ummansa da Babansa Sunyi Masa fada da Nasiha har sun gaji sun kyaleshi, aikinsa ya kwashi Mata su tafi Hutawa Yana kashe musu kudade,daga wannan budurwa sai waccan,Shine wajen Aisha,Badriyya,Salima etc har Aikin Hajji ya biyawa wasu Yan Matan nasa,shine siyawa Budurwa wayoyi masu tsada etc anan kudinsa suke karewa sai shaye shaye da ya karu Akan da, yanzu yaci uwar uban da a shaye shaye,yanda yake bulbular hayaki ka rantse salansar mota ce.
  Sabo da shaye shaye duk sai ramewa yakeyi Yana karmashewa sai Dan wuya,Umman Mus'af musamman ta Kira Hunaif ta karanta Masa halin da Mus'af ya sake canjawa tace dan Allah yayi Masa fada,sannan ta Kira Ummi tace danki ya dakko hanyar lalacewa Dan Allah ki Masa fada.

   Ummi Bata ji Dadi ba sai kawai ta tausayawa Mus'af tasan zarginsa take da rashin gaskiya Amma Bata kamashi da kanta ba sai kawai ta maida shi matsayinsa na da yanda yake a Company din,yaji Dadi sosai,Haka Hunaif ya dinga Murna abinda Ummi tayi yaji Dadi ko ba komai Mus'af din nasa zai gyara halayensa idan Yana samun kudi sosai.
   Shi kanshi Mus'af yaji Dadi sosai sai dai ya kullaci Ummi a ransa Yana Nan ya rantse sai ya dau fansa,sannan Kuma har yau Hassadarsa tana Nan Akan Hunaif ya tsani yaji Hunaif ya fishi,burinsa ya kassara Arzikin Hunaif kowa ya rasa,ko zai talauce yafi son Haka matukar Hunaif ma zai talauce.

    Khairat Kuma murna takeyi ta Rama abinda su Talatu suka Mata ko ba komai ta nuna musu iyakarsu,Sannan Hajiya Baturiya ma Haka sannan tana so Nan gaba Dole ta tashi gidan Baturiya sabo da sabon Allah da akeyi yayi yawa,sai Kuma Musa'af Wanda tafi tsana a duniya hanya take nema da za tayi maganinsa irin abinda ya mata.
   Rokon Allah take Hunaif ya aureta ta samu Mus'af a banza tayi maganinsa kowa ya huta.
 Mus'af kuwa sabo da yasan ta Ina zai bullowa Ummi sai yace ya dauki hutu a Office zai zo Abuja gidan su Hunaif zaiyi 2mnths,Ummi Bata damu ba,Hunaif Kuma har da Jin Dadi ma.
    
    Yau Sunday Hunaif Yana guest House nasa tare da Musaf Wanda ya sauka a Abuja jiya,suna Hutawa suna ta buga game,Sai Mus'af yace Wai Ina Yan aikin gidan Nan ne? Gidan ya min Dirty Kuma yunwa nake ji ya kamata kasa a Mana abinci,Hunaif yace me abincin ta tafi ganin gida Amma Bari na Kira wata yarinya na biyata kudi tayi mana ko nasa Ummi ta bayar a kawo Mana? Mus'af ya tabe Baki kawai ka kyale Ummi ta huta, Kira mana yarinyar.
    Hunaif ya nemi waya tare da Kiran Recharge card Sunan da ya sawa Khairat kenan.
   Tana dagawa yace Guesthouse Dina Zaki zo ki dafa mana Abinci Zan biyaki bako nayi,Ladi ta kalla sannan tace tsaya na fadawa Anty ko zata Amince,Ladi ta sanarwa,Ladi tayi shewa tace Kai yaron Nan akwai iyayi wlh,kudi ne suka Masa yawa yaro da kudi,tunda biya zaiyi maza jeki ga harkar Karuwa,Amma dai ki kula ki tsare mutuncinki kina gamawa ki dawo,sannan ki kiyaye kadaicewa da Namiji baligi a gida daya,Dan ma yaron Naga me hankali ne da Dan iska ne baza kije ba,Khairat tace ai na sanshi tun a Kano,Ladi tace ok sai kin dawo.

    Khairat ta shirya tasa Riga da skert na lace tayi kyau da mayafinta tasa flat shoe ba Wanda zai ce batayi kyau ba duk da cewa ba kwalliya tayi ba.
   Tana zuwa gidan taji kida na tashi ya cika gidan tun a Compound Ana ji, Door bell ta danna,Hunaif ne ya bude Mata sanye yake da jallabiya Fara fitted ta Masa kyau matuka ta tsangale Masa Balarabe sak,kamshi ke tashi kawai,Yaki Bata hanya ta wuce Yana Kare Mata kallo,kawai ya tuno da rannan da Bra dinta ta dawo cikinta Bai San sanda ya kwashe da dariya ba,Khairat ta harareshi ta shige ciki sai ko sukayi Ido Hudu da Mus'af, ba karamin Mamakin ganin Khairat Musa'af yayi ba,yasan Hunaif baya tuna baya to me ya sake hadashi da Khairat,Khairat kuwa dama tasan abokin Hunaif ne Bata yi mamaki ba.

    Ganin yanda Khairat ta Kara kyau ,Nan take yaji shaawarta ta taso Masa,gata me kyau Wai me yasa kullum Hunaif ke da sa'a ne a rayuwarsa,samun mace irin Khairat ai sai an tona Amma ga Hunaif a banza ya samu,Wani bakin ciki ya Kama Mus'af Ina ma shine Khairat ke kulawa.

   Ita kuwa Khairat Harara ta watsawa Mus'af ganin kallon da yake mata,Amma dake munafuki ne bai nunawa Hunaif ya santa ba ko tayi aiki a karkashinsa ba,sai ma cewa yayi a Ina ka samo wannan Yar kauyen kuma,? Khairat tace bashi kaci a ranta,Hunaif baiji dadin Furucin Mus'af ba sai ya share shi kawai suka ci gaba da buga game,Khairat Kuma ta Shiga kitchen tana girkinta,tana gamawa Hunaif ya sata gyara gida Nan ma tayi sosai ko Ina ya fito neat.

     Suna ta game tana sani ganin Mus'af Yana ta hararar Hunaif a boye sai ta zauna kusa da Hunaif,tace ranka ya Dade an Gama komai? Wani tsaki Mus'af yaja,Hunaif ya kalli Khairat yace kin rainani fa,Murmushi tayi tace dan Allah kafin na tafi koya min game din Nan Zan na Yi a gida,tun rannan nake so na koya na kasa,Hunaif yace Ok Mus'af Bata Handle naka minti kadan, hararar Khairat yayi tare da jefar da handle din ya mike ya koma Dining ya Shiga cin abincin Khairat me shegen Dadi Wanda shi kadai sai Santi yake a ransa,da niyyar cin kadan yaje sai gashi Yana ta ci.

     Game suka Fara da Hunaif Yana koya Mata suna ta faman dariya,Khairat idan taci sai Murna,wata suka sake sai Hunaif yake ta cinye ta Bata iya ba,yace bafa Haka akeyi ba ya ajiye Handle nasa ya daura hannayensa saman nata dake rike da Handle ya fara koya Mata kin gani,wannan idan kika danna sai kiyi pressing wannan,hannayensu ya Hadu wani shock suke ji a jikinsu,Kasa Kallon Computer Hunaif yayi ya koma kallon Fuskar Khairat gasu gaf da juna,tana shakar kamshinsa Wanda ke kashe Mata jiki,. Mukus tayi ta sandare a Haka sabo da abinda take ji a jikinta,Hunaif ma Haka gashi sai magana yake mata a hankali cikin kunnenta,Wai koya Mata game yakeyi a Haka,dukkansu Babu Wanda ke Fahimta sun manta ma game sukeyi jikinsu kawai wani shock suke ji Wanda Basu taba ji ba Tunda suke.

    Mus'af bakin ciki ya Masa yawa Yama rasa me zaiyi kamar ya hadiyi zuciya,karaji ya kwarara kamar zai kashe musu dodon kunne Wanda ba shiri suka dawo daga duniyar da suka Lula,Khairat ta mike da Sauri tace Zan tafi,Hunaif ya Mika Mata dubu Hamsim rafar yan dari biyar, Musa'af yayi tsalle ya cafki Hannun Khairat tare da fisge kudin Yace Akan Dan wannan abin da tayi shine za a Bata har kudi Haka,wannan karuwar Banzar matsiyaciy.....tas..tas kakeji Khairat ta wanke Mus'af da Mari har biyu tace uwarka ce Karuwa,Kai ka Isa ka taba min ko hannu kazami da kai,Musaf ya mutu a tsaye Ya rasa na Yi Khairat ta fisge kudinta a hannunsa ta kwasa da gudu tasan idan ya dawo hayyacinsa sai ya kusa Halaka ta,Shi Kuma Hunaif shi kanshi Khairat ta bashi haushi ta Mari abokinsa duk da yasan Laifin Mus'af ne amma baiji dadin Marin Mus'af da tayi ba,Bai San Khairat tun tuni da wata a tsakaninsu da Musaf ba, Bai San dama hanya take nema ba,shima Mus'af dama burinsa ya tozarta Khairat tun tuni sai gashi ta rigashi daukan mataki.
   Har zai zauna ya fasa yayi Kan Hunaif da masifa wlh kaje ka kamota na Rama tun wuri,Dariya Hunaif yayi kaji kunya Kato da Kai ka tsaya 18yrs girl ta Mareka Haka Kuma ka kasa komai,ai da nine sai na ballata.

    Tunda Khairat ta fita da gudu Ashe ba tafiya tayi ba,ta glass din window take lekensu tana jinsu,tana kallonsu farin ciki ya isheta sai Muryarta suka ji ta window ta zuro hannu ta dage labilen tace Musa'af in ka Isa Kai Kaine ka Rama,kalli yanda na zabga maka Mari,  in Allah ya yarda sai fuskarka ta kumbura tayi ruwa, wullu ta Masa gwalo Dan bakin ciki kalli kudina a hannu,Kai baka sanni bane Nan gaba sai na zubar maka da hakora,Wai Kai me kudi har da wani gadara kana wani kashe kala kana Shiga shadda Kai me kudi, kallonta Mus'af yake galala,tace hum hum Dalla can daina kallona Ido kamar na zakara.

   Tana ta surutunta Bata San Hunaif ya bar Palon ya fito wajenta ba sai ji tayi caraf an kama Mata hannu Kam,Tayi matukar tsorata ta Fara Dan Allah ka sakeni,in kanawa Allah,wlh na tuba,bazan sake ba,wayyo uwata wayyo ubana,Kokawar kwacewa take ta kasa ta tsuguna tana Jan hannunta dake cikin nasa, Amma ta kasa kwacewa tana ji yace Mus'af fito gata sai ta rushe da kuka,wlh bazan Kara ba, Mus'af Kam da murna ya fito da belt a hannunsa ya kusa karasowa sai Hunaif ya saki Khairat yace ki gudu,ai ko ta arce a guje tana dariya tace wullu na Mari banza.

   Takaici yasa Mus'af ya dauki key din mota kawai ya bar gidan Hunaif a fusace sabo da yaga Lallai Hunaif son Khairat yakeyi,ya daina damuwa dashi,Kuma duk ranar daya Kama Khairat shi kadai yasan me zai Mata,Khairat Kuma tuni ta shige taxi ta gudu Garinsu Suleja.

     Talatu mutanen Kenya ga Kawu ya zame Mata Kaya ko Ina tana rike dashi suyi fada su Shirya sun kwashe sati biyu a Kenya ga Basu da kudin kashewa,Abinci ma ya gagaresu,sun rame,Sunyi baki,ganin ba Mafita sai talatu ta koma bara tana Jan Kawu suna bi titi cikin Tasha suna bara,Kawu yace Ina ma a kasar Hausa ne ai da tallan maganinmu zamuyi mu samu Kudi,Talatu bakin ciki ya isheta ita kadai take ta wahala gashi har ta Kaisu ga bara.

   A masifance tace Dan darajar Allah Kayi min Shuru Sabiu ka dameni taja tsaki tare da fincikar hannun Sabiu ya tafi taga taga ya bigi jikin wata katuwar mota da akayi parking kansa ya fashe jini na fita kadan,Amma Talatu ko a jikinta,yace wayyo kaina Talatu taja tsaki, ragon Namiji kawai Akan Dan wannan kake wayyo, Allah kiyaye ta jashi tana bara a titi gashi Bata Jin yarensu sai dai kawai ta langabe Kai tana Mika hannu,Kawu Yana Kara wani kanne Ido,suna samun kudi sosai kuwa,Kawu yace kaga gari me dadin bara ba irin Kano ba daga biyar sai goma,Talatu kuwa Rana,sanyi Iska ta Kare a kansu,Basu da wurin kwana sai Karkashin gada ko wani waje su Dan fake,rabonsu da wanka har sun manta.

    Bayan Talatu sun samu hutu a gindin wata bishiya tace to Sabiu mun samu kudi ya kamata mu Shiga birnin Kenya sosai ko Allah zai hadamu da Dan Nigeria ayi Mana hanya mu koma gida,Sabiu yace ki Bari dai mu Kara Tara kudi sosai inda idan mun koma gida zamu samu na cefane,Talatu ta harareshi tace wlh na gaji bazan iya ba,Oh Allah sarki Khairat Ashe Haka take Shan wahala,Lallai tayi kokari cewar Sabiu,Talatu tace ai sai yanzu na tabbatar,duka zagi da cin mutunci da muke Mata,mu hanata abinci ta kwana da yunwa ga aikin gida,Kai Dole yarinyar tayi Mana Haka ta azabtu a hannunmu, sai da muka busar Mata da zuciya ta daina tsoro ta Zama Bata kyalewa idan an Mata to gashi muguntar Khairat ta fada kanmu,Kawu ya gyara Zama yace hakkinta ne wlh yake binmu har muka Shiga motar Aljanu oh Allah ya taimakemu da tuni fa Muna birnin sin,Allah yasa nayi dabara muka sauka a Kenya,Kawu yace kafin kyaftawar Ido fa naji Wai an tsaya ance daga Nan baza mu Kara tsayawa ba sai a Birnin sin.

     Talatu tace ka manta ga hakkin Khairat na gadonta,Kai munci zalin yarinyar Dole muyi mummunan karshe matukar Bata yafe Mana ba.ci gaba sukayi da bararsu suna Tara kudi,Talatu tace ko a mota ko ta jirgin ruwa sai mubi mu dawo Nigeria.
   Talatu wahalar da suke Sha ta baci sabo da kwana a titi yini a titi,tun mura na Kama su har ta daina kamasu.

     Zainab da Rahinatu tare da Soja da sauran Kannensu gaba daya sun koma kamar gidan mutuwa,Shuru kake ji,duk masifa iyaye iyaye ne Kuma katanga ne,sai gashi yanzu da kyar suke samu su Dora tukunya,ba kudin sabulu,ba na abinci,ba komai ga sauran kannensu Basu San Babu ba kullum kukan yunwa sukeyi,Soja makarantar ma ta gagara duk da yayi nisa Yana final year Amma Yana gani an wuceshi Yana gida,itama Zainab ba kudin makaranta tana level 2 karatun ya tsaya, Rahinatu da kyar ta Karasa zana waec dinta Neco kuwa Babu kudin da za a je makarantar sai hakura tayi duk da cewa sun Dade da biyan kudin Neco kudin mota ne ya gagaresu,sai da tayi kuka ta gaji Babu mataimaki,Yan ragowar Samarin nasu da suka rage a jikinsu suke Dan samun kudin Abinci kadan,Garin kwaki kuwa har sun gaji da Sha,Haka kantinan Unguwarsu sun gaji da karban bashinsu sun daina Basu,Dole Soja yaji yunwa ta ishesu ya kwashi karnukansa ya Kai gidan wani me kudi da yake son karnuka ya siyar Masa ko wanne guda dubu Biyar, yanzu Babu karnuka Babu kudinsu anci Abinci a gidan,ganin ba sarki sai Allah Zainab ta ajiye girman Kai ta Fara sana'ar wanki da guga ita da Rahinatu,Soja Kuma shine me guga,ba karamin rufa musu asiri sanaar tayi ba.

   Zainab da Rahinatu suna wankinsu Zainab tace kai rayuwa ba Dadi,gaba daya bana Jin dadin duniyar Yan iskan samarin ma duk sun gudu,dama da yawa ba aurenka zasuyi ba,jikin mutum suke so,Yanzu gashi Dan budurcin namu ma mun watsar a titi,tsoron da nake Kar nayi aure Mijina ya gane,Rahinatu tace Allah yasa sau uku na taba yi,sai Romancing,Zainab tace uhmm ai Dan ma Allah ya taimakemu a waye mukayi harkar Dole mutum sai da Cundom ai da tuni munyi ciki ko mun kwashi cuta,Rahinatu tace tuni na fara istigifari Kar na Mutu naci ubana,Zainab ta kalli Kanwar Tata tace ai gwara mu Khairat fa Karuwanci aka turata gashi har tayi kudi,Baki Rahinatu ta tabe tace ke nufinki Khairat dince zatayi Karuwanci kamar Baki santa ba,duk da cewa Dan Adam Yana canjawa Amma nifa Ina da ja wlh Akan Khairat,Shu'uma ce ta gaske Bata da tsoro, Ni tsoro na ma Kar ta fardewa wani Alhajin tumbi Dan Khairat ko a schl Namiji baya ko rike Mata hannu ba a kwashi balai ba,ki duba wayonta da gogewarta idonta Kar ita ce zata yi Karuwanci,Ni wlh ban yarda ba,Zainab tace gaskiya Kam, na tuna Hammad dinta yanda nayi kutun kutun na raba su,gashi tunda ya gane Bai sake ko saurarata ba.

Yace lfy Lau Bari na Baki labarin me ya sameni,Tiryan tiryan ya bawa Khairat labarin Hatsarinsa da abinda ya sameshi baya iya tuna abinda ya faru na last year,sannan Memory nasa baya ajiye komai,yace yanzu na tuna na taba Baki sadaka kina Tallan magani da Kawunki,kinje Office dinmu neman aiki,sannan munyi aiki tare, Kuna yawan fada da Mus'af frnd na.

    Khairat taji tausayinsa Hawaye ya zubo mata ta matsa kusa dashi tace sannu kayi hakuri Dana kasa Fahimta,Baki da laifi Inshallah Zan koma normal.
   Allah yasa cewar Khairat tana murmushi yanzu ko ba komai ta daina Jin Haushinsa,Bayan ya tafi ta koma gida cike da tausayin Hunaif.

   Washe gari Khairat da wuri ta Kira Hunaif lokacin Yana Office tare da Mus'af tace kana ina? Yace Office,Ina son ganinka yanzu idan ba damuwa idan da matsala Kuma watarana...no Ina Free kizo ya Furta da sauri Kar ta fasa zuwa,wata macece ta shigo Office din tayi magana Khairat kishi ya taso Mata Jin Muryar mace na magana da Hunaif dinta,Tace wace wannan?budurwarka ce? Murmushi ya saki yace secretary nace, idan kana busy....ya katse ta da no bana busy kizo ko nazo?kina Ina? Gani zanzo Office naka yanzu,ok sai kinzo yace Mata.

    Mus'af yaja tsaki Wai wace kake wani rawar jiki a kanta Haka,jiba yanda kake zubar da kimarka kana wani azarbabin tazo? Haushi Kuma Musa'af ya bawa Hunaif Akan me zai na wani Jin haushin Khairat,shi Akan Haka zasu Bata da ko waye. Khairat kuwa Office din ta Shiga bako knocking ta Shiga da Sallama,Hannunta dauke da Leda Fara me kyau.
  Mus'af ganin Khairat ce sai yaji kamar yayi hauka,gashi wani son Khairat yake ji,Khairat ganin Musaaf sai taji tsoro sabo da rannan ta Masa rashin kunya da kyar ta dake ta Karasa gaban Hunaif Yana kujerarsa.

    Ina wuni? Ta furta,Hunaif ya amsa kawai, Mus'af Kuma Bai kulata ba itama Bata ko kalleshi ba ta mikawa Hunaif ledar,yace Mene a ciki? Murmushi tayi tace Gift ne naka ne,da sauri ya bude ledar tare da dakko Katon kwali guda biyu ya bude babban Riga t-shirt ya Ciro Fara Kar me tambarin Sky blue a gaban rigar,ta hadu sosai me tsada ce ta Kai dubu Bakwai,Murmushi yakeyi kawai,sannan ya bude na buyu yaga zoben azurfa me shegen kyau na maza,gefe Kuma Perfume ne Gucci, dagowa yayi suka hada Ido da sauri tayi kasa da kanta tana Murmushinta me tsada.

    Yace Thank you so much,you are welcome ta Furta tana Wasa da yatsunta,oya zo ki saka min ring din da hannunki,Kishi ya Gama kashe Mus'af kansa ya sadda kasa Baya so ma ya gani,Khairat ta rike Hannun Hunaif tare da Sa Masa ring din a babban yatsansa ya Masa Masifar Kyau. Ya Kara Furta tnx,tace na tafi,Tsaya na rakaki suka fice tare da Hunaif Mus'af takaici ya dameshi dama shi ta bawa Rigar da ring din,Yana bakin ciki Hunaif yasa kyautar Khairat kawai sai ya sace Gift din Baki daya,Ring ne kawai dake Yana Hannun Hunaif,a motarsa ya jefa Gift din ya dawo Office din yaci gaba da Jiran Hunaif.

     Hunaif kuwa Suna tare da Khairat baya so ma su rabu da juna duk da cewar yasan Kawai mutunci sukeyi ba soyayya ba, a gefen titi suka tsaya suna Hira,ya kalli Khairat yace me kika fi so a yanzu? Karatun boko,naga Yan uwan Mamata da Abba na, Nayi aure..Hmmm yace kawai,taci gaba sannan Na siyi katuwar mota Ina yanga, sannan gidan Mijina na dauki Yan aiki Ina bada doka da Order,sannan Nima na dinga aiki a katon Office me ac da kamshi.
  Yace banji kina lissafo biyayyar da Zaki wa mijinki ba, tab Namiji ai ba Dan goyo bane,duk wacce Naga ma ta Goya Namiji sai na sata ta saukeshi ta sakeshi ya kwala kansa da kasa,dariya Hunaif ya Shiga yi,tace Yana daka min tsawa Zan daka Masa shima na zare Masa ido,Me mazan suka iya a zamanin Nan sai a auri mace a kasa ci da ita,Ni fa bazan Bata lokacina Ina lallaba miji ba,Ko wani waye waye,Kuma ba mutunci ba daga kafa jambaki sai ya siya,Kuma bazan Bari ayi mini gara ba Dan kar ma zuciyarsa ta mutu, gara tana karewa ya sakeni,Wanda kika Raina zakiwa ya kyaleki yarinya,Amma idan nine ko tari baza ki iya ba abinda nace zakiyi,Khairat ta tafi tunani tace ba sai na dinga Addua ba kullum na mallakeka, nifa Nan daka ganni mutunci Bai wadaceni ba,Ina bacci aka raba mutunci,sai da safe Dana tashi aka ce ya Kare,Dariya Hunaif yayi tare da cewa ke kurin banza ne dake bakya iya komai sai tsoron tsiya,wlh Kika yi Wasa sai na aureki Naga iya karshen rashin Mutuncin naki da kike fada,Khairat tace to idan ba tsoro ba ka aureni a gani, Hunaif yace an Gama ki bani Nan da 2mnths,Yayi nisa Ina laifin 3wks ma a daura,yace to an Gama yarinya,Khairat Bata yi tunanin Hunaif da gaske yake ba Sam Wasa take Masa ita.

    Mus'af ne ya fito da motarsa zai tafi ya gaji da jiran Hunaif Yana Fitowa ya iskesu gefen titi sai dariya suke suna Hira,Glass na motarsa ya sauke yace kaji kunya da wannan kazamar ka tsaya a titi ana kallonka,Khairat ta Kalli Mus'af sai ta Masa Dakuwa (Ambola) tace kaga ta tuwo kaga ta Miya kaga ta tattasai da tumatir who are you? 
   Mus'af maimakon ta bashi haushi sai dariya ma data bashi wannan zagin nata tun suna Yara yasanshi.

    A taxi Hunaif ya sata tare da biyan Drop sannan ya koma Office,Yana Shiga yaga ba gift tabbas yasan Mus'af ne ya sace,ran Hunaif yayi Masifar baci, Akan ka taba kayan Khairat gwara ka cinye Masa milliyoyin kudi,mota ya Shiga a fusace yabi Bayan Mus'af Wanda tuni Yana Palon Ummi,Yana Shiga bako sallama ya shaki wuyan Mus'af sosai ba Wasa idonsa yayi jajir yace ina abinda Khairat ta bani? Mus'af yayi Masifar mamakin Hunaif da fushi haka,rabon da yaga Hunaif a irin wannan Hali tun mutuwar Abbinsa,Tsoro ne ya Kama Mus'af yace Yana motata dama dakko maka nayi Zan kawo maka gida na Adana maka su.
    Hunaif yasan karya yake a hasale yace bani kawai karka Kara taba min Abu wlh Akan Haka zamu Bata har abada.
 
   Dadi Ummi taji da Hunaif ya fara gano Halin Musa'af,Ummi tace haba Hunaif Kai da kake me hakuri me ya hadaku?
  Ummi Kinga shine Baya son zaman lfy,Ina ruwansa da yarinya tunda ya ganta ya tsaneta kullum Yana zaginta kawai fa Ina sanin me nake domin ko Mene indai akanta ne bana mantawa,ya ganmu tare Kuma ya damu yarinya,da dama Yana min Abubuwa kawai kyaleshi nakeyi.
  To kayi hakuri ga kayanka Nan ma ya dakko maka cewar Ummi,fisge ledar Hunaif yayi daga hannun Mus'af, ya Haura Samansa a matukar Hasale.
   Mus'af kuwa wani mugun kallo yake bin Hunaif dashi tare da Ummi,shi kadai yasan irin muguntar da yake hadawa.
     
    Talatu Ana titi tare da kawu a kasar Kenya Ana zuba bara wata Trailer ta kwace driver Yana bacci ta taho Kan mutane saura kadan ta talitse su Kawu Amma duk da Haka ta fyallar dasu sun daki wata Taxi daga Nan Basu sake sanin inda suke ba,sai ji Talatu tayi Ana kwanta karki tashi cikin harshen turanci,Tana bude Ido ta ganta saman gadon asibiti tare da kawu shima a nasa gadon,kudin da suka Dade suna Tarawa ta duba taga Babu ko sisi barayi sun sace lokacin da basa hayyacinsu,kawai sai gani Nurses sukayi Talatu ta rushe da kuka,Tunaninsu Zafin ciwo ne,ai tuni suka Danna Mata Allurar bacci,Kawu kuwa Makaho Yana farkawa ya fara Khairat Allahumma Tafatsinini a kanki,Shima aka tsira Masa karfen nasara sai Shuru kake ji Sunyi baccin Dole.
    Da yamma Talatu ta farka tana tashi ta koma kamar mahaukaciya ta Fara Kenya Allah ya tsine muku,Mutanen Kenya Allah wadaranku,Kenya tsinannen gari,wayyo gwara na Mutu na huta,Da kyar aka samu Talatu tayi Shuru,Kawu Yana farkawa tace an sace Mana kudi ta rushe da kuka, Nurses suna Bata hakuri da yaren Kenya Talatu tace kunci ubanku tsinannu bakaken Banza, Kawu Kuma cewa yake ku kyaleta tayi Kuka,Talatu Yi kuka kinji ko kyaji sanyi,Nima kukan zanyi yanzu, wlh da a Hannuna Kahon busa tashin Alkiyama yake da tuni na hura shi kowa ya mutu a tashi duniya a huta,Talatu tana kuka tace ai wuta zamu Shiga,Khairat Bata yafe Mana ba,hakkinta ne yake binmu da halayenmu Marasa kyau,Kawu yace ah na tuna bana Hura kaho ba..Harara Talatu ta zuba Masa tace maza kayi sabo Masifar da muke ciki ta karu.

    Talatu kullum suna asibiti Yan Kenya sun rasa wanne yare takeyi Amma zasu ji tana Allah tarwatsa kasar Kenya ya tsine musu,sai dai suyi ta Basu hakuri da turanci,Ana kawo musu bill na asibiti Nan take Talatu ta yayyaga takardar ta cafki wuyan Nurse din da kyar aka raba su,Masifar Talatu tasa Dole suka sallamesu kyauta ba tare da sun biya sisin asibiti ba.
   Tunda suka ci gaba da bara ganin Yan Kenya basa Jin Hausa sai Talatu ta koma wakar bara da Allah ya tsine muku Yan Kenya....Kenya Allah ya tsine muku Yan Kenya ..Haka take ta rerawa tana langabewa, tunanin Kowa Addua takeyi da wani yaren tana roko,sai suyi ta Basu sadaka Talatu suna caskar Naira.
  Wani Dattijo Dan Kenya yayiwa Talatu magana da yarensu Wai Yan Nigeria ne? Talatu da sauri tayi gwari gwarin turancinta  tace yes yes mu from Nigeria can Kano stase (state), Mutumin yace Uhmmm,Dan Talatu ta birgeshi ya taimaka musu sai Kawu yace kice yazo mu tafi Nigeria yaci abinci me dadi.
    Talatu kuwa tace mu damu da Kai You muje to Nigeria eat shinkafa da wake,Dankali,da rogo eat Food Dadi, mutumin Bai gane me Talatu take nufi ba,ganin yanda take wani washe bakinta ba hakoran gaba sai ya harareta yayi tafiyarsa.
   Sabiu yace shashaSha Haka ake turancin duk kin damalmale da Hausa me zai gane,Ni Bari mu hadu da wani a hanya kiji yanda ake turanci.
   Talatu tana sani Dan ta kure Kawu sai ta tare wani Dan matashi,tace bismillah Kawu Sabiu Nemo Mana taimako ga yaro Dan Kenya, kace yasa a maidamu Nigeria da harshen turanci tunda ka fini iyawa. Kawu ya gyara tsaiwarsa tare da yin gyaran murya ehem..ehem....

      Kwana biyu Khairat Bata siyar wa da Ladi Kati sabo da yanda Hunaif ya hanata sakat kullum ya kirata a waya,ko yazo su hadu suyi fada suyi Hira.
  Kamar Wasa Hunaif suna tare da Khairat a jikin motarsa unguwarsu sai kansa ya Sara ya rike kansa sai ya fara tuna baya tsakaninsa da Khairat,har sanda ruwa ya taso ta Shiga motarsa,da zuwa gidanta da yayi,tare da yaran Nan Mohd da Meenal,har shirye shiryen auresu kaf ba abinda Bai dawo Masa ba Amma iya abinda ya shafi Khairat da shi,sauran abubuwan baya tunawa, farin ciki ne ya mamayeshi Wanda har ya kasa dannewa sai Murmushi yakeyi ya riko hannun Khairat ba zato,yace Kece Khairat wadda naje gidanki har naci Danwake,nace Zan aureki,na Baki takardar Rules,sannan na dauki Meenal da Mohd na kaiwa Ummi,Ummi Kuma ta bawa sister nata yaran sabo da matsalar Dana samu,Khairat farin ciki ya kamata da ya tuno da komai yanzu,da sauri ya rungume Khairat Kam a jikinsa tare da kissing nata a lips,da kyar ta kwace kanta badan ta so hakan ba,ya kalleta still Yana rike da hannunta yace Address din danginku da Kawu ya bani Yana Nan Zan dakko muje garin naku ki shirya muje Saturday,Kuma aurenmu Yana Nan baza a fasa ba duk da cewa ba soyayya muke ba,Zan aureki in kin Amince? Khairat tace na Amince,Khairat a ranta tace muje zuwa.

     Saturday da wuri suka shirya ya turo Driver ya dauki Khairat ya kaita Aairport zasu wuce Taraba state, wasu Arabian Riga da skert ya bawa yaronsa Usman ya kawowa Khairat masu Masifar tsada,sai Kaya kala uku Suma ready made sun hadu Wai tayi Shirin tafiya,Murna wajen Khairat ba a magana,kicif ta shirya Yar Jakar daya Aiko Mata ta Yan gayu komai na bukata ta zuba, ta shirya cikin Arabian Riga da skert tayi bala'in kyau sosai light blue and black color,Haka takalmi da jaka ma same color Wanda Hunaif ya kawo,Ladi tana ta kodata gaskiya kinyi kyau Khairat karfa ki zautar da yaro,dariya tayi kawai sukayi sallama da Ladi ta Shiga rantsatsiyar motar Hunaif da Driver yazo daukanta.

    Tana zuwa Airport ta hango Hunaif da ruwa Eva Yana Sha Yana Danna waya,gefensa Yar karamar Jakar maza ce ta manyan Yara ya hade cikin Shadda light blue da takalmi Baki agogonsa Baki dama Bai fiye sa wata hula ba,Suma taci kudi sai sheki yakeyi,Khairat wani nishadi take ji sai wani fara'a takeyi,ji take kamar tafi ko wacce mace duniya,Nan kanta ya Kara girma,ta Fara yanga da gadara tana taku dai dai kamar wacce zata tafi England,tun kafin ta karaso wajensa da kyar ya gane Khairat sabo da tsananin kyan data yi, kamar balarabiya,sai yaji ta Kara birgeshi Bai taba ganinta da kwalliya Haka ba sai yau.
  Murmushi yake saki shi kadai tana karasowa ya sunkuyo tare da leka Fuskarta Yana dariya yace kwalliya Kika yi min? Gaskiya na iya zaben Kaya,Khairat tayi Murmushi tace ai wacce tasa kayan ita ce me kyan ba kayan ba,dadina dake kuri da yabon Kai cewar Hunaif,yarinya kinyi dacen miji Dan Umminsa, kafin ya rufe Baki tace kaima kayi dacen mace Khairat marainiyar Allah zankadedediya son kowa kin Wanda ya rasa,Murmushi ya saki suka tafi aka musu Screening tare da shigewa jirgi,Khairat gata ga Hunaif sit dinsu su kadai,Kamshi kawai suke musamman Hunaif sarkin kamshi,Khairat an Shiga jirgi yau harda zaro Qurani a jaka ta Fara karance karancen adduoi Allah ya saukesu lfy,Hunaif ya kalleta ta birgeshi Yana son mutum me addini da yawan addua.

   Mintuna kadan sai gasu a Taraba,Ashe tuni Hunaif yasa an shirya Masa lafiyayyar mota tare da driver Dan garin Taraba Wanda yasan lungu da sako a garin, Khairat ta kalleshi a ranta tace kudi masu gidan nara,ko me kake so indai da kudi an Gama, ita kanta abar motar abar  kallo ce,baya ta shige kusa Da Hunaif sabo da kamshi da sanyin dake motar a fili Khairat tace Naira maganin masifa da  Jarabar duniya,Naira masu gidan nara.
 Hannu ya Mika ta tare da Furta bani Address note din naki uwar surutu.
  
   Yar takardar data rubuta Address din da Kawu ya Basu ta Mika Masa shi Kuma ya mikawa Driver,Ido Driver ya zaro yace tab Kauye ne sosai kafin muje kauyen sai munyi kusan 4hrs,nisa ne da garin,idan zaku ci Abinci ma ya kamata kuci tun muna cikin gari,Hunaif yace muje kawai bama Jin yunwa, a'a nifa bana jure yunwa Allah ya gani sai naci na koshi nake iya tafiya cewar Khairat, Dole aka tsaya a wani eatery na manyan yara suka yi take away sannan suka dauki hanya.

    Daji ne sosai suka Shiga abin tsoro,Khairat tsoro ma takeyi Kar matsala ta samesu a Dajin,suna tafiya Sunyi rabi Motar tasu Haka kawai ta mutu a Dajin,Karfen nasara ba tabbas,Tsoro ya Kama Khairat Amma Driver da Hunaif ko a jikinsu,anyi anyi motar ta tashi Taki,Hunaif Yana fita Khairat ta fice da gudu ta makale kusa dashi kafa ya motsa sai ta motsa,Driver yace mota sabuwa dal kawai ta mutu karfen nasara,suna ta gyara Driver da Hunaif Amma taki ko motsi har Magrib ta wuce,a wurin sukayi Alwala da salloli sannan suka ci take away nasu.

     Sallaya Hunaif ya dakko tare da Shimfida musu shida Khairat a gindin bishiya ko Ina koren ciyayi luf luf fresh air na kadawa,Driver Yana can jikin mota Yana fama ta tashi taki.
   Dare yayi 8pm Bayan Sunyi sallar Isha Tsoro da bacci ya Kama Khairat tana gyangyadi Hunaif na gefenta Yana latsa waya sai ji yayi ta Fado jikinsa,dama ya Santa da bacci duk inda ya kamata a Nan zatayi,Murmushi yayi Yana karewa kyakyawar Fuskarta kallo,kwanciyarta ya gyara Mata tayi matashi da cinyarsa baccinta takeyi sosai sai da ya gaji yaga Allah ba Wasa ba Driver ya shige mota yayi kwanciyarsa Yana bacci,shi kanshi Hunaif yanzu tsoron Dajin ne ya kamashi,ba shiri ya zame Kan Khairat daga cinyarsa a hankali,ya Dan matsa can karshen katuwar carpet din ya kwanta Yana so shima yayi bacci,idonsa ya rufe ruf.

  Cinnaka ne ya sadado ya ciji Khairat ta mike a firgice tana Sosa wajen,Daji ga duhu ko Ina  Tsoron Aljanu ya Kama Khairat ta Matsa jikin Hunaif ta kwakwume shi,Yana jinta shima tsoron yake ji baya so ya bude idonsa.
    Kukan wani Abu sukaji Khairat tace wayyo namun daji ne ga kukan Damusa can,Hunaif da sauri yace Allah? Wani Abu yayi wani Gurnani,Hunaif ya juyo tare da rungume Khairat sosai itama ta shige jikinsa tana cewa fada sukeyi da Zaki da Damusa wancan kukan Zaki ne,Innalillahi cewar Hunaif mu koma cikin mota,da sauri suka tashi suka tafi wurin motar da sauri,Driver ya farka a tsorace shima yace lfy? Hunaif yace Dabbobin daji ne harda su Damusa gasu can suna ta kuka,Driver ya koma gaba da sauri,Khairat da Hunaif suna Bayan mota,Abin mamaki Driver na gwada tashin mota sai kawai sukaji mota ta tashi lafiya Lau,farin ciki ya kamasu,yaja mota suka ci gaba da tafiya,Khairat da Hunaif bacci sukeyi sosai,har Allah ya taimakesu suka kusa zuwa garin daga Nan suka dauki Hanyar kauyen,lokacin 12am, Saida Driver ya kawosu lfy cikin garin sannan ya samu wuri yayi parking motar ganin darene Bai tashi Hunaif ba,shima sai ya gyara kwanciya ya fara baccinsa.
    Basu farka ba sai Asuba Kiran sallah ya tashesu, da ruwansu Na roba sukayi Alwala sannan Hunaif da Driver suka tafi masallaci,Khairat ta Shimfida sallaya jikin mota tayi Sallah da azkhar sannan ta koma motar taci gaba da baccinta, Hunaif ma dawowa yayi yaci gaba da bacci,Driver kuwa ya bazama garin abinsa.
    Tunda suke bacci sai sha daya suka tashi,Lokacin Driver tuni yaje table din me shayi yayi hadin kauri ya karya abinsa.
   Khairat ta Kalli Hunaif,shima ya kalleta suka sakarwa juna Murmushi,Driver yace Hajiya ki fito tuni na tambayi gidajen da kuka bani Address an samu kuma.
   Khairat ta fito ta Dan gyara Fuskarta da jikinta,Suka tafi,Gidan me Unguwar Garin shine Dan yayan Baban Khairat.

   Khairat tace to kaji Ashe ma jinin sarauta zaka aura,dariya Hunaif yayi kawai suka Shiga gidan,da Sallama matar gidan ta amsa tana kallon Khairat,tace shigo,Khairat tace da bako nazo,haba gidan ai gidan jama'a ne ce Masa shima ya shigo,Ganin Hunaif ya shigo Dattijuwar wata juwa ta kwasheta don tunaninta Bature ne yazo,sai taji yayi Sallama Kuma ya gaisheta,ta amsa da fara'a sannan ta Shimfida musu tabarma katuwa,ga gidan ko Ina tsaf, Me  Unguwa ta kirawo a dakinsa tace kazo kayi Baki,Tunda yaga Khairat yasan jininsu ce,Bayan sun gaisa da me Gari Khairat tayi Masa bayanin ko wace ita,Me unguwa yace Allahu Akbar dama Sabiu na Raye,Munje Munje baya zuwa karshe ma idan Munje Kano akace ya canja gida sannu Khairat,Allah yaji kan Mahaifinki Dan uwanmu,Khairat tace wannan Zan aura shine nazo na sanar muku,Ina shi Sabiun? Khairat tace Yana Kano tace Nasha wahala a hannunsa Nan ta kwashe labari ta bawa me Unguwa.

    Me Gari yace ai tun Sabiu na yaro Haka Halinsa yake, ba mutumin kirki bane Allah Yana sane zai saka miki,yanzu ku huta kuyi wanka sai a rakaku wurin dangi kaf,Gidan Mamanki Yana can gaba damu,Khairat tana ta murna aka bawa Hunaif wani daki simintine aka sa carpet da katuwar Katifa yasha gyara,me kyau ko Ina fes,ita Kuma Khairat ta Shiga dakin Matar gidan me suna Adama.
    Sai ga Babbar Yar Adama me Suna Suwaiba16yrs,Tunda taga Khairat ta manne Mata.

   Adama ta Fara dafawa Hunaif ruwan wanka,yayi wanka da Brush,Khairat ma Haka,ga gida ya dau kamshin soye soye duk da cewa kauyene,Sai ga Adama dauke da katon tire ta kawo musu kayan Kari,Flask din Kunun gyada ne,ga chips,sai soyayyar doya da kwai,wani plate kuma cike da Naman zabi.
    Khairat ta shirya cikin doguwar Riga black and red ta dauki tire din ta Shiga dakin Hunaif ta ajiye musu suka zauna suna ta ci magana kasa kasa kamar munafukai,Khairat tayi Muryar rada tace kaga a kauye harda Chips,Hunaif shima kasa da murya yace Kuma ta iya girkin Yar tsohuwa Haka,harda Kunun gyada cewar Khairat,Hunaif yace Dan Naga tana da Tsafta ne da bazan Ci ba,Nima Haka Khairat ta Furta.
   Me Unguwa ne ya shigo suka ci gaba da Hira sosai suna cin abinci kamar sun Shekara da sanin juna.

     Sai da suka huta sannan da Yamma Me Unguwa da kansa yace kuzo muje Khairat a rakaki wurin Dagacin garin Nan shine Yayan Mamanki uwarsu daya ubansu daya dake auren zumunci akayi shi yasa Kika gaji sarauta ta fannin uwa da uba,Khairat tanaji ta kalli Hunaif tana murmushi suka hada ido,kasa da Murya tayi tare da rada Masa kaji fa jinin sarauta ce Ni Dole kayi biyayya,Haba shi yasa a jikina nake tunanin Anya ba jinin sarauta bace Ni,sabo da Haka kawai Me Unguwa sai kaga Ina gadara da takama,na rasa Dalilin hakan Ashe ma ga inda nayi gado.
   Me Unguwa ya washe Baki yace ai Dole kiyi domin Ummanki da Abbanki jinin sarauta ne,Khairat tace ai Kawu komai nawa sai naji kullum kaina Yana Kara girma,ga Isa ga mulki watarana idan abin ya motsa min ko magana bana yi,Me Unguwa shima kamar yaro biyewa Khairat yakeyi sabo da yanda yake Jin kansa Me Unguwa ne ka rantse sarkin Kano ne, Hunaif Yana jinsu dariya suke Bashi Akan me Unguwa da Dagaci irin na kauye sai Alfahari sukeyi.

   Me unguwa ne ya katse Masa tunani da cewa ai Dole ki Zama me Gadara da Izza ai jinin sarauta ce ke gaba da baya,kwana Nan za a bawa Kanin Mamanki Me Unguwa again,Khairat tana murna tace ehem ai a Nan zan zauna har ayi bikina,Harara Hunaif ya watsa Mata tare da cewa gobe zamu tafi kima shirya.
    Gidan Dagaci suka Fara zuwa,sunsha mamakin yanda Khairat ta girma Haka,Sunyi murna tare da Allah wadai da Jin labarin Kawu da Talatu,Karrama su Khairat akeyi sosai shi Kuma Hunaif Yana musu bulala da Kudade masu nauyi.

   Har dare suna aikin Zaga dangi har suka Gama suka koma masaukinsu wajen Me Unguwa.
    Me Unguwa kuwa da daren ya zauna tare da Khairat da Hunaif sai Matarsa Adama tare da Dagacin garin yace zai musu Nasiha tunda aure zasuyi.

    Me Unguwa ya fara Nasiha sosai me ratsa jiki sannan karshe yace Khairat bamu gaji tsokana da wulakanci ba,karki yi tsokana Amma duk wanda ya tabaki ki taba shi ko waye,karki Bari a taka ki,kaf danginmu bama daukan raini,ki tabbatar kinyi gado,Mamaki ya Kama Khairat da Hunaif, Dagaci ya amshe yace ice ko a makaranta bakya ragawa kowa? Ko yatsa mutum ya nunaki to ki balla yatsan ko uban waye,Nan da kika ganmu kaf ba a taka mu a zauna lfy,kema karki sake sannan ki rike mijinki Gam karki Zama shashasha wata ta kwace Miki shi,Adama tace ato kinji dai da kike mace ki tsaya ki Zama mace sosai wurin me gida yaran yanzu ba wuya sun kwace Miki miji,ko kishiya za a Miki karki kulata da fada Amma tana tabaki ki wanketa da soso da sabulu,Khairat tace ai Kawu Sam bana ragawa duk Wanda ya Shiga gonata,nifa duk inda naje idan aka cuceni sai na bar musu lesson,Me Unguwa yace Mene lessin (lesson) Kuma?
   Darasi cewar Dagaci sabo da Yana da ilmi shi yayi Nce.
   Me Unguwa yace Madalla kinyi dai dai yanzu nasan ke jininmu ce,ai Me Unguwa gashi Nan ka tambayeshi shi kanshi ba kyaleshi nakeyi ba cewar Khairat tana Nuna Hunaif, shi Kam Hunaif dariya ma suke bashi abin nasu kamar wasan Yara.

   Talatu a jirgin ruwa Kato tare da Kawu duk jirgin bata Gari sunfi yawa a ciki,sabo da Haka Ana bada abinci,Talatu ga cin masifa tace wannan abinci baifi na turashi a hanci ba aikin banza,ta tafi tace a Karo Mata suka ce sai dai ta siya,Talatu ta zaro Yar Doller darinta zata siya wasu Majiya karfi Maza masu kalar Yan China suka zo tare da zare Mata wuka,Dole ta Mika musu kudin suka fisge sukayi tafiyarsu abinsu.
    Talatu ba abinci ba kudi,salab salab ta dawo kusa da Kawu ta zauna tare da yin tagumi.
   Jirgin ruwa dai Yana ta tafiya abinsu lfy har Allah ya taimakesu suka kwashe kwanaki a cikin ruwa ba dare ba Rana har suka tsaya a lagos,Talatu tana Fitowa ta dinga murna tana godewa Allah sannan Kawu yace saura mu tafi Kano a Ina zamu samu kudin komawa ki Bari muyi Bara ko ta kwana biyarce mu samu kudin mota,ba da son ran Talatu ba Amma ya zasuyi Dole su hakura sabo da sun San baza a daukesu kyauta ba.
   A Lagos suka zauna tare da Fara bara,lungu da sako suna ta Tara kudi,gashi kwana a kasan gada aikinsu ne.

   Sun kwashe Kwana Uku ba karamin kudi suka Tara ba dake Kudu ne,Amma wahala ta ishesu, a kusa da shagon wani Yoruba suka zauna,Ranar Kuma wasu suka sacewa bayaraben sabuwar wayarsa me tsada,sai kawai ya kalawa su Talatu sata, yace Wai sune suka satar Masa waya,Nan fa rigima ta kacame,Yan uwansa Yoruba suka ratayawa Kawu Taya a wuya da Talayu zasu konesu,Kawu ya rushe da kuka Haka Talatu ma,Da kyar Allah ya kawo wasu Hausawa suka fanshi su Talatu da kyar kafin a konesu,ana sakinsu Talatu tace Ni da Lagos har a bada Nan taja Kawu sai Tasha, kudinsu Bai Gama cika ba Babu Wanda ya kulasu ,sai suka nemi trailer wacce ake eban shanu Ana kaiwa kudu,Kudi kalilan suka bayar Talatu ta daka tsalle ta fada Bayan  motar Shanu,sannan masu motar suka daga Kawu sama tare da jefashi shima ciki,mutane da yawa Yan cirani suka cika motar Shanu tab sannan suka dauki Hanyar Kano.

    Suna Tafiya Sunyi nisa sosai Yan fashi suka tare motar su Kawu Dan abinda ke hannun kowa sai da Yan fashi suka kwace,Sannan suka samu suka musu dukan tsiya duk jikinsu a farfashe gashi Sunyi tumurmusu a kasa sai suka dawo kamar an tono su daga cikin Toka kowa yagansu sai ya tausayawa su Talatu kamar Mahaukata Haka suka dawo suna doyi da tsami,a Motar shanun ma Babu Wanda ke matsawa kusa dasu.Talatu kuwa tana can karshen Motar ta time karfe idan ta bude Baki da niyyar yin magana Wanda yake farkon Motar sai yajiyo Doyin bakinta,hakora sun dafe, Sunyi yellow har gansa kuka suke,Gwara Kawu Yana wanka sannan Yana yin aswaki kullum da itace.

    Wata Yare Igbo ce tana kusa daTalatu,sannan tana Jin Hausa Talatu tayi Hamma, kai.....matar ta Furta da karfi sannan tace me kana ci Haka? Cikinka na buso wari ohhh I can see Naga baki naka baka Brush?,pls Ajiya Kana wanka da Brush ka goge baki naka,Sai ki kashe mutum da wari.
   Talatu na fada Miki bakya jin magana, zan iya sakinki fa kina cin darajar yaranki kawai Amma kazantar Taki tayi yawa cewar Kawu shima.
   Talatu tace wahalar duniya ce kawai Amma Zan gyara halayena kayi hakuri.
  Duk bake Kika jawo min ba, bakya bani shawarar arziki,naci Amanar Dan Uwana na jini,na cuci marainiyar Allah,na nuna son kai,bazan yafe Miki ba,Talatu Hawaye ya zubo Mata tace naga darasi ka yafe min,zan gyara halayena mu hadu mu gyara halinmu.

    Yayin Da Zainab su Kuma damuwa ta musu yawa,wahalar yau daban ta jibi daban,ta gobe daban itama,ga rashin iyaye,sun Kara Masifar lalacewa komai ya tabarbare musu,gashi Mijin aure ma suke nema Amma ya gagara,Soja kuwa kullum bashi da aiki sai tunanin Khairat.
   Yanzu Masifar son Khairat yakeyi,ya Kira wayarta har ya gaji Bata Shiga,damuwa ta Masa yawa, Zainab tana zaune tayi tagumi ga yaran kannenta na Kuka basa jure yunwa,sanaar wankin ma Bata
Samu ba,Rahinatu ce ta shigo futu futu da ita sabo da Babu Sabulun wanki da wanka,Leda ta ajiye tace Aunty ga garrin  kwaki da sugar da kyar na Samu Dennis ya bani bashi, mu samu mu jika musha kafin dare muga abinda Allah zaiyi,Zainab ta kalli Soja ya kamata ka nemi sana'ar hannu ga wurin Uba carpenter can tunda mutumin kirki ne ya koya maka kana Zama kana samo mana ko na abinci ne,a Haka Khairat zata aure ka? kana zaune ba Sana'a gaka lafiyayyen Namiji Amma mu Mata mu muke Rika gida, mazan zamani matasa Musamman Hausawa burin kowa sai yayi kudi, sai Kuna Raina sana'a, matasa lafiyayyu Amma zuciyarsu ta mutu.

    Soja Jin ance Khairat baza ta aure shi ba matukar Babu sana'a,sannan komai kankantar Sana'a yafi Zama Haka musamman a wajen Namiji,Nan take ya mike ya tafi wurin Uba Carpenter ya rokeshi Allah Annabi suka Fara aiki tare,sai gashi kullum Soja idan suka tashi Yana samo dari biyar dubu daya,watarana ma har dubu biyu Uba yake bashi, sai gashi basa rasa na cefane da sabulun wanki da wanka harda na Omon wankya wanke,gashi yanzu sun dage da Tsafta sosai suke gyara gidansu fes.
   Soja shima yanzu yafi Jin dadin rayuwarsa,sannan ya tabbatar da shi Namiji ne Yana rike kannensa.

    Mus'af Kwance yake a  Hotel Room dinsa Bai San Hunaif yayi tafiya ba,sabo da Sam Hunaif yanzu ba komai yake fadawa Mus'af ba,Ummi ma kanta ce Mata yayi ya tafi Meeting Kwara state,Bata San me ya tafi Yi ba bare wani Mus'af,Tunanin Khairat ya hanashi Sakat idan Kuma ya tuno Hunaif na sonta shima a fili sai ya Furta sai naga bayanka Hunaif,baka Isa ba,baza ka auri Khairat ba nine nake sonta Dani ta Dace.
   
    Washe gari Hunaif yayi Shirin komawa Abuja sannan Fafur yaki yarda Khairat ta zauna wurin danginta har ayi bikinsu,Dole ta hakura zata bishi su Koma in yaso idan an kusa Bikin saura sati daya sai tazo har ayi komai a Gama a kai Amarya.
    Bayan Sun dawo Abuja da Sati daya,Hunaif ya sanarwa Ummi da Yanzu Yana tuna Khairat wacce yace zai aura Nan ya bawa Ummi labarin komai Haka suka ga Dr yace a hankali ma zai tuna komai,zai dawo normal,farin ciki ya cika Ummi,ba tare da Bata lokaci ba ta sanarwa dangin Uban Hunaif Kan suzo nemawa dansu Aure.
     Bayan sati Guda sai ga bakin Larabawa sun sauka a Nigeria,da Hunaif suka tafi Kauyen su Khairat suka Kai dukiyar aure da komai ,Ladi ta Hana Khairat komawa wurin danginta,tace can Kauye ne Babu kayan gyara Amarya,Ladi tace kawai suje can kauyen a dauro aure ke Kuma ayi shagalin biki a gidana Dangin naki duk suzo Abuja asha shagali Bayan an daura auren.
   Haka suka shirya komai da Ladi duk da cewar ba shagali za ayi ba sai Kamu kawai za ayi sannan a daura aure a Kai Amarya.,su Kuma Dangin Khairat suka ce sai dai Khairat taje can ko Ana gobe Daurin aure ne,idan an daura sai a kawo Amarya a mutunce,Hunaif ya dauki nauyin komai na biki.sannan Ummi tasa ya bawa Khairat kudi masu nauyi na gyaran jiki,Ladi Kuma tare da kawarta me Hada Amare sun Fara aikinsu Akan Khairat.
 
     Hunaif a waya ya Kira Khairat Kan ta fito Yana kofar gidansu,lokacin da yamma ne,Khairat ta kalleshi tace muje yawo a kafa mu Dan zaga layin Nan,Hunaif Bai San manufar Khairat ba ya biye Mata suka jera suna tafiya tare gwanin Sha'awa, farin ciki ya mamaye musu zuciya,suna Jin wani nishadi da shauki,Hannunta ya rike ta fisge abinta tare da cewa sai ka Bari sai an daura Auren tukun,Oh Dan na rike hannunki wannan Hannun naki ma duk tauri ba laushi,Tafiya suke suna Hira Khairat tana ta zage unguwar da Hunaif Ana ta kallonsu,Hunaif yace Wai Ina zamuje ne sai zaga unguwarku mukeyi har Tasha da kasuwa kin kaini,Murmushi tayi tace so nake nayi yanga da gadarata kowa yasan Ina da saurayi me kudi Kuma balarabe kalli yanda na birge mutane sai kallonmu ake kowa Yana Jin dama shine,Dariya Hunaif yayi suna tafiya duk Majalisa sai Khairat tace musu Salamualaykum idan tasan wani a ciki ma sai ta Kira sunansa sun gaisa dan a gane Khairat ce da Alhaji Hunaif.
    Majalisar su Me Dawa suka zo wucewa ta wajen suna ta Shan wiwi, Khairat ta musu Sallama suka amsa tace Me Dawa a huta lfy, kishi da takaici ya mamaye Me Dawa, Khairat ta Kalli Hunaif cike da Shagwaba tace Ni ka bani Kudi a Dan Yi musu kyauta,Hunaif ya zaro Yan dubu dubu ya Bata Yana Murmushi,ta mikawa Me Dawa tace gashi ku raba inji Alhajina, Murna ta kamasu suka Fara yiwa Khairat kirari sai Khairat ta Hunaif,Khairat tace Alhaji Hunaif Naira cikakken sunansa Haka ake ce Masa,Kiri Kiri ta karfi a Unguwar Nan Khairat sai tace sunansa Alhaji Hunaif Naira,Mata kuwa sai Sha'awa suke da kishi Ina ma sune suka samu Hunaif balarabe.

    Khairat abin nata Bai tsaya a Nan ba sai da ta shiga da Hunaif gidan Makwafta da suke mutunci,tayi ta Sa Hunaif Yana Kyautar kudi,Kafin kace me an San da zaman Khairat a Unguwar tare da Alhaji Hunaif Naira,sai girmama Khairat akeyi,Hunaif ya gaji ta rokoshi mota tace Alhmdllh na kankaro mutunci na Dama yan unguwar Nan suna min kallon talaka Yar tuwo tuwo me Saida Kati Basu daukeni komai ba,kowanne gara sai yazo wajena,to yau na Gama dasu,Burina ya cika kayi hakuri na wahalar dakai Naira tayi kuka. Murmushinsa Mai tsada yayi yace ba damuwa,shi Hunaif baida zafi babu ruwansa,hakan ma yasan yarinta da kuruciya ce ke damun Khairat dinsa birgeshi takeyi,komai tayi sai ta birgeshi Bata laifi. 
   Bayan Sunyi Sallama tace Kai me Kudi Ni jinin sarauta ce karka Fara girman Kai Kaga yau Ina cewa me kudi to Nima Ina takama da sarauta.
  Dariya Hunaif yayi tare da riko Hannunta zai Mata Kiss ta fisge hannunta ta gudu gida tana daga Masa hannu.
 Murmushi kawai yayi sannan ya ja motarsa ya tafi gida.
