         Khairat tana Shiga gida Ladi ta Fara Mata fada ya Ana gyaran jiki Zaki lalata Mana aiki kina yawo sannan kin Bari yazo Yana ta kalleki haka,Dole hanaki zanyi fita wajensa sai an daura aure, Dan lips dinta Khairat ta turo tare da cewa Haba Anty pls Mana karki wa bawan Allah Haka,ba lafiyayye bane,tausayinsa nake ji shi yasa Kika ga Ina kula dashi sosai,
  Kai Ladi ta jinjina tace sannu yaran zamani Allah shiryeki, Ameen Khairat tace.
   Washe gari kuwa Khairat tana zaune Text din Hunaif ya Fado wayarta Kan zaizo ya kaita wurin Umminsa,Khairat ta Masa reply da gaskiya kunya nake ji,tunda gida daya zamu zauna da ita ka Bari kawai idan anyi biki sai ta ganni, Dole fa kije Ummata ta ganki Taya za ayi biki ko fuskanki Bata sani ba,Jin kamar ransa ya baci Khairat tace yaushe zamuje to? Gobe ki shirya kawai Amma bazan zo ba Ina da aiki a Office zan turo Usman yazo ya dakko ki, ok Allah ya kaimu Khairat tace kawai ta kashe wayar tare da sanarwa Ladi, Ladi tace ba damuwa ai ga Sadiya kawarki ta unguwar Nan da take mugun sonki yarinyar kirki ce ki fada Mata ta shirya sai ta rakaki kuje tare ko? To Zan fada Mata cewar Khairat.

    Da dare taje har gidan su Sadiya,Sadiya Kyakyawa ce chocolate In Complexion gata Yar gayu ce sabo da Iyayenta suna da kudi,tunda taga Khairat take sonta,Khairat ce ke share ta shi yasa ta rage zuwa wajen Khairat,Tunda taga Khairat take murna ta Shiga nunawa Mama da Yan gidansu ga Kawarta Khairat,Bayan sun zauna Khairat tayi Kyau sai yabonta suke,Bayan Sun nutsu tare da Sadiya a bedroom,Khairat tace Sadiya gobe ki shirya 5pm Zaki rakani gidan Mijin da Zan aura,yace naje Umminsa ta damu ta ganni,Kawai ki shirya Driver dinsa zai zo ya dauke mu,Sadiya Jin gidan su Hunaif ne tana so taga haduwar gidansu Bayan Haka tana son Khairat da wuri ta Amince tare da Furta Allah ya kaimu.
   Washe gari kuwa Khairat tana zaune sai ga Usman ya kawo Mata rantsatsen lace na gani na fada me tsada dinkin Riga da Zani ne,Zanin me style idan ka daura kamar kasa Skert Red and Golden color,takalmi da jaka golden color tare da mayafi,suka dau wanka, Sadiya ce ta tsarawa Khairat kwalliya ba wata ta hauka me yawa ba,ko ayi ta lafta powder da wata gira duk ba ayi ba, Powder ta shafa sama sama sai eyeliner a saman Ido, sai jambaki red,dake Fara ce Khairat sai ta fito kamar wata Yar India,takalmin half shoe ne kamar wata Amarya,Sadiya Kuma Doguwar Riga tasa Atamfa green and black,takalmi da Yar Jakarta Black tare da mayafin,Usman Yana waje Yana jiransu.
   Suna Fitowa ya budewa Khairat mota ta Shiga ya rufe,Sadiya ta bude da kanta ta Shiga gefen Khairat.
  Suna Hira har Usman ake hirar sabo da Khairat Bata da wulakanci ta iya Muamula me kyau sai ka Shiga gonarta zata Rama.

    Tun daga unguwar zuwa layin da su Hunaif suke na daban ne a Abujan ma,Gidan da yafi kowanne kyau da tsaruwa suka ga Usman ya nufa,sun koma Yan kallo,gidane gari guda babu abinda Babu na Jin dadin rayuwa a gidan,Komai na daban ne,Babu abinda zaka gani a gidan kace ka taba ganin irinsa a Nigeria sai dai a film din turawa,gashi gidan part uku hudu ne,Part din Hunaif daban Wanda yafi ko Ina kyau Wanda a Nan Kuma zaisa Amarya,Sai Na Umminsa daban,Sai Na Baki Kuma,sai na Masu aiki,bangaren garden daban tsuntsaye iri iri,sweeming pool gasu  biyu daya a part din Hunaif yake ya ratsa a tsakiyar part dinsa,dayan Kuma Ana Umminsa, wurin parking motoci daban ga motoci na Alfarma sai ka zaba,Yan aiki ke zirga zirga kawai, flowers ko Ina Kore luf luf ga Grass carpet a garden,har Round abt ne a gidan tare da Dancing water Yana tsiri sama yana zubowa kasa ya koma ta kasan ya dawo,sannan akwai kida duk Wanda kake so idan kasa Haka ruwan zaina tsiri sama Yana rawa ga light iri iri a wajen,da dare ka rantse Rana ce,tsayawa fada muku tsaruwar gidan zai cinye lokaci,ya Gama haduwa karshen karshe an kashe Naira a gidan.
    
     Usman ne yayi musu iso zuwa part din Ummi sannan ya Kira Hunaif a waya ya kawo su Khairat,Ummi tana Palo Tasha wanka cikin Shadda brown tayi kyau na gaske sai kamshi take,kana kallonta kaga wacce hutu,Jin Dadi da Naira ya ratsata,Da faraa ta amsa Sallamar su Khairat Wanda dama tasan da zuwansu,Tunda taga Khairat tasan ma itace Amaryar Dan nata sabo da Yana Gaya Mata kyawun Khairat.
  Kunya Khairat take ji tayi kasa da Kai,suka zube a kasa tare da gyaisar da Ummi,ta amsa da sakin fuska sannan tace tashi ku zauna ai ke yata ce,Ina Khairat din? Sadiya ta nuna Khairat,Khairat tayi Shuru sai kunya take ji,Sadiya da Ummi kadai suke Hira,Khairat ta wani nutsu tayi Shuru sai kunyar Ummi take ji,Ummi ta kalleta tayi Murmushi,har ga Allah Tunda Hunaif yake aure Babu wacce tayi Mata irin Khairat duk da cewa ita da kanta ta nemawa Hunaif Aure,Khairat ce kadai Zabin Hunaif.
   Yan aiki ne suka dinga jera kayan ciye ciye na Alfarma,Ummi tace Bismillah fa,Ganin Khairat tana Jin kunyarta sai tace ina zuwa ta haura Sama ta Basu waje ko zasu Fi sakewa.  

    Ummi na tashi Khairat tace kaga Abinci kamar a Japan ko Korea,Suka yi dariya suna kus kus tare da Fara ci a nutse ba laifi sunci da Dan yawa Khairat ta dinga radawa Sadiya ke kadan zamuci fa ko so kike ace bamu Saba ba, ko mu Dan Kara kadan waccen green rice din nake Sha'awa Bari nayi sauri na ci cewar Sadiya,Khairat ta jawo farfesu tace Ni Bari na kurmushe wannan a ciki na, sai suka Fara ci da sauri Sadiya tana muyi sauri Kar a ganmu.
   Sai da Ummi ta tabbatar sunci sannan ta dawo wurinsu ta zauna, Khairat tana jansu da Hira sama sama,har take bawa Khairat labarin Yaranta Mohd da Meenal suna wurin kanwarta cikin Jin Dadi an sasu a private schl ma.
 Khairat Godiya tayi kunyar Ummi takeji tace bari zamu tafi gida Ummi Magrib ta kusa,Ummi tayi Murmushi baza ku Bari Hunaif ya dawo ba? yace fa gashi Nan ya zu daga Office ya wuce wurin Doctor dinsa.

    Kyale shi Ummi kawai cewar Sadiya,Katuwar Leda Ummi ta Mikawa Khairat,ta mikawa Sadiya ma Tata,Khairat taki karba Fafur,sai da Ummi tace kinci gidanku Ni ba Umminki bace,ai kamar uwa nake a wurinki,Sai lokacin Khairat ta karba suka yi Godiya har Mota Ummi ta rakasu Usman ya jasu suka tafi gida,Suna Fitowa Hunaif Yana shigowa da Mota da sauri,Khairat ta glass ta Shiga daga Masa hannu tana Murmushi,Horn ya musu tare da Murmushi Yana Daga Mata hannu shima.
   Bayan sun koma gida text din Hunaif ya Fado wayar Khairat,yace Ummi tana ban gajiya,Kin min laifi Kika tafi Baku jirani na dawo ba kin wani kwashi jiki kin tafi gida,Reply Khairat ta Masa da na gode, ai dare ne zaiyi shi yasa na kasa jiranka, Alright no prob ya tura mata.

     Biki Yana matsowa Babu Wanda yasan Hunaif zaiyi aure daga Dangin Mahaifinsa,Farouq frnd nasa,Ummi sai dangin Khairat, Mus'af ya cuci kansa ya tare a Hotel Akan Yana Jin Haushin Ummi yaki Zama a gidan Bai San me akeyi ba,Haka Hunaif Bai ko neme shi ba ganin Mus'af Yana wani share shi, Ana Haka Biki sai karatowa yake,Yayin da Amarya ta Sha uban gyara ta ko ina,kyau ba a magana,ga Ladi Bata fiye barinta tana zuwa wajen Hunaif ba,ya Dade baya ganin Khairat har ma ya rabu da ita ya Shiga harkarsa,saura sati biyu biki Farouq ya bugo hadadden iv na gani na fada kowa ya kalli Iv din yasan na masu kudi Ne,na ango daban na Amarya daban,Khairat nata iya Wedding Dinner aka sa on Saturday 5pm event daya zata yi ba wahalar da Kai.

    Hunaif Kuma Daurin Aure da Wedding Dinner aka sa a jiki kawai,Dinner Saturday,daurin aure Sunday Kuma a ranar za a Kai Amarya.

     dangin Khairat na Kauye zasu wahalar da Yan Daurin Aure sai suka ce su zauna kawai zasu zo gidan Kawu Sabiu ayi komai a Nan,Sai Hunaif yace Yana da Masauki za a Basu a cikin Abuja kowa ya zauna cikin Jin Dadi aci a Sha a daura aure a Kai Amarya sai su tafi kawai,dangin Khairat sai Godiya suke,Nan Kuma Sadiya kawar Khairat tace Dole suyi gayyar frnds da yawa,Sadiya ta dinga kaiwa kawayenta schl mate nata Iv,Haka Khairat ma Wanda ta sani na unguwar duk da ba wani kawaye gareta ba domin Bata Shiga harkar kowa Amma ba laifi duk wacce suke mutunci ta gayyaceta,Sadiya kuwa a kawayen nata ma idan Baki hadu ba baza ta gayyaceki ba.  
   Saura Sati daya biki Ummi ta aiki Yaron Hunaif Usman Kano ya kaiwa Iyayen Mus'af Iv, tare da Yan uwa da abokan azirki na ko Ina dage Nigeria,da Kuma na kasashen ketare an tura through social media,gidajen radio,tv Ana ta sanarwa ko Ina an San da bikin abinka da me kudi,Lefe kuwa kawar Ummi Hajiya Bilki Yar kirki itace Yar kasuwa tana zaga kasashen duniya tana business itace aka bawa kwangilar Hado lefe,size na Khairat kawai ake fada Mata,ta hada akwatu set biyu guda goma Sha shida,ko wacce Tasha Kaya na alfarma,Babu abinda Babu a lefen kowa ya gani sai ya koka ya tafi da santin Kaya.
   Ladi da kawayenta tare da Dangin Khairat wasu Mata da maza sunzo su Bakwai suka karbi lefe a gidan Ladi sannan suka koma sai Kuma biki,Ana ta tururuwar zuwa ganin lefe,Khairat kuwa takanas ta shirya ita da Sadiya Maman Sadiya ta Sa Driver ya kaisu Kano zasu gayyaci kawayen Khairat dake Kano Unguwar su Kawu,sannan zasu je wajen su Kawu Suma a gayyato su,Har sun tafi tasa Driver ya koma Office din Hunaif,waya ta Masa kana Ina pls?

    Office ya Bata amsa,gani nazo zamuyi Sallama Kano Zan tafi kaiwa su Kawu Iv,a mota ta bar Sadiya ta Shiga Office din Hunaif,sai kallonta yakeyi yanda ta canja Baki daya tayi shegen kyau,sai kamshi da sheki takeyi,fuska a tamke yace sai yanzu Zaki wani tafi Kano,ko tsoron Tsautsayin Amarya bakya ji? Dariya ya Bata tace au Amarya har Tsautsayi gareta? Usman ya nema yace yaje ya yiwa Khairat da Sadiya Booking din jirgi from Abuja to Kano, Khairat ta kalleshi kawai tace da ka barshi mun tafi,banza ya Mata ya dakko envelope Wanda kudi ne dubu dari cash ya Mika mata Wai tayi Hidima dasu,Farouq Yana Kano zai zo airport ya daukeku duk inda kuke so Driver din Farouq zai kaiku,number Farouq ya bawa Khairat tayi saving,sannan ya turawa Farouq ta Khairat.
  Godiya Khairat tayi,Usman yace an Gama komai ya mikawa Hunaif flight ticket nasu,Su Khairat Drivern su Sadiya Airport ya kaisu ya koma gida,Su Khairat sai Murna akeyi za a Shiga jirgi again.

    Su Kawu sun Iso Kano mota ta tsaya a kwanar dawaki Tasha,Dole suka sauka suka Shiga Mota zuwa cikin Kano,a Dangi suka sauka tare da Shiga Napep zuwa gida,sai Murna sukeyi,Tun a Lagos Kawu ya tsaya ya siyi manja jarka daya Babba,da Doya guda shida,Sai Talatu ta siyowa su Zainab kwakwar manja,da Coconut,Kawu yace ya kamata suyiwa yaran abin arziki sabo da Haka sai Talatu ta zabowa Soja 3quarter da singlet daya,Yan yaran ma Haka mazan kowa 3quarter da singlet,Rahinatu Kuma ta siya Mata Glass Baki faskeke da Riga wata tsangalalliya ita ta wuce gwiwa Amma Bata Kai kasa ba irin ta arna masu Talla a titi.
   Zainab kuwa ganin Yan Mata ce sai aka siya Mata t-shirt da Dan Skert me rawa,irin Wanda kana tafiya Yana rawa na masu gasa masara a titi, da an ga kayan an San wannan kayan sai talaka shi zai sa.
   
   Sabo da Haka da suka sauka a Kano Kawu dauke da jarkar manja,Talatu ta riko ghana must go sai Doyarsu etc a buhun bacco.
   a kofar gidansu Napep ya saukesu suka biya shi ya tafi,Don Kar a ganesu suji kunya sai Talatu ta rike Hannun Kawu kamar walkiya wukil suka fada cikin gida kamar Aljanu.
   Lokacin Zainab ta fito tana kwashe girkin da ta gama na Rana katsam ba zato taga Su Kawu sun Fado gida da gudu ba sallama har suna bigewa,Da kyar ta iya ganesu sabo da wahalar da suka sha, ihu ta saki da tsalle tare da ihu, Rahinatu ta fito,Soja da sauran Yara suka yo waje,ai gaba daya duk Doyin da Talatu ke Yi Basu ji ba suka rungumesu suna Ihu da murna.

   Bayan komai ya lafa Talatu ta kalli gida gaba daya ya canja yayi kyau sabo da Tsafta,Yara duk sun nutsu abin mamaki,Talatu tace ki fara bani labari me ya faru Bayan tafiyarmu,Nan Soja ya kwashe labari ya fadawa Talatu,yaran Nan sannu kunsha wahala kuyi hakuri da yanda muka raineku,bamu koya muku Abun Kirki ba,ku yafe mana mun gane kuskurenmu Allah ya kawo Khairat duk mu taru mu yafewa Juna,Suka hada baki wajen cewa Ameen,nanfa Talatu ta Fara Hawaye tana Basu labarin irin gwagwarmayyar da suka Sha tunda suka bar gida da niyya tafiyar Makkah, Rahinatu tace Khairat Bata da masaniyar Zaku Shiga wannan halin na tabbata .
   Nanfa aka dinga Hira sai da suka huta suka ci abinci suka Sha ruwa sannan Talatu ta Shiga toilet ta dinga dirje jikinta,Bayan ta Gama yin wanka fes sai ta samu ta dinga Brush ba ji ba gani har gawayi da gishiri ta hada ta goge,Kawu ma Haka. gida Rahma sai gasu Talatu Ana bacci.

   Su Zainab su dai abin mamaki ya Basu Jin su Kawu a Kenya sai abin ya Basu dariya,Amma Khairat ba karamar Yar iska bace,ga iyayensu Kamanninsu sun canja sabo da wahala,Abin dariya ma Bai kamasu ba sai da suka ga Kawu dauke da jarkar manja, ga Talatu da doya muku muku harda su kwakwar manja Yar Lagos,Sannan su 3qtr din da sauran tsarabar duk Babu na kirki.
   Yanda suka basu labarin wahalar da suka Sha sun tausaya musu matuka,Sannan abinda ya burgesu yanda su Kawu Suma suka gane gaskiya suka tuba har suna neman a Nemo Khairat su Bata hakuri sannan ta dawo gida su zauna tare lfy.

     Bayan kwanaki da dawowar Su Kawu sosai gida ya canja,rayuwa ta gyaru suna zaune lfy yayin da Soja ya dage da Sana'a Yana rike gidan,Mutanen Unguwa ana zaune lfy,duk tunaninsu Talatu sunje Makkah basusan Talatu boye Zancen tayi sabo da Makiya aka barsu kawai a sunje sun dawo,Yanzu ta karfi Kawu ya koma Alhaji Sabiu,Hajiya Talatu itama ake ta ce Mata,Basu San iyakarsu Niger,Kenya da Lagos ba.
  Talatu ta dage da Tsafta tsaf,komai ya canja Khairat kawai suke neman Hanyar ganinta.

    Talatu ta Kira Kawarta wacce ta Bata Khairat ta kaita Karuwanci Abuja, Talatu tace Khairat Dan Allah Ina kika kaita?ki dawo min da ita,Ni yanzu na tuba nabi Allah bazan sake zalinci ba,Kawar Talatu ta tamke fuska tace yo wa yasan inda take,wannan in Banda bala'i da ta jawo min ta jawowa Hajiya Baturiya me tayi Yar iskar yarinya marar mutunci,Talatu ta kalli Kawarta tare da cewa karki sake zaginta ai tayi min dai dai Khairat,To Bari kiji Talatu yarinyar Nan duk Saida ta jawo muka ci dukan tsiya da kwanaki a sail,Wani Senator da Baturiya ta hada Khairat dashi yarinyar Nan ta Masa aski ta tsaga Masa kirki shine yasa aka Kama Baturiya sannan aka kori Karuwan data ke Tarawa a gidanta kaf,ita Kuma Zancen da nake Miki an yankewa Baturiya hukuncin Shekara ashirin a gidan yari,muma da muke Kai Mata Yara anci tarar mu sannan munci duka daya Bayan daya Hajiya Baturiya tasa aka Nemo mu,Munsha wahala mu mun tuba,gidan Hajiya Baturiya ma Gomnati ta kwace ta rushe shi Baki daya yanzu Senetor din da kansa ya fara Gina katafaren masallaci a wurin.

   Wannan Yar taku ko sati hudu batayi ba a gidan Baturiya ta gudu,yarinyar tana da hankali ga addini sannan wayayya ce,Ta sanadiyyar Khairat gashi yaran Baturiya da dama sun shiryu sun koma gaban iyayensu,Duk aikin Senetor ne Wanda Khairat ta Masa aski, Mudassiru yanzu aikin Allah yakeyi,Ban San inda Khairat ta Shiga ba,Talatu tace to Allah dawo Mana da ita,Ameen sannan suka yi sallama Kawar tata ta tafi gida.
    Zainab tace ban San me yasa ba a samun Khairat a waya ba ko kadan da Kuma Kinga muna waya da ita,Kawu Yana daga dakinsa ya Furta Allah ya bayyana Mana Khairat mu ganta ko Dan mu roketa gafara ta yafe Mana.

    Misalin 12am jirgin su Khairat yayi landing a Kano,suna Fitowa da jakarsu a hannu Farouq already Yana jiransu a airport,gaisar dashi sukayi Yana tsokanar Khairat da Amaryar next wk suna dariya suka Shiga Motarsa Khairat na baya Sadiya na gaba,Kwatance tayi Masa na gidan Kawu ya kaisu har Kofar gidan,Zainab ta dawo daga Shago ta siyo Sabulun wanki zatayi kawai taga dalleliyar mota Yar gaske a kofar gidansu,Wata hadaddiyar kafa ta gani sanye da takalmi me tsada High hill kamar kafar Yar Shugaban kasa,gata Fara tas,Khairat ce ta fito Baki daya daga motar,da kyar Zainab ta gane Khairat ce sabo da yanda Khairat ta waye,ta goge,tayi kyau da kiba,ga sutura me tsada,da gani a hutu take,Sadiya ma ta fito zukekiya da ita,Zainab a Nan ta Raina kanta har kunyar kanta taji ma,Amma hakan Bai Hana ta Karasa wajen Khairat da gudu gudu ba,ta rungume Khairat tana murna,Khairat ma tayi missing nasu murna take,Amma tayi mamakin canjawar halayen Zainab,sannan duk taga ta lalace ba irin da ba,Farouq ta gaisar ya amsa da fara'a sannan sukayi Sallama da Khairat yace sai Sunyi waya idan tana bukatar wani Abu.
    Bayan yaja mota ya tafi Zainab tace Khairat wannan Kyakyawan saurayin fa? Ga kudi Ina kika sameshi ko shine saurayin da Zaki aura? Khairat tayi Murmushi tace bashi bane Wanda Zan Aura gobe zaizo da kansa shima ya gaida Kawu,Zainab ta daukar musu jakarsu tace ku zo mu shiga ciki.
  
    Talatu sai Khairat ta gani katsam itama ta rude da yanda taga Khairat ta canja hutu ya Kama jikinta,Haka dukkan Yan gidan ma,Soja kuwa tuni a ransa yaji Khairat tafi karfinsa ta wuce ajinsa,matar manya ce,Talatu tace Khairat Ina kika buya Ana ta nemanki ko a waya bama samunki,Jin Khairat tazo Kawu ya fito har Yana tuntube,A katuwar Tabarma suka zauna Baki daya,Bayan gaisuwa aka fara Hira Talatu tace Khairat kinci gidanku,kin bamu wahala,nanfa Talatu ta bawa Khairat labarin tun barin Khairat gida har zuwa Niger, Kenya,da Lagos, da irin wahalhalu da shiryuwa da suka yi,itama Khairat ta Basu labari tun daga barinta gidansu,gidan data kama haya,tsintar su Meenal, zuwa Abuja,Har Hunaif labarinsa da aurensu da zasuyi ta Basu labari kaf,sai Murna suke Taya Khairat,Kawu yace ki yafe Mana Khairat mun San bamu kyauta ba mun zalunce ki,Khairat tace wlh ban rikeku a Raina ba na yafe muku ko Mene ma har gadona duk na yafe muku Nima ku yafe min ban San zaku Sha wahala Haka ba,Talatu tace kaddara ce ba laifinki bane mun yafe,Nan fa aka yafi juna sannan aka ci gaba da hirar duniya,Kawu yace ai zamu je muma Taraba mu fara zumunci sannan mun hutar da Angwaye muma sai muje Abuja ayi bikin damu tunda ya bada masauki ai yayi ko,Khairat tace a'a Kawu ku zauna Yan Taraba sai suzo Kano a daura auren a gidan ubana kawai ayi biki da komai ai yafi mutunci,dama rashinku yasa za ayi a Abuja Amma yanzu ai bazan koma ba zama zanyi,Talatu tace a'a tunda Ladi na gyaraki ki koma can idan anyi Dinner an Gama Ana gobe Daurin aure sai kuzo a daura a dauki Amarya a Nan a kaiki ko?
   Sadiya tace hakane Kam Umma.amma dasu Zainab zamu tafi Abuja ayi Dinner dasu sai mu dawo Kano tare ko? Cewar Khairat,Zainab tace ko fa anko bamuyi ba,ai ga naku na siya muku kyauta,Nan Khairat ta bawa Talatu dinkunanta na biki kala uku lace,Atamfa,Shadda,a dinke dai dai Talatu,Zainab ma kala uku da takalmi da jaka kala biyu da mayafai,Haka Rahina ma same things,yaran ma kala Uku uku,Kawu ma shadda kala biyu da yard rantsatsu,Haka Soja ma,nanfa gida ya kacame da murna,Talatu tace Yar nan Ina kika samu kudi Haka? Khairat tace Hunaif Wanda ya taba zuwa gidan Nan kuka ce kun sanshi a tv da radio ai shine Mijin,Ihu suka dauka da tafi Suna Taya Khairat murna,Zainab tace Allah bamu I taku suka ce Ameen.
    Dubu Darin da Hunaif ya bawa Khairat ita ta dauka kacokam ta mikawa Kawu tace gashi na hidimar biki da zirga zirga Kar ace dangina sun Gaza.
   Talatu Nan aka fara lassafin yanda za a gudanar da biki lafiya.

   Khairat a ranar Yan kawayenta ta na unguwa da abokan arziki suka raba katin biki,Har na maza an bawa Kawu da Soja Suma suna gayyatar nasu,Haka Talatu ma an gayyaci danginta da kawayenta,sai su Zainab Masu tarin kawaye Yan gayu sun gayyatosu.
  Khairat ba Zama zirga zirga sukeyi tunda suka zo Kano tare dasu Zainab da Rahinatu,Zainab da Rahinatu har Talatu ta Basu kudin siyen kayan kwalliya na Mata iri iri sabo da suyi kyau kafin bikin yazo Kar abarsu a baya.
Saida Khairat suka Gama komai suka kwana daya sannan Hunaif yace ya fasa zuwa Yana da meeting idan sunzo daurin aure a hadu,Khairat waya a nuna musu lefenta dake gidan Ladi suna ta kallo sun haukace,Talatu tace a barshi acan a Kai Miki gidan miji Ana gobe za a Kai Amarya.
   Jin dadinsu ga Hunaif ya dauki nauyin komai cokali baza a kaiwa Khairat ba sai iya kayan sawa.

   Khairat kwanansu biyu suka Shiga jirgi suka koma Abuja aka ci gaba da shirye shiryen biki,Me magani fans sun Gama Shirin zuwa biki, AsmaBaffa fans club ma sun Gama shiryawa tsaf,House of Hausa Novels duk gasu Nan Ana ta shirye shiryen zuwa a bawa Ido Abinci.
  
    Mus'af yana ta zirga zirga daga Hotel zuwa Hotel ya daina saurar Hunaif sabo da bakin ciki,gashi Bai San ma Hunaif zaiyi aure ba,Yana can Yana kulle kullen ya za ayi Khairat ta Zama Matarsa,Sannan Yana so yaga Bayan Ummi da Hunaif,Yana Hawa Online ya fara chart kenan Yaga sanarwa ta ko Ina da Iv na auren Hunaif da Khairat,Mikewa yayi zumbur,Ya Fara sallallami da Gurnani,zuciyarsa kamar zata fasa Kirjinsa ta fito,Nan take kamanninsa ya canja,komai nasa ya canja kala,ransa ya dugunzuma,Ummansa ya Kira a waya Dan ya  tabbatar da gaskiyan abin,yace Umma an Aiko a kawo muku katin biki ko? Dama bazan samu zuwa Kano ba sai Ummi tace zata tura a kawo muku,Ae an kawo tun wancan satin ai Abu yayi kyau Haka ake so Hunaif zaiyi aure saura kaima ka dage ka Nemo Mana taka,Duf Mus'af ya kashe wayar baima Bari ya Karasa ji ba,a fili ya Furta na rantse da Allah da Hunaif ya auri Khairat gwara na Mutu,Dole ayi wacce za ayi Akan Hunaif ya auri Khairat Ni ban sameta ba gwara mutuwata,koma me zai faru ya faru wlh bazan kyaleshi Ina ji Ina gani ba, Nan Fa ya haukace Mus'af ya fito ya figi motarsa ya nufi gidan su Khairat Can Suleja Dama Already ya Dade da samo Address din.

    Khairat ta fito kenan zata Shiga gidan su Sadiya kawai sai taga Mota ta Sha gabanta tare da cin wawan birki,idon Mus'af jajir sabo da bacin Rai Yana huci ya fito ya tsaya a gabanta, Khairat ta kalleshi sama da kasa tace lfy dai ko? Da yatsa ya nunata wlh kinji na rantse Baki Isa kin auri Hunaif ba,Dani Kika Dace,duk abinda zanyi na raba Baku sai nayi ko zan tafi tsirara,gwara ma ki hakura da aurensa Ni ki aureni tun wuri,tun kafin na muku illa Baki daya,Shekeke Khairat ta kalleshi tayi Murmushin takaici tace kalleni tsaf nayi Kama da matarka? Dai dai lokacin kuma Hunaif yazo wurin Khairat zai kawo Mata kayan Dinner da zata sa,ya hango Mus'af a wurinta suna Hira,ran Hunaif ya baci,kishi ya taso Masa Duk da cewar ba Wai wani soyayya suke da Khairat ba,aurenta zaiyi Dan farin cikin Umminsa Amma ya tsani Yana kula mace wani ya kulata.
   Ransa ya baci tunaninsa Khairat hirar kirki suke da Mus'af.

   Lokacin Kuma Khairat tace ja tsumman rayuwarka Dattijo nafi karfinka wlh duk tuggunka sai dai ka rainawa wasu hankali ba Khairat ba,Kuma aure inshaallah anyi an Gama mutu ka raba Ni da Hunaif,da munyi Shawara da Kai? a Haka ka gammu tare ,inba shishigi da Hassada ba mene hadina da kai,wlh idan baka kiyayeni ba sai nasa an canja maka kamanni,Kai rayuwarka Hassada kawai ka iya?shi yasa baza ka taba ci gaba ba a duniya,Allah ya shiryeka,ka tuba ga Allah.
  Tana Gama fadin Haka tayi gaba ta danyi nisa ta juyo ta kalli Mus'af dake huci shi kadai tace Ni Khairat kwalelenka,babu rabonka a lafiyayyen jikina du na Hunaif ne.

    Hunaif ne ya karaso ransa a bace,Khairat tana ganinsa ta juyo da fara'a ai kuwa sai ya juya a fusace ya bude mota ya dakko kayan auren ya Mika Mata ransa babu annuri ya juya baice kala ba ya shige mota yaja a fusace ya bar wajen, Mus'af ma ya juya kamar zai tashi sama ya shige mota ya tafi shima.

   Khairat tsoro ya kamata yanda taga Hunaif Yana zarginta,cike da zullumi ta dauki ledar kayan ta shige gida kamar kwai ya fashe Mata a ciki,a ranta tana ta tunani to me tayiwa Hunaif Kuma?sai kawai ta fashe da kuka tana Mus'af ka cuceni tsinanne zai jawo ya fasa aurena.
   Kuka takeyi ba ji ba gani,Ladi tayi tayi ta fada Mata Amma Khairat taki fada,sai Kawai Ladi ta dauki waya ta Kira Hunaif Bugu daya ganin Ladi ce dama Yana da number ta ya daga suka gaisa a mutunce,Ladi tace tofa Ango Amarya kuka take min me ya sameta ne ko ka sani? Hunaif yace Ki kyaleta kawai Aunty ita tasan me tayi,Akan me zata tsaya da wani tasan an kusa Mana aure,ba damuwa ki kyaleta ai an kusa bikin idan anyi ai ba Wanda zata gani bare ta kulashi,Talatu tace hakane Kam,Amma Khairat ba halinta bane akwai Dalilin tsayawarta da koma waye,na sani Aunty shi yasa ma bance Mata komai ba,Ka Dan Lallasheta Dan Allah ko ta samu tayi bacci,to kawai Hunaif yace,Amma Bayan sun Gama wayar Bai ko nemi Khairat ba.
   
   Haka abin nasu ya kasance, Mus'af baya kula Hunaif,Hunaif ma haushinsa yake ji ya ganshi da Khairat dinsa suna zance ba Wanda ke kula wani ko a hanya suka hadu,Sannan Khairat ta rasa sukuni Bata ko saka Hunaif a idonta,Haka ya daina zuwa ba text ba waya,Amma duk abin shirye shiryen na auren Yana Aiko da Usman ya kawo Mata,ta Nan take Jin Dan sanyi tasan auren Yana Nan za ayishi .

   Yau biki saura Kwana daya a Fara,duk abinda ya Dace ayi anyi shi,Yan uwan Khairat suna gidan Kawu a Kano acan za a dauro aure,Nan Kuma su Khairat da Bangaren Hunaif suna Abuja za ayi Dinner gagaruma ta gani ta fada,an kama wuri tsaddaje Wanda sai me kudin gaske ke Kama irin wajen,dangin Uban Hunaif sun sauka Larabawa,Haka dangin Umma kaf,frnds na Hunaif kasa kasa duk sun sauka Kuma masauki a lafiyayyun Hotel aka musu,Ana ta baragaza da Naira,yayin da Zainab da Rahinatu sun sauka a gidan Ladi sai anyi Dinner zasu tafi Kano daura aure har Khairat.
    Abin ba acewa komai, Mus'af ya haukace sai Kora giya yakeyi a hotel kamar zai kashe kansa,Can kauyen Ummansa ya nemi wasu daya sani Kan a hadashi da malami zazzafa Wanda Sha yanzu magani yanzu yake son aikin,Amma Bai San ya rigada ya makara ba,Dole abinda Allah ya tsara sai ya faru boka ko Malam Bai Isa ya canja abinda Allah ya tsara ba.
    Meenal da Mohd sun Kara girma da wayo yanzu sun manta ma da wata Khairat sai kanwar Ummi suka sani,sabo da basu Dade tare da Khairat ba.

    Farouq shi yake komai ya shigewa Hunaif gaba ganin Hunaif Yana da lalura Bai wani Karasa warkewa ba,cutar mantuwarsa tana Nan Akan Khairat ne kadai baya manta Abu har gobe.
   Gidansu ma an canja Masa fasali ya Kara bada wani haduwar daban, Komai yaji Ras,Sabo da a Nan za a kawo Amarya sai Hunaif ya dauke Ummi ya canja Mata gida Wanda zata zauna anan ta sauki baki da Yan Uwa har a Gama biki sabo da Kar Yan biki su Bata gidan tun ba a kawo Amarya ba.

Kaifa kace baka da lokacin ganinsa kana da kamata Me zakayi da Mus'af,sannan ka bani labarin irin tuggun da yake hada maka na korar maka Mata sannan ya zage ya auresu.
    Mus'af ya mike a fusace wato Hunaif Kaine kasa tayi min Haka ko? Ni Musa'af Ni Baku Isa ku wulakantani ba wlh,Akan ka auri wannan Abun? Khairat ta bude Baki zatayi magana Hunaif ya jawota jikinsa tare da rungumeta zatayi magana ya hade bakin su wuri daya Yana tsotsa tun yanayi Don Kar ta sake yiwa Mus'af rashin kunya har ya koma na soyayya Bai ma San da wani Musa'af ba ya Gama rudewa,Khairat ma ta wani dage kafafu tare da sakalo wuyansa da hannayenta tana maida martani, a fili Mus'af Yace kun jawowa kanku,wlh na daina sonki yanzu fadan Makiya zai Fara,sai na wargazaku,Hunaif sama sama yaji Furucin Mus'af da yayi niyyar ya bashi hakuri Amma jin yace son Khairat dinsa yake sai yace Mus'af dama matar tawa Dana ke aure kake so? Mus'af ya juyo yace kwarai tun kafin aurenku Kuma wlh sai kasan Ni ka wulakanta,Hunaif yayi Murmushi yace Ina zuba Ido.
   Khairat Kuma tace a sannu sai nasa ka tsani kanka,sai na nuna ma Khairat ta daban ce,yanzu Hunaif ya auri ingantacciyar mace.
  Barin gidan yayi a fusace Yana faman Danna Horn a bude Masa Kofa,kafin Gateman ya bude Mus'af ya fito a motar ya samu Dattijo me gadi ya fesa Masa maruka har Uku sannan ya bude Gate da kansa yayi waje,daga Nan Bai tsaya ba sai kauyensu ya tafi sake sabon shiri yanda zai dawo ya tarwatsa Khairat da Hunaif tare da Ummi ya karasata.

   Tunda Musa'af ya fita su Khairat suke faman tsotsar lips din juna sai da kyar ta dawo Hayyacinta ta kwace kanta da kyar,suna Haki kamar Wanda sukayi Tseren gudu... Khairat ta Kalli Hunaif kunya ta kamata ta boye fuskarta cikin Cinyoyinta,Murmushi yayi me Sauti,ba tare data Dago ba tace yaushe Wai ya akayi na iya wannan Abun ne? Taya na koya? Hunaif yayi dariya ba shiri sannan yace me kikayi ya zauna kusa da ita,tace uhm....wannan Abun Mana Abun Yan Iska Nan da mukayi yanzu fa.
  Wai abun Yan iska See you abin masu aure ake cewa,Khairat ta Dago da kanta da sauri tace kai wlh sanda Zainab ta Zama Yar iska Bata da aure fa Naga suna ta Yi a mota da saurayinta,kaima watarana ka taba yimin kadan sannan yanzu zaka ce abun masu aure to harda samari da Yan Mata yanzu Yi sukeyi,Murmushi yayi Yana me dariya yace to uwar surutu ki Fadi gaskiya tsakani da Allah da Dadi ko ba Dadi? Khairat ta daga Kai cike da kunya tace dadinma harda na masifa,Wanda ka taba yi min kaga dai Dan kadan ne ko kafin muyi aure? Hunaif yace ae, tace to kullum sai nayi ta tunanowa.
    Ai Dan kina so nane shi yasa Kika ji Dadi,Khairat tace yaushe nace Ina sonka? Gashi kina min kallon so kuwa,Khairat tace to Kaine baka ganewa kallonfa kiyayya ne nake maka.
   Dariya Hunaif yayi suka ji Karar Door bell,Khairat tace maybe Musa'af ne Lallai watan cin ubansa ne ya tsaya kawai, Hunaif ya kalleta tare da furta karki sake Masa rashin kunya frnd Dina ne, Hmm Kai Wai ko kishina baka yine nifa yace Yana so,sanda ka ganshi a gidanmu wurina yazo zance zai kwace maka Ni Amma Kai kullum baka ganin laifinsa,to Ni Allah maganinsa zanyi,idan Kuma kaci gaba da biye Masa sai na koma na soshin kawai tunda Haka kake so,da sauri Hunaif ya kalleta Yana me hade fuska cikin fushi ya Furta ki soshi fa kika ce?kina matar tawa? To ba Haka kake so ba,Amma Kai kullum ka zama Namiji ka kasa sai kana wani sanyi,Shike Nan indai Zaki iya ki min maganinsa na Baki dama,Khairat ta kyalkyale da dariya tare da kwanciya a kafadar Hunaif tace harna gama kulla muguntar da Zan masa.  
   Mikewa Hunaif yayi Yana Murmushi a duniya komai Khairat tayi Kyau yake Mata,gata da iya Shagwaba,idan tana taba Masa ko hannu ne wani Dadi yake ji yanzu data kwanta a jikinsa kamar su dawwama a Haka,yau Kam ya rantse tare zasu kwana ko Bata zo inda yake ba zai je wurinta,ga iya Hira ga kuruciya,gata da abin dariya.

  Karar Bell suka sake ji,ya mike tare da daukan Khairat kamar jaririya ita kuwa tace kai Dadi Dan Shillani sama ka Cafe Ni naji yanda Yan jarirai ke ji,dariya yayi yace Anki din,A kafada ya sabata ya bude Kofa ya wangale sai ko sukayi Ido biyu da Ummi,da kanta ta kawo abincin ta rasa Yara,sannan gidan ba kowa duk maaikatan ta Basu hutu sabo da gajiyar Biki,sai taga ai gidan kusa ne ta tako a kafa sanye da Hijab ta kawo musu Abinci sabo da son Hunaif da Khairat da takeyi.
    Mutuwar tsaye sukayi,Yaji kunya,Khairat ma Haka da wuri ta dirga a kasa ta zube gwiwoyinta tare da sadda Kai kasa tana Ina kwana Ummi...farin ciki ya Kama Ummi ta samu Suruka ba irin sauran ba da kallon banza suke Mata,da fara'a suka gaisa,Hunaif ma ya gaisheta ta juya zata tafi,Khairat ta rude ga kunya tace dan Allah Ummi ki shugo ciki Ni ba ruwana kin ganshi Nan Ummi baya ji.

   Hunaif yace karya take Ummi laifinta ne,Ummi dariya ma suka Bata tace to Ni Ina ruwana dama abinci na kawo na tafi Kuma ta juya tayi tafiyarta tana musu Addua a ranta Allah ya zaunar dasu lfy etc.
     Khairat tace ka jawo min Jin kunya,gwalo ya Mata ta Rama itama tana Masa dukan Wasa ya dauki basket din suka koma ciki.

        Abinci ne gashi Nan iri iri na Alfarma Ummi ta shiryo shi,Dinning suka zauna,Khairat zata zuba komai daban daban,Hunaif yace Haka ake cin abinci Mata da miji? Shuru tayi tana murmushi har Tea a cup daya tal ta hada musu,tana Zama a kujerarta yace ba Haka akeyi ba,hannunta ya riko ta mike tsaye ya daura ta saman Cinyarsa,Khairat kunya ta rufe ta, kasa ko tari tayi,tana gani ya Shiga ci Yana Bata a Baki,dole ta hakura har suka Gama ci.
   Bari naje wurin Ummi cewar Hunaif, Khairat ta kalleshi tare da cewa pls ka tafi Dani idan ka tafi tsoro zanji,Ga Yan Aiki ko Ina sannan ma kince zakiyi gyare gyare Kinga sai ki zauna kiyi kafin na dawo,ok Khairat ta Furta tare da mikewa tsaye ta raka shi Compound Allah ya dawo da Kai lfy,Ameen ya Furta Yana Murmushin Jin dadin Adduar ta.

    Dawowa tayi ta fara gyaranta Shara,Mopping tare da wanke wanke ko ina ta gyarashi tsaf ya dauki kamashi,har ta Gama Hunaif Bai dawo ba,wayarta ta dauka tana dannawa har 1:30pm Shuru,Bayan tayi Sallah taji shugowar motarsa,dauke da Basket din Abinci ya shigo dashi daga wurin Ummi,Sallamar ta amsa Masa tare da karbar kayan hannunsa tana Sannu da zuwa? Ya Ummi? 

    Lfy take ya Furta Yana kallonta Yar yarinya da ita Wai shine ya aure ta,ita Kuma a ranta farin ciki takeyi ta Zama matar aure duk girman Namiji Bai wuce Matarsa ta aikeshi ba,yanzu yarinya da ita zata Iya Aiken Hunaif Kuma yaje,kanta taji ya Kara girma har wani yanga takeyi tace bari ya huta ta aikeshi ta gani zai je,Abinci suka ci tare, shi dai Hunaif Bai dauki Khairat wata me hankali ba ganin Shekarunta kadan,Kallonta yake kamar Kanwarsa sabanin Matan daya aura tsofaffun guzumaye, da kuma kalar macen da  yake so wacce tayi hankali 25yrs zuwa sama.

    Suna Gama cin Abinci Bayan sun huta Suna Kallon Tv Khairat ta Kira Hunaif tace Mijin Khairat? Dariya yayi ba tare da ya shirya ba sannan ya amsa da Naam ya akayi,Fari Tayi da Ido farrrr sai da zuciyar Hunaif ta buga sabo da abinda yaji,Khairat tace Ina zan samu Aya Jikakkiya ita nake so kaga dazu duk na aiki Yan aikin gidan Nan Amma Wai Basu samo ba,to ba sai ki hakura ba Ke bame ciki ba ki damu kanki, Khairat ta kalleshi tace to wa ya sani ko Ina da cikin jiya na sameshi,Jiya me mukayi da Zaki samu ciki Kuma daga jiya sai ciki? Dariya sukayi Baki daya ta riko Hannunsa tana Wasa da yatsunsa tace Dan Allah kaje da kanka ka siyo min Nan baya ne fa ba nisa,kaf layin Nan baza a samu wata Aya ba,Kawai wahalar Dani zakiyi,shike Nan tunda Ni baza a iya min abinda nake so ba ai shike Nan cewar Khairat.
   Har Sunyi Shuru suna kallo ta sake cewa yawwa na manta pad zaka siyo min bani da ko daya,Kuma dazu na fara kafin ya fara tsiyayowa ka Nemo min pad Kuma karka bawa kowa ya siyo, komai ku sai dai ayi muku sabo da sangarcewa Pad dai Kana bawa wani ya siyo zai Fara tunanin matarka ya wajen yake.
   Bakin ciki kike min Kar na Huta cewar Hunaif Yana Mikewa tsaye tare da taje sumarsa ya fita Yana cewa Bari na siyo Miki.
   Yana fita Khairat burinta ya cika ta aiki Namiji Kato kamar Hunaif me Naira ita Yar mitsila ta aikeshi Kuma ya tafi,Tsalle ta dira tare da fadawa saman kujera tana dariya, tare da Furta Kai Aure rahma ne,yanzu Ni na aiki Hunaif ai kuwa duk sati sai na aikeshi.

   Hunaif Bai Shiga Mota ba a kafa ya taka zuwa Wani Karamin kanti na layinsu,mutane sai kallonsa akeyi har yaje ya siyo pad da yawa ya kwaso Mata ya dawo,Yana shigowa taje gabansa tana murmushi a duniya halayen Hunaif Yana birgeta,ba ruwansa bashi da zafin Hali ko girman Kai,taji ya Kara wani birgeta ta fada jikinsa tare da rungumeshi,Kin bani wahala ai Dole ki rungumeni,Dariya tayi shima haka ya dauketa cak suka haura Sama,Bedroom dinsa ya kaita tare da kwantar da ita saman bed,ya fara kokarin cire Mata skert,ta Fara Wutsil Wutsil tana bashi hakuri yace ba kince period kike ba? Bari na sa miki pad din da kaina,Kara Khairat ta saki tana cewa karya nakeyi Dan Allah kayi hakuri.

    Bai saurareta ba ya zuge Zip Khairat ta Fara Hawaye da gaske zai kalle Mata tsaraici,ganin zata Masa Kuka ya gyara Mata skert dinta yace Quite na fasa,Hawayenta ta goge tare da gyara kwanciyarta saman Bed dinsa lafiyayye,Gefenta ya kwanta shima tare da lumshe Ido,Khairat ta riko hannunsa tana Jin tausayinsa sabo da cutarsa har yau Bai warke ba,da karfi ya jawota jikinsa tare da kwantar da ita saman Kirjinsa,Gemunsa ta shafa a hankali,muryarsa taji yace kina sonsa? Khairat tace sosai ma ai idan Namiji bashi da irinsa bazan so shi ba,to gashi Nan ai Ina dashi,Khairat ta Furta na Dade Ina sonsa nayi ta kallonka baka sani ba tana murmushi,Hannunta ya daura saman gemun yace Yi min susa nayi bacci,kitso ta Fara Masa a gemun tana ta jagwalgwala shi tana shinshinar kamshinsa sabo da Turaren gemun Hunaif na daban ne.

   Bacci ne ya kwasheshi kuwa.
wayar Khairat ce tayi Kara Sadiya Kawarta ce ke Kira,dagawa tayi tace Amarya Ana Shan Amarci an manta damu ko? Dariya Khairat tayi tace ana Shan Amarci Kam Alhmdllh ai ban taba sanin aure Haka yake da Niima ba sai yanzu,an barki a baya kiyi sauri ki Shiga daga ciki.

   Dariya Sadiya tayi tasan Khairat da shiririta Amma tace jiya bakuyi first Night ba? Sabo da idan kunyi Baki Isa kiyi Maganar aure da Dadi ba,Khairat tace nufinki Haka zai kalleni a samarin yanzu Baki da hankali wannan sirrinmu ne Allah ya Hana bankada sirrin me gida,Sadiya tayi shewa sannan tace Ina Angon? Bacci yakeyi kin ganshi kusa dani,Uhmm masoya cewar Sadiya, sun Dade suna Hira sannan suka Gama,Khairat ta Kira Ladi suka gaisa,ta Kira Kawu da Talatu sai zainab ta karshe.
   Zainab tace Amarya ya Jin Dadi? Alhmdllh muna Nan muna ji,Mijin Khairat ba karamin son Khairat dinsa yake ba cewar Khairat sun dade da Zainab sannan suka Gama wayar.

    Mus'af Bai tsaya ba sai a kauyensu ya nemi wani Dan Uwansu Saddiqu,Saddiqu suka tafa da Musa'af jikinsa futu futu ya dawo daga Gona Yana warin Rana,ya washe Baki Yana murna ganin Yana muamula da Dan birni Mus'af,Bai San Mus'af bashi da mutunciba, ba Dan Allah yake kulashi ba,Saddiqu yace ka shigo kenan yanzu muje wajen Malamin daga Nan sai mu je wurin sauran na samo maka zafafa guda biyar,kaga idan na wannan Bai ci ba Dole na wani zai ci su.
    Dariyar mugunta Mus'af ya saki Hhh sannan suka wuce wurin Malam na Farko Ana ce Masa Malam Mai tattabara,suna zuwa yayi dubansa na karya sannan ya dago ya kalli Musa'af yace kawo kudin Tattabara, Zan baka ita da dare misalin 1 na dare kaje gidan Abokin naka ka kira sunansa dana matar tasa sau Uku sannan ka saki tattabarar a gidan zata tashi sama,idan kayi Haka shike Nan da kansa zai saketa sannan bazai waiwayeta ba har abada.
    Farin ciki ya Kama Mus'af ya karba tare da bawa malamin kudade masu yawa suka tafi.
  Saddiqu yace ga Shawara Kar mu sake zuwa wurin wani muje a gwada wannan idan yayi shike Nan kaga mun San  yana yi sai mu rike shi hannu biyu Amma idan mukaje wajen wasu da yawa zamu rasa na waye yayi aiki na waye baiyi ba,Hunaif yace Haka ne idan wannan baiyi ba Zan dawo mu tafi wajen wani,Saddiqu yace daga Nan har Niger sai bukata ta biya zamu hakura suka sake tafawa sannan Musa'af ya Shiga Motarsa ya tafi ransa fari karrr.

    Amarya Khairat da dare sun wani cakare kamar zasu je party kowannensu naji da kyau ga daukan wanka,10pm taje tayi shirin bacci cikin wata Yar Riga me daukan hankalin da Namiji,da kadan ta rufe Mata bazaune hannunta irin na bra gata me silk pink color tayi kyau surar Nan ta fito ga cinyoyi a waje farare Kar lukuta lukuta, sai kamshi take na fitar hankali, Palo ta fito Hunaif ta iske har ya rigata yin wanka tare da Sa kayan bacci na maza rigace armless sharara sai wandonta 3qtr shima shara shara dashi,Khairat kasa kallonsa tayi sabo da komai gani akeyi ba kunya ba komai ko a jikinsa.
    Yana kallo ta kashe kallon da kayan wuta ta gyara ko Ina,tace bacci zaka yi,kallonta yayi kawai a fili yace zanyi maganinki,Khairat tace akan nayi maka gata ai duk cikin kula da lafiyar ka ne, Mikewa yayi tsaye tare da Furta Bari ki gani,da gudu ta kwashe, a hankali ya bita Bedroom din lokacin ta kwanta tana Danna wayarta,Gefenta ta nuna Masa da hannu tare da cewa kwanta a Nan tana murmushi,Ita Kam tausayi yake Bata sabo da rashin lafiyar dake damunsa ta mantuwa.
   Murmushinsa me tsada ya sakar Mata sannan ya dauketa sama sai dakinsa ya kaita can ya kwantar da ita tare da Haye Samanta Yana Kare Mata kallo.

    Mamakin kansa yakeyi me yasa yake son yarinya kamar Khairat? Sannan Abubuwa da yawa tafi masu shekaru da ilimi saninsu, yanda yake jinta a jininsa da kyar yake iya controlling kansa, Khairat kuwa tayi nisa a son Hunaif Danma Kar ta zubar da ajinta yasa take share shi sai ya sauke girman kansa da kansa sannan zata bashi mamaki,sai ta goge Masa hadda tare da tsotse Masa ruwan kansa,tunda taga alamar ya rainata kallon yarinya yake mata wacce Bata waye ba,sannan Bata da wani Ilmin Boko sai Dan kadan a sannu zata ganar dashi kurensa cewar ba Lallai me Degree bace ta waye ko tasan ta duniya,abinda ma masu Degree din aikin banza ne basa amfani da ilminsu.
    Tunanin da take ya katse Mata da Kwanciya a gefenta da yayi tare da rungumeta a jikinsa sosai,wata ajiyar zuciya ya sauke sabo da laushin jikin Khairat, ga Kamshinta ko Ina neat,Hannayenta tasa ta Kare kirjinta sabo da Babu Bra a jikinta Wai Kar ya taba Mata Bata shirya bashi ba.
     Khairat duk ta rude Bata Saba ba gashi tudun mazaunanta a daidai wurin Sandar girmansa,Wani cikin yanayi Hunaif ya tsinci kansa Wanda Bai taba ji ba a duniya,shi kadai ya fara Vibration,mutsu mutsu ya fara,Khairat ta kasa magana domin ta shige wani Hali kasala ta sauko mata.
   Ba Wanda yayi magana Shuru sukayi kowa da sake saken da yake a ransa,Hannayensa ya Sa da Niyyar ya rungumo kirjin Khairat Amma sai ta Kare tare da yin folding hannayenta ta Hana,a hankali ya rada Mata Mene Haka? Khairat cike da Shagwabarta da ta Kara yi Masa Illa tace Ni da kace min Yar yarinya ce me Kuma zaka ji a kirjina? Murmushi yayi yace yarinyace Mana Amma sai kayan aiki nufi na kenan fa, Kuma kin San da tsada na biya na samesu Sadakinki ai Sunyi tsada,Murmushi tayi me Sauti tace to Gori zaka min? A'a na Isa amma kin San Sadaki ne yasa har muka kasance a Haka ko? Khairat tace hakane,to me zaka ji ai shima fata ne ka taba kafafuna Mana,Hunaif yace Alright,a ransa Yana dariya yasan abinda zai Mata da kanta zata kyale Masa komai,Yace tunda kin yarda da kafar ma ai ta Isa,Khairat tace ae na yarda.

    A hankali ya Fara Mata tafiyar tsutsa a kafafunta tana kyalkyala dariya,Babban yatsan Kafarta ya Shiga tsotsa a hankali Yana lashe Mata tare da shafa tafin kafarta a hankali,Khairat tayi mukus ita tasan kawai me takeji,kafafunta yake shafawa har ya gangaro Cinyoyinta a hankali ya daga cinyartata a hankali  Yana Mata shafa da murza a hankali ta cikin yar rigar yaje saman Mazaunanta,Khairat jikinta kamar mazari sai rawa yake tana shidewa ta saki jikinta,Hannunsa ya cire tare da daurashi saman cikinta Yana shafawa ta saman rigarta silk, sama ya gangaro zuwa Saman kirjinta yabi ta kansu a hankali,Khairat ta shide tare da lumshe ido,Bata Kare da hannu ba sai ma gyara Masa da tayi ganin akwai duhu baya kallonta bare taji kunyarsa.

    Dukiyar Fulaninta yake murzawa a hankali cikin nutsuwa da kwarewa,Kissing nata zai Fara Khairat ta rigashi hade bakin nasu wuri daya tare da Sa tafin Hannayenta ta tallafo kumatunsa tana shafo Masa sajensa suna tsotse juna.
   Har ya raba Khairat da kayanta Bata sani ba,Shima du ya cire kayansa ba komai a jikinsu,Khairat da munafunci tuni ta daina kunyar ma ta koma Yi Masa salo daban daban Wanda shi dai Hunaif iya aurensa Babu wacce ta taba gwada Masa ko Rabin Haka,shi kadai yake musu komai suji Dadi shi basa Yi Masa,Khairat ta bashi mamakin yanda take jiyar dashi Dadi sabanin su Ameera da sai dai su kwanta shirim ba motsi.
   Yar mitsilar yarinya Amma sai sarrafashi takeyi,ta Gama mantar dashi komai sai Dadi take jiyar dashi.

    Baiyi niyyar kusantarta ba Amma yanzu Kam da kyar zai iya jurewa bazai iya ba,ta Gama kaishi karshe, Khairat a ranta kuwa so take ta ganar dashi itama fa wayayya ce ba girman kauye ba,sannan Wacce ta Mata gyaran Jiki ita ta Kara koyar da ita tare da fada Mata zafafan sirrika.
   Khairat yanzu itace ta koma saman Hunaif tare da Sa Masa Boobs dinta daya a Baki daya Kuma yasa hannu Yana Wasa dashi,kafafarta Kam ta sata tsakanin cinyoyinsa tana goga Masa Abubuwa, Hunaif sambatu ya fara Wanda Bai ma San Yana yi ba.

   Sai Albarka yake sawa Khairat taki karewa.
  Wani Idea ce ta fadowa Khairat da Me garan jiki ta fada Mata,sannan taji bakin wasu Matan aurenma,Sai watarana ta taba karbar wayar wani Almajiri zata Danna kawai ta kamo Bf da yawa a ciki taga yanda suke Sucking tsoro ya kamata ta bawa Almajiri wayarsa tare da Kare Masa zagi yasa ta kalli iskanci.

    Yau yayi Mata Rana sai ta zamo kasa ta Kama Hajiya Babba ta Fara Masa Socking an Dade ba a hadu ba Hunaif da wuri ma sai gashi yayi Releasing me yawan gaske,Yaji dadin da yafi Wanda ya taba kwanciyar aure dasu,farin ciki da nishadi ya wanzu a ransa,hankalinsa ya dawo jikinsa, Khairat Kuma da kanta ta jawo tissue ta goge Masa komai Allah yasa a saman rigarta ya kwanta Bai sani ba a jiki Kuma komai ya zuba,bed dinsu Bai baci ba.

   Mus'af takaicin Khairat ya hanashi bacci,ya kudurce niyarsa gobe da safe 11am zaije gidan Hunaif, yini guda zaiyi Dole dai yasan sai an kawo musu Abinci tunda yini zaiyi a gidan,anan zaiyi Amfani da damarsa wajen zubawa Hunaif maganin tsafinsa.

 Masu Sharhi kwana biyu banyi reply ba afwan karku gaji pls aiki yasha kaina.tnx all.... gaba daya na karanta Naga na ko waccenku.🥰🥰🥰👍🏻👍🏻💋😍😍💋..







         Washe gari sun Makara Babu Wanda ya farka da Asuba bacci suke kwasa gari yayi Rana tangararan Shuru Shuru Basu ko farka ba har 9am ta wuce,Bacci sukeyi ba ji ba gani,10am ta wuce sosai sannan Karar wayar Hunaif ya farkar dasu,Khairat Bata San Rana tayi ba cikin Bacci ta sake shigewa Jikin Hunaif tare da Kara lafewa,Kusan gaba daya jikinta Yana saman Hunaif,Hannu ya Mika tare da jawo wayarsa idonsa cike da bacci ko duba me kiran baiyi ba ya Daga tare da Kara wayar a kunnensa cike da Muryar bacci yace Hlo,Muryar Secretary nasa yaji yace Hlo Sir an Gama hada takardun Nan Signing naka ake bukata ya kamata ka shigo Office sharp sharp kayi signing,Tsaki yaja kadan tare da Furta bazan iya ko lekowa waje bare har naje wani Office Kawai Zan turo maka Usman ka bashi papers din ya kawo min nayi signing na bashi ya kawo maka,Ok sir ba damuwa.

   Khairat Bata San Waya akeyi ba tana magagin bacci tace uhmm...kamar safiya ce tayi? Kai muguna yanzu Sallar ma baza ka tasheni ba? Secretary yaji ogan nasa da Alama Love ake Sha ba Shiri ya kashe wayar, time ya kalla a wayar Hunaif yaga 10:40 Salati ya saki tare da direwa kasa tare da fadawa toilet da sauri Yayi Alwala,Khairat ma ta mike da kyar zata je toilet,Hunaif ya zaunar da ita tare da cewa kiyi hakuri na idar da sallah sai na kaiki Toilet, oh sabo da Kai kadai kake son ka Shiga Aljanna ko?No..no Ni ka kaini first sai ka dawo kayi sallar,Daukanta yayi tare da kaita toilet sannan ya dawo ya tayar da Sallah,Har ya idar yayi nisa da azkhar Khairat Bata fito ba,tana ciki tana faman gasa jikinta sannan tayi wanka tare da Brush,ta Shiga kwalawa Hunaif Kira Mugun Miji... dariya yayi tare da dakkota ta tayar da Sallah,Kafin ta idar da Sallah ya Kira Ummi a waya Kan ta bayar a kawo musu Breakfast Khairat Bata Jin Dadi.
   Cikin kankanin Lokaci sai ga Ummi ta Aiko Driver da karin safe.

   Hunaif duk ya rasa Inda zai saka Khairat komai shi yake mata har wanka da shiri sabo da ba karamin so yakewa Khairat ba,har mamakin kansa yakeyi, Mus'af kuwa zazzabi yau ya hanashi zuwa gidan Hunaif, Hunaif da kansa ya ciyar da Khairat,Sai Kuka take Masa,tana saman Bed Yana lallashinta taci abincin,Sai faman yarfe hannu takeyi tana Kuka ko hannunta ya taba sai ta saki Kara tace wayyo Ciwona.
   Tana Hawaye tace Dan Allah ka Kira min Sadiya kawata ko Aunty Ladi,Hunaif ya kalleta Yana danne Dariyarsa tare da Furta haba Sweetheart Dina so kike ki tona Mana sirrin aurenmu idan sun ganki a Haka kice musu me ya sameki? To...to ..ai...ai...Ni bazan...fada...musu komai ba..Ina da Hankali fa...Nasan Babu kyau a fada, ba Kaine kake ce min yarinya ban San komai ba,nayi maka kadan,kullum kana Raina min wayo,sai kace Ni yarinyace ban san duniya ba,sannan kana kallona marar Ilmi Akan banyi Degree ba,ko Secondary ban Gama,yanzu Kuma me za kayi da yarinya wacce Bata waye ba,kazo kayi ta min mugunta tun jiya kake azabtar Dani kana bani Wahala.
   Dariya ce ta Kwacewa Hunaif sabo da shi a cikin farin ciki yake yau,muryarsace ta katse Mata tunani da cewa kiyi Hakuri to ai Dan ban sani bane yanzu Kinga na gane Kuskurena akanki,Naga kinfiye min Yar 30yrs ma,sannan kinfi me Masters hankali da nutsuwa tare da dumbin ilmin shayar da me gida Zuma,sannan ga biyayya kina ji Dani kina lallabani to ai sai dai na godewa Allah na Kara rike Yar ficikata hannu biyu,Dariya Khairat ta saki tare da dukansa a kirji kadan da Wasa tace kagani ko nice ma Yar ficikar? Da Sauri Hunaif yace a'a Wasa nake Yar budurwa me kayan marmari ga back and Front wa ya Isa ya kirata ficika.

    Murmushi Khairat tayi tace to ka bani Wahala bazan Hakura naci abincin Nan ba sai ka siya min mota kasa an koya min Nima Ina tukawa, To ga sababbi na siyo guda Uku ciki ki zabi wacce ta Miki,Wasa nake fa ai idan kaji Mace na tuka mota da kanta to talakawa ne masu rufin asiri,kudi Bai Kai kudi ba,Ina da Mijina me kudin gaske ai nafi karfin na tuka kaina Nima Driver ne zai Jani na harde Ina karanta Jarida,sannan a bani Escort suna take min baya,Dariya Hunaif yayi tare da Mika Mata hannu suka tafa yace yarinya kin San Jin dadin duniya abinda kike so za ayi Miki.
   Har schl Zan saki kwana nan,Khairat ta Bata Rai Ni Allah bana son makarantar Nan Azo kullum Ina Kan hanya wata ta kwace min mijina,Ta Furta tana rufe Ido Wai kunya, ki kwantar da hankalinki Babu wacce zata kwace Miki Miji naki ne ke kadai.
  To shike nan ka sani a schl din.
      Sannan na Manta ban fada Miki ba na biyawa Kawu Da Umma(Talatu)  Makkah,tunda Kika sa suka hau motar Aljanu zuwa Kenya yanzu zasu shiga jirgin mutane,Khairat ta dinga dariya harda rike ciki tace gaskiya Ni shegiya ce sai ni wlh Allah ya bani baiwa,wa ya baka labari? Hunaif shima dariya yake yace Umma Talatu ce ga asarar hakora kin mata Ina zuwa gidan ta dinga bani labarinki tana ta min masifa tunda ni me kudi ne sai na biyata hakoranta an Sa Mata na roba,yanzu sai sun dawo daga Makkah zamu dakkota a sa Mata,Khairat tace yawwa Dan Allah Zan kalli wawulon bakin Talatu again kafin a sa mata hakoran wlh zamuyi missing nasu.

    Rai Khairat ta hade tare da cewa tunda kace kana son farin cikina to a barmin Bakin Talatu ba hakoran gaba Yana sani nishadi idan na kalleta Yana sani dariya,musamman idan Talatu zata ce Sisi ba hakoran Nan abin dariya sai kyal kyal har Hunaif Yana ta dariya yace wlh an cuci Kawu Dan anga Makaho ne aka bashi Talatu zukeke dashi,Shima zamu gwada kaishi magani wurin manyan malamai tunda ance Aljanu suka makatar dashi ko za a dace.

  Sai Ammar Soja na maidashi schl dinsa yanzu ya daura Daga Inda ya tsaya,na biya Masa schl fees din Baki daya,Sai Zainab itama na Gama komai ta koma Al-kalam University dake katsina da transcript nata ta Daura Daga Inda ta tsaya,Haka kannenku ma duk an maida su Secondary schl,Rahinatu tace bata sha'awar Karatun boko Daga Secondary aure zatayi Amma ita jari kawai take Bukata na Bata zata Fara kasuwanci.
    Farin ciki ya Kama Khairat tace na gode Allah ya Kara budi,Allah yasa kafi Haka Amma ko a waya Basu fada min ba,Ni nace Kar su fada Miki cewar Hunaif, na manta Aunty Ladi ma na biya Mata Makkah Sai jari Dana Kara Mata.
   Duk ta dalilina fa kayi musu ko? Hunaif ya daga Kai Khairat ta rungumeshi tare da zuba Masa Godiya,Lips dinsa ya Mika mata ya nuna Mata da yatsa a Nan Zata Masa kiss,ai kuwa tayi Masa kadan suna dariya tace ace dai irin bakin Talatu ne dani ya zaka ji a Kiss? dariya sukayi gaba daya,Hunaif yace ya zanyi ai ba Dole sai me kyau ba iyakaci idan nazo zanyi harka na danne kanki da filo tunda ba fuskar Zan ci ba,Dariya sukeyi cike da so da kauna.

      Yace Ba Godiya ba ki daure muyi Breakfast din Nan gashi Rana nayi,Karba tayi suka ci tare sannan ya Bata Magani Pain killer Tasha tare da kwanciya bacci ya kwasheta,Ummi ce ta Turo musu Me aikinta mace sabo da Gidan Hunaif Maza aka Bari masu 
Kula da Compound da flowers etc, Tana zuwa tace Ummi ce ta aikota ta gyara gidan,Hunaif ya shirya ya wuce gidan Ummi zasu gaisa kafin Khairat ta tashi,Me Aiki ce ta gyara ko Ina duk da cewa Gidan ba Dirty ko Ina Kal yake Amma Haka ta Kara gyara ko ina banda Dakin Hunaif Inda Khairat take kwance,tana gamawa ta tafi gida wurin Ummi.
   Can ta iske Hunaif ya tasa Ummi a gaba Lallai shi Pounded yam da miyar Kwai zata yiwa Khairat da Farfesun kaji.

    To naji zanyi muku sarkin naci cewar Ummi,Wai Khairat din me ya sameta ne haka nasan yarinyar da kokari,Hunaif yace malaria ce Ummi kawai, ai Tasha zazzabi me zafi jiya da dare Allah sarki baiwar Allah shi yasa nake sonta Ummi, Ummi rankwashi ta zubawa Hunaif tana marar kunya,Kara ya saki Yana shafa wurin, harga Allah Ummi yarda tayi da Zancen Hunaif Malaria ke damun Khairat sabo da yanda ya zake yake ta Bata labarin Karya.
   Yana kitchen ya zauna,Ummi na girkin daya sata,yake ta bawa Ummi labarin cutar Khairat,Yace Ummi jiya na tausaya mata Allah sarki gaskiya kasar Nan baza a taba ci gaba ba,Ummi tace wlh kuwa ai na lura kiyama haka Zata tsaya ba tare da Nigeria munci gaba ba,kullum mune koma baya a idon duniya,Hunaif yace ace common Malaria an kasa kawo karshenta a kasar Nan Allah yasa Ni ban Nigeria bane ba ruwana, Ummi tace Ina ji a radio suna babatun banza Wai rayuwar sauro data Zuma tare suke rayuwa idan aka kashe sauron kasar Nan shike Nan an daina samun Zuma a kasar Nan,masu noman Zuma shike Nan.

   Hunaif yace to Dan Zuma sai a shigo Mana da ita daga wata kasar, Ummi tayi dariya tare da cewa kasar Nan baza muyi wani hankali ba gwara ma a saki kudi kowa ya huta, dariya Hunaif yayi tare da Furta tunda ke Ummi danki me kudi ne ai Baki da matsala, mikewa yayi tare da yiwa Ummi Sallama tana cewa kayi mata sannu zuwa dare Zan shigo na dubata,ok Ummi Zan fada mata ya tafi gida.
    Khairat kuwa tuni ta gaji da bacci ta tashi ta gyara room din da Toilet sosai ko Ina ya dau kamshi itama ta fesa wanka tare da Kara gasa kanta sosai,maganin daya bata dazu yayi Mata magani sosai,kwalliya ta tsantsara sosai tasa doguwar rigar wani arnen Material Purpple and Maroon dinki ne na manyan Yara tasha kyau Bata daura dankwali ba Kawai gashinta me tsayi ta gyara tare da sakinsa kamar wata balarabiya Haka ta fito tana kamshi tako Ina.

    Karar motar Hunaif taji ya shigo gida, Murmushi ta saki ta fito Palo tare da Hakimcewa a lafiyayyar kujera 2seater, tana latsa wayarta kawai tana kallon wani Film a Mbc2, Hunaif ya bude Kofa tunaninsa bacci takeyi har yanzu baisan Khairat tayi wanka har da gabatar da Sallar Azahar ba sabo 1:20 tayi shi yasa tayi sallarta ta azahar, Yana shigowa Kamshinta Dana Palon ya bigi hancinsa ya hango Dan lips din Nan yasha jambaki maroon,Ido suka hada kunya Khairat taji shi Kuma Murmushi yake sakar Mata ya karosawa gabanta yayi tare da sauke gwiwowinsa kasa ya daura kansa Saman Cinyarta,Wayar ta ajiye gefe tare da nutsa yatsunta a lafiyayyar Sumar sa tana shafa gashinsa tace Ina kaje ko Wurin Ummi kaje? 

    Ae mana tace tana Miki sannu da jiki ya Bata amsa,Baki bude Khairat take kallonsa idonta ya ciko da hawaye yanzu Ummi ka fadawa cutar da nakeyi yanzu ya zanyi da kunya? Dagowa yayi ya kalleta yace ke kin fiye Saurin kuka yanzu,da ba Haka kike ba kin Zama raguwa Malaria fa nace na damunki,tace da dare zata zo dubaki,Malaria nace karki kiyi kuka,Yanzu naji zance harka sa hantar cikina ta kada,Matsoraciya kawai Allah ya shiryeki.
Ameen Khairat ta furta,lokacin Hunaif ya dawo saman Kujera tare da daura kansa a saman Albarkatun kirjinta Yana tambayarta kinyi Sallah ko? Ae tace nayi,Nima a masallaci na tsaya nayi,yanzu za a kawo Abinci nasan zakiji yunwa ko? Khairat tace duk tarkacen daka zuba Mana a kitchen komai gashi Nan na ci da Sha ai bazan ji yunwa ba Tunda ga kayan ciye ciye Nan iri iri suna Haka sai ga Yar aiki Ummi ta aikota da katon basket girke girke ne iri iri sai ka zaba masu dadin gaske.

   Khairat da dare sukayi waya dasu Talatu suna Bata labarin irin abin arzikin da Hunaif yayi musu sai Murna sukeyi,itama Khairat taji dadi sosai, Talatu tace ke Dan Ubanki Mijinki zai biyani Hakorana da kika rotse min su,Dariya Khairat tayi tace ai na hanashi,Uwaki Khairat zanzo Abuja ne ai wlh Dole sai ya biya, bashi Kika ci Masa.Harda kaimu mu Haye motar Aljanu to gashi jirgin sama zamu Dane,dariya ake tayi Ana Wasa da dariya gwanin sha'awa Kawu Yana cewa Allah yasa idona ya bude na Karo Miki kishiya Talatu budurwa Zan Aura suruki na zai min Aure,Khairat tace Ni Zan biya sadaki ma Kawu,Talatu ta waya ta Shiga aunawa Khairat zagi har Abuja zanzo naci ubanki Khairat,Ana ta dariya har su Zainab da Soja.
   Mus'af da wuri yaje asibiti akace Typoid ce dashi aka bashi Magunguna,Bayan kwana biyu ya warke Har Hunaif yaje duba shi da sukayi waya.
  Ranar kwana na Uku ne sai gashi yazo gidan Hunaif 11:30am lokacin Khairat tana kitchen taji maganganunsu da Hunaif,Fitowa tayi hannunta dauke da spoon tana ganin Musa'af ne da kyar ta gyada shi,tana fushi ta koma kitchen abinta,kamshin girkin Khairat ya cika Palon,sai Hadiyar yawu sukeyi suna Hira,Musa'af a ransa sai Jin haushi yakeyi Hunaif yayi dacen mace shi Bai samu ba.

     Suka je masallaci tare da Hunaif Bayan sun idar Liman ya fara wa'azi akan masu Hassada da irin azabar da Allah ya tanadar musu,sannan ya karanto Hassada iri iri kowacce da azabarta,Mus'af yayi mukus Yanaji  cikin Hassadar da aka lissafa Babu wacce Baya yin irinta,da sauran mugayen Halayensa, da cin Amanar da yayiwa Hunaif sai lokacin ya Shiga nazari da tunani,tsoro ya kamashi yasan halayensa Basu da kyau Amma yau tunatarwa tayi amfani domin yaji tsoron Allah ya shigeshi,Wanda sabo da Hassada! ba Halinsa bane neman malamai sai gashi Akan Hassada ya fada harkar shirka,sannan neman Mata da shaye shaye duk cin Amana da Hassada ya jefashi ciki,Babu Wanda Kuma yakewa Hassada sai Hunaif Wanda shine silar arzikinsa,Jin dadinsa Dana iyayensa,ga Hunaif Yana sonsa duk abinda yake Masa baya taba daga Kai ya kalleshi, sai Ummi yanda ta daukeshi da, tasan Bashi da Hali me kyau yanda yakewa danta data Fi kauna a duniya Abubuwa da yawa na cutarwa Amma Bata ko nuna Masa komai,Ga Matan Hunaif da ya Kora sannan ya auresu sai yanzu Nadama da tsoron Allah ya kama Mus'af yaga Sam Bai Dace da Zama abokin Hunaif ba,sannan da wanne Ido zai kalli Hunaif da Ummi ya Basu hakuri tare da fayyace musu Halayensa da mugayen abinda ya musu ba tare da sun sani ba, Liman Yana zazzaga waazi Mus'af Hawaye ya kwararo Masa,Liman yace wlh duk me Hassada bazai shiga Aljanna ba wannan fadar Allah ce,Allah yayiwa wani Niima kana bakin ciki ta gushe ta dawo kanka,ko kaima ka samu irinta, da me cin Amana da masu Shirka Ana bin malamai Akan biyan bukata ka manta Allah ke komai,Jama'a mu taru muyiwa kanmu fada,mu gyara halayenmu,Allah maji Rokon bayinsa ne, kofar tuba a bude take cewar liman bamu makara ba.

    Kuna ganin har yau akwai lokaci ko? Kullum Ana kiyama ta kusa tashi gani akeyi kamar Wasa ne,wasu har cewa suke akwai saura ai kaza Bai bayyana ba sai kaza ya bayyana,wlh inda akaci gaba komai ya Gama bayyana manya ne suka rage kawai,je kasashen ketare ku gani komai ya bayyana cewar liman,Yaci gaba Allah yayi alkawarin Annabi bazaiyi Shekara dubu biyu a kasa ba face an tashi kiyama,Annabi bazai Yi Shekara Dubu biyu ba a kasa za a tashi kiyama,jama'a nawa yayi saura? Yanzu Shekara nawa muke a shekarar musulunci? Wlh ya kamata mu farga muji tsoron Allah,Ana Wai Wai Wai kiyama ta kusa tashi wlh watarana Ana tashi za a ga Rana ta hudo ta yamma,a Haka Ana gani kamar Wasa ne za a bude Ido kofar tuba ta rufe wa yasan yaushe ne? Ba sallama ko fada mana za ayi ba sai dai kawai aga Rana ta fito ta yamma,kurunkus,daga Nan Kuma da manyan sun bayyana ba za a Kara kwanaki Mai tsayi ba,sai dai da safe wannan masifa ta danno,anjima da Rana kaza ya bayyana,da yamma wancan yazo,Haka dare ga wani ma, kafin kace me an tashi kiyama.

    Munanan ayyuka da muke aikatawa a kasa ya kamata kowa yayiwa kansa hisabi ya tuba ya daina tun da sauran lokaci,idan kana wani Abu marar kyau Kuma ka kasa dainawa Addua akeyi yaku alumma,kayi Addua kace Allah kasa na daina aikata maka laifi kaza kaza,Allah kasa na daina kaza Dana keyi,Allah ka yaye min, inshallah baza ka mutu ba Allah zai baka ikon dainawa ka tuba ka gyara halayenka.
   Fans Dan Allah a dage da Addua duk abinda muke aikatawa muka kasa dainawa a roki Allah yasa a daina Yi, inshallah Allah zai sa a daina,komai sai da Addua Allah zai baka sa'a.
    Liman yaci gaba da kawo Ayoyi da Hadisai Akan masu Hassada da shirka tare da cin Amana.

Yau Allah ya amsawa iyayen Mus'af adduarsu, tuni sun Dade sun Fahimci halayen dansu sai suka yi dabara suka dage Masa da Addua ba dare ba Rana Allah ya shiryeshi ya ganar dashi gaskiya,sun Dade sunayi sai yanzu Allah ya amsa,ko Dan uwanka,iyayenka,yaranka da miji etc duk Wanda ke Abu Bai Dace ba yan Uwa Addua ta Dace a dukufa Ana yiwa mutum Allah zai amsa.
   Mus'af Mikewa yayi Yana goge Hawaye Imani ya ratsa zuciyarsa,Hunaif yayi mamakin ganin Mus'af yau yaji wa'azi harda Hawaye, gida suka koma Mus'af ya kasa komai abincinma da kyar ya ci kadan,Hunaif ya tambayeshi lfy? Yace zazzabi yake ji yayi karya,Mikewa yayi yace zaije ganin Doctor,Har mota Hunaif ya rakashi Yana Masa sannnu,Mus'af Yana fita ya koma Hotel ya sharbi kuka Yana Rokon Allah gafara sai ya kwaso tarkacen da malamai suka bashi ya watsar dasu Baki daya,ya shirya kayansa ya bi jirgin yamma sai gidansu wurin iyayensu,Gaba daya ya rasa sukuni ya hargitse ya rasa taya zai roki Hunaif Gafara da Ummi.
   Kuka yake kullum a dakinsa ba dare ba Rana Yana tuba ga Allah,Ummansa ta rasa gane kansa me ya dameshi Oho,Haka Babansu ma,tambayar duniya sai yace ba komai,Ya rame sosai ya Kara wani haske,Wayoyinsa ma kaf kashewa yayi Babu Wanda ke samunsa,abubuwan daya aikata munana a rayuwar kawai yake tunawa Yana kuka da tuba ga Allah.
   Ganin Yan uwansa da iyayensa sun Shiga damuwa ganin halin da Mus'af yake ciki sai ya yanke Shawara gwara yaje ya fara neman yafiyar mutanen daya zalunta tun lokaci Bai kure Masa ba,tun suna raye, Matan Hunaif daya Fara aura ya nema ya Basu hakuri sabo da lokacin daya auresu ya wulakantasu ya sakesu ba bisa laifin komai ba,duk da cewa yasan sunwa Hunaif laifi Amma Dole dai ya nemi yafiyarsu,ta karshen Daya tafi wajenta Ameera ce wacce ya barta da ciki,sannan yarsa data Haifa Bai ko Santa ba,Ameera wani Dan Majalisar tarayya take aure, Ya nemeta har kasa ya duka tare da Bata hakuri,Ameera tayi Murmushi tace Allah ya min canji na Alkhairi na yafe maka,sannan cikin da ka barni dashi zafin abinda kayi min yasa na zubar da cikinka,da sauri Mus'af Yace Ina yata fa Meenal? Na jefar da ita wata baiwar Allah ta tsinceta ta raineta tsakani da Allah,ka godewa Allah Ina bibiyar rayuwar Meenal dita.
  
   Da sauri yace Dan darajar Allah Ameera wace ta tsinceta? Wlh ko wace sai na Bata abinda na Mallaka kaf,Murmushi Ameera tayi tace Lallai ka tuba Mus'af Allah ya yafe Mana Baki daya Meenal itace wacce Khairat matar Abokinka ta rike duk talaucinta a lokacin tasan darajar Dan Adam a kansu ta nemi aiki a Company naku Dan ta sata schl,ka dinga gana Mata azaba tare da yaran da take rikewa,ko ita bata San Yarka bace,ka dinga tsinewa Yar cikinka baka sani ba,tsinannun Yara etc,Kar tazo maka da Yara Office,duk Ina monitoring naka.
   Shi yasa ake so ko me mutum zaiyi yabi duniya a sannu,baka dauki Dan Adam a komai ba sabo da kana da dukiya.

   Mus'af yace to wannan yaron Kuma Dana ga Khairat dashi na waye? Wlh ban San na waye ba shima dai tsintarsa tayi, Meenal ce yarka kawai cewar Ameera tana zaro wayarta katuwa tare da nuna Masa Hotunan Meenal iri iri,ya karba ya tura Pics din a wayarsa Yana Jin Dadi,sannan yace to naji Ummi tace su Meenal suna katsina wurin kanwarta ta bar Mata su,ae Haka Zancen yake suna can cikin daula domin Mijin kanwar Ummi Hamshakin me kudi ne yaransa Biyu kacal shi yasa suke kaunar Yara.
    Bayan Sun Gama Magana da Ameera Mus'af mutanen Office yaransa da abokai tare da duk Wanda yasan ya batawa sai da ya nemi gafarar,Mutanen Company din sai mamaki sukeyi suna Jin Dadi yanzu Oga ya Zama mutumin kirki,kowa da abinda yake cewa,ga taimako yanzu kowa a mutunce suke Muamula ba zalinci da cuta,shi kanshi yanzu yafi Jin dadin rayuwarsa,Abu daya ne ya dameshi Bawa Hunaif da Ummi Hakuri tare da Khairat ya rasa ta inda zai iya Furta musu abinda ya aikata iri iri.
    Tunawa yayi da Yan Uwan Khairat su Zainab a Kano suke,Sunday da yamma ya figi motarsa tare da tafiya gidan,Wani yaro ya aika yace ya Kira Masa Zainab,Zainab fa yanzu Jin Dadi ya samu tayi kyau da haske Ana ta daukan wanka dama Ita Yar kwalliyace Bata yarda ta zauna kurar baya ba.

    Ta fito sanye da doguwar rigar Lace tayi kyau matuka tayi Yar kiba ko Ina a cike,tana kamshi,ganin Mus'af tayi tunanin Hunaif ya Aiko shi ko Khairat,a mutunce cike da ladabi suka gaisa, Mus'af da kyar ya daure ya bawa Zainab labarin irin abinda ya shukawa Hunaif da Ummi har Khairat,sannan da tuban da yayi da komai ya Bata labari kaf Babu abinda ya boye Mata,Zainab ta jinjina Hali irin Na Mus'af sai taga duk abinda ta aikata Ashe ita Yar Aljanna ce Akan Mus'af, Amma ya Bata Tausayi Kuma,sannan taji dadin tuba da yayi sannan Imani ya shigeshi,yace to yanzu me zan iya yi maka? Mus'af yace ki tayani Dan Allah muje Abuja tare na Basu hakuri,nasan Hunaif Yana matukar son Khairat idan Kika lallabata zata yafe min sannan zata sa Hunaif ya yafe min.

    Zainab tace to Allah ya taimakeka shekaran jiya muka Gama exam munyi hutun Sati biyu Zan sanarwa Iyayena cewar Khairat tana nemana sai muje,Farin ciki ya Kama Mus'af yace na gode sosai Nan sukayi sallama tare da exchange na number wayarsu.

   Washe gari Monday da yamma Mus'af da Zainab suka bi jirgin karfe biyar zuwa Abuja,Nan danan sai gasu a Abuja city,Gidan Ummi sukayi masauki Kar a takurawa Amarya da Ango.

  Ummi tayi mamakin ganin Zainab Yar Uwar Khairat da Mus'af,sai da suka huta tare da cin abinci,har dare Mus'af ya fita,Zainab ta samu Ummi a Bedroom dinta tana shirya Kaya,tiryan tiryan kamar yanda Mus'af ya Bata labari Haka ta bawa Ummi.
    Ummi batayi mamaki ba sabo da tasan za a rina,karshe Zainab tace Dan Allah Ummi wlh ya tuba yayi Nadama da gaske Imani ya shigeshi,kunyarku tasa ya kasa fada muku, Murmushi Ummi tayi tare da cewa ko Mai dadewar abu a duniya zaizo karshe,tun sanda Mus'af ya tafi Naga irin halin daya ke ciki na gane shiriya tazo Masa,na Dade da ganewa kawai Allah na barwa lamarin sabo da nasan mutum Bai Isa ya maka abinda Allah Bai maka ba,sannan Mata daya aura ban damu ba sakamakon dama Hunaif Ni na zabo Masa su Bai taba auren so ba sai a Kan Khairat,sannan Wanda ya aura bamu sani ba Basu da tarbiya Basu Dace da Zama Matan Hunaif ba.

    Zainab tace haka ne Ummi Dan Allah ku yafe Masa kisa Baki Hunaif ma su yafe Masa,nasan Hunaif zai yafe ba sai ma nayi magana ba sabo da shi me yafiya da hakuri ne Akan komai Allah ya yafe Mana Baki daya.
   Ameen Amma Khairat Kam nasan za a Kai ruwa rana da ita Bata ji nasan halinta cewar Zainab, Murmushi Ummi tayi tare da cewa a'a yata me hakuri ce wlh ga hankali karma ki fara cewa za asha wahala da ita.
   Dariya sukayi gaba daya. Da dare Mus'af ya dawo Yana bin bango Yana kunyar Ummi,Ummi tace gidanku Mus'af zo Nan Allah ma ana Masa laifi Yana yafewa,aini naji Dadi da Allah ya ganar da Kai gaskiya da wuri,Haka Ummi ta dinga Masa fada da Nasiha ba ji ba gani yayi mukus dashi.

    Washe gari da Yamma Zainab da Mus'af suka tafi gidan Khairat,Mus'af kirji na dukan uku uku.ko Hunaif zai yafe oho kun San me hakuri fa Bai iya fushi ba.

   Dariya sukeyi har Hunaif dake makale a jikin Khairat ya Kara kunnensa shima a wayar Yana Jin hirar Talatu.

    Washe gari da wuri Zainab da Mus'af suka bi jirgi tare da komawa Kano,Sai godewa Zainab yakeyi harda Mata shopping Kaya masu tsada ya Bata kudi sannan suka rabu ya ajiyeta a gidansu ya tafi.

   Bayan Sati biyu Ango da Amarya suna zaune lfy kullum Kara kaunar juna sukeyi,Ana Shan soyayya,yayin da Ladi ma tuni tana kasa Mai tsarki sai waya da sukeyi da Khairat,Sadiya da Farouq an Kai kudin aure an Sa ranar biki Nan da wata Uku, Zainab da Mus'af suna ta Shan soyayya ta kullu a tsakaninsu,ya samu dai dai shi kamar yanda yayi bariki a da ya tuba yanzu Haka Zainab ma da sonta ya kamashi itama tayi barinkinta ta tuba Allah ya zaba ya hada ba cuta ba cutarwa,bazai yuwu ka watsa kanka ba sannan kace kana so Allah ya baka kamili Wanda yaji tsoron Allah ya kame kansa ba,sannan mace ma baza ki watsa kanki ba sannan a Baki kamili ba,dai dai da abinda mutum ya aikata Haka za a bashi sai dai ko jarabta ta Allah mutum ba kamili ba Yana iya samun kamila Dan a jarabce shi,Haka mace ma kamila za a iya Bata tantiri wannan jarabta ce ta Allah.
  Aji tsoron Allah Ana duba gaba da baya mean yaran da za a Haifa naka ko na Yan uwa,da Kuma rayuwa ya karshenka zai zo.

    Yau Sunday da yamma lis Hunaif da Khairat suna main Palo suna buga game kamar Yara Sai hayaniya sukeyi gwanin Sha'awa kowa ya gansu sai sun birge mutum,Wata Yar macece Kyakyawa baza ta Wuce 25yrs ba,sanye take cikin Arabian Gown tayi rolling a kanta, Khairat data bude Mata kofa da fara'a ta karbeta,cike da mutuntawa ta kawo Mata Drinks da Abinci, Hunaif tuni ya Basu waje ya tafiyarsa daya Palon sama,Khairat tace ban ganeki ba Hajiya,Murmushi tayi sannan tace sunana Naja'atu nice tsohuwar matar Farouq daya taba aura muka rabu,sannan a rabuwarmu bashi da laifi ko kadan nice na biyewa duniya wajen harkala da tsofaffin samari na,Ina chat dasu,har maganganun batsa mukanyi da wasu Bayan Kuma Ina da aure, Khairat tace tab to yanzu Ni Mene nawa? Naja'atu tace ya sakeni ta Dalilin Haka sabo da lokacin ya min fada naki ji, sai Bayan ya sakeni na gane Ina da cikinsa.

     Bayan na Haifi Dana Namiji Wanda aka sa masa suna Farouq Sunan Babansa kenan sabo da Ina son Mijina,wani saurayina ya dinga zugani Bayan na yaye Farouq yace na kaiwa Ubansa dansa nazo ya aureni,Bayan na nemi Farouq Akan Maganar sai yace shi ba dansa bane Bai Amince ba nasan ya zanyi dashi,naji haushi sabo da ban taba bawa wani kaina ba,Amma abinda nakeyi a chart shi ya jawo Farouq yake zargina,saurayina shi ya dinga zugani naje na jefar da yaron,lokacin kina Unguwar da Zama,Kika daukeshi,duk wannan labarin ban sani ba Mus'af ne yaje shekaran jiya har gidanmu yace yaga me kama da Farouq naje na duba ko Dana nane,lokacin Ina cikin Nadama,sabo da Wanda ya zugani Yana aurena ko Shekara banyi ba yayi min duka ya sakeni,sannan Nadama ta sameni na gane kurena,dama Kuma tunda na jefar da yarona ban Kara samun kwanciyar hankali ba a duniya.
   Nayi Dana sani na tuba sannan na gyara halayena Ina matukar gode Miki Dan Allah ki taimaka Naga yaron Nan ko shine Dana?

    Khairat tace Wai me muka dauki duniya ne? Waya ta dauko tare da nuna Mata hoton Mohd,Hawaye ta Fara tana shine Dana ne,sai yanzu ma ita kanta Khairat taga kamarsu da Farouq,Kiran Hunaif tayi tana Honey..ya fito yace lfy? Khairat tace matar Farouq ce fa, Hunaif yace tsohuwar Matarsa dai ai na santa,Nan Khairat ta bashi labari yace sai itama taje wurin Ummi a Basu yaransu kawai.

   Address suka Bata na Ummi taje ta roki Ummi,Ummi tace sanda kika jefar dashi me kika ce a gida? Naja tace karya nayi nace munje kasuwa ya bace,Kanwarta Ummi ta Kira ta umarce ta masu Yara fa sun bayyana a Basu yaransu,Haka bayan sati daya Farouq ya Riga Naja'atu zuwa ya karbo dansa Farouq Wanda ake ce Masa Mohd, Mus'af kuwa yace ya barwa kanwar Ummi halak malak taci gaba da rike Masa ita,sunji dadin Karar da Mus'af yayi,Farouq kuma Mamansa ya bawa sabo da shi kadai ta Haifa a duniya ta samu yaro,Ummi tace ya kyauta.
Naja'atu sai kuka takeyi uba ya kwace dansa ta cuci kanta data jefar dashi da Bata aikata ba da tuni danta na wajenta.
   Gata ba Miji ba da shike Nan sai aci gaba da tilo Mata wanke wanken gida tanayi da shara,ga tsangwamar kannai da dangi sun isheta.

   Khairat tace ai gashi Nan yanzu bata a tsuntsu Bata a tarko,gashi an kusa bikin Farouq da Sadiya kawata,Allah ya kyauta cewar Ummi, Mus'af shi dama Zainab din ya aura kawai ya huta,ai Suna Soyayya da Zainab yanzu ta Amince zata aureshi cewar Khairat,Su Umma suna dawowa daga Saudiya cikin satin Nan za akai kudin aure, Alhmdllh hakan yayi ai cewar Ummi.

    Khairat tace to inshallah zanyi Ummi Bari na tafi to sai naje nayi Masa,Ummi tace a'a Banda yau ai tunda kinzo zauna a Nan zanyi na bayar a Kai Masa,Ummi ta Shiga Kitchen Khairat ta bita tare da nacewa Dole sai ta Taya Ummi aikin,tare sukayi girke girke lafiyayyu na Yan gayu tare da shiryawa a katon Basket cikin Flasks na Alfarma Driver ya kaiwa Hunaif har Office Wai inji Matarsa Khairat,Farin ciki ya Kama Hunaif,Tare da wasu Maaikatan dake karkashinsa suka ci suna ta Santi yanzu suka San Oga yayi aure sunci sun koshi ba tare da kwandalarsu tayi Ciwon Kai ba girki me dadin da yafi na Restaurant,Allah yasa Hunaif baya kyankyamin mutane Wai Dan ya fika kudi ko kana karkashinsa yace bazai ci Abinci da Kai ba,ko ya nuna maka kyama shi Sam ba Halinsa bane,shi yasa ba dai kaji Ana zaginsa ba sai dai yabonsa ko Ina.

   Khairat sai cewa takeyi muyi sauri Sadiya,kofa abinci banyi Masa ba,da kyar ta Bari aka Karasa siyayya suka zaba sai waya suke da Hunaif ta soyayya,Sadiya tace jarababbiya an Gama muje na sauke ki a gida.

    Koda biki yazo kullum Hunaif da kansa yake Khairat ya koma ya dakkota,Gashi Abokin Ango Ana ta hada hada,Anyi rantsatsiyar Dinner sannan aka Kai Amarya Kano tsararen gidan Amarya,Hunaif dai Da Khairat Basu je Kano ba sunce sai anzo bikin Zainab zasuje su gani.
    Khairat murna takeyi sun kusa tafiya Kano bikin Zainab,sai da bikin ya rage saura kwana daya a Fara suka shirya da Hunaif suka bi jirgi sai Kano State.

     Zainab an Gama shirya komai domin Mus'af komai ya zuba a gidansa shima harkar girma kenan,Zainab ansha gyaran jiki lungu da sako tayi matukar kyau,Talatu Tasha murnar ganin Khairat da mijinta,Kawu ma Haka,Khairat sai kallon gidan takeyi gaba daya sabon gini aka canja,ko Ina tiles da tiles,Zainab tace ai Kawu da Ammar Soja ne sukayi hadin gwiwa suka gyara gidan,sabo da Ammar Yana karatu Kuma ya bude katon kanti yasa yaro a kantin Kuma Hunaif ne ya bashi jarin.
    Hunaif kuwa tuni Ango Mus'af yazo ya daukeshi sun wuce Hotel da suke angwancinsu a Nan ake saukar frnds na nesa kaji masu abin.
    Khairat tana cikin Yan Mata da ita ake komai,Hunaif ko a waya baya samunta ta samu dangi da Yan Mata ta shareshi kawai,Friday yau za ayi party,Tun safe Hunaif yake neman Khairat a waya tana ta ringing Bata dauka ta barta cikin jaka sabo da Lalle aka tsantsara Mata,sannan suka je Saloon gashi yaci kudi, Rahinatu ce taji Karar wayar yayi yawa ta daga tace ai sun tafi gidan kwalliya da Amarya,daga can zasu wuce Wurin event din.

     5pm aka sa Amma sai 7pm aka fara,Khairat kyan data yi ba a magana,Hunaif ma Haka kamar shine Angon,Khairat ta fito a motar Farouq kenan tare da Sadiya Kawarta sai ga Hunaif yazo a lafiyayyar motarsa.
   Tasan tayi laifi sabo da tasan zai nemeta ta kyale wayarta,Wurinsa ta karasa,Ya fito Yana ganinta bacin ransa ya gushe,yaji sanyi a ransa,Bai Mata fada ba ya rike Hannunta suka tafi ciki,kida na tashi I'm sorry na Shiga busy ne ta Furta masa, kiyaye gaba kawai cewar Hunaif.

    Ansha rawa,an zubar da Naira,anci ansha Party yayi matuka,washe gari aka daura aure tare da Kai Amarya,Khairat ta zaga mutanen arziki na Kano Wanda suke mutunci da,taje gidan Sadiya,washe gari kuwa Hunaif yace tafiya gida zasuyi,Talatu itama ta Basu tsarabar makkah,Rahinatu ma ta samu Mijin aurenta wani matashin Doctor ne Amma Bai Gama gini ba yace a jirashi kadan.
   Bayan Khairat sun koma gida da Sati daya ta Fara Laulayin ciki,zazzabi da Amai,sai da sukaje asibiti aka Bata Magunguna sannan Doctor ya Basu takardar cikinta Dan wata biyu.
   Sunsha Murna,Haka Ummi ma sai Murna,Lokacin Kuma Hunaif ya maida Khairat schl ta zana waec da Neco sannan ya dakko Mata Irin copper me Mata karatu a gida.

    Exam na Fitowa ya sata a private University me tsadar gaske a Abuja,Driver ke kaita ya dakko ta,watarana har Escort dinsa yake bata sabo da kula da lafiyarta,tuni makaranta ke tsoron Khairat matar Hamshaki ce.
   Ta Kara gogewa da wayewa,ga frnds tayi wasu yaran mutunci.

Talatu ta Kama Sana'a sosai take Business na siyar da atamfofi,dasu Inner wears.

      Yau Khairat tana da schl Gashi ta tashi Bata da lfy sama sama take zazzabi,Hunaif ya kalleta tana rawar sanyi,ji yake kamar ya dawo da Ciwon jikinsa,ga ciki Dan ma Allah ya taimaketa Bata laulayi me zafi,tana jikinsa duk zafin da jikinta yayi Amma Baya jinsa,ta lafiyarta yake yace pls a hakura da Schl yau sai muje Hospital a dubaki tare da Baki Magunguna,Khairat fafur tace Ni Allah sai naje schl Muna da Test,Ba yanda Hunaif baiyi ba har ta bashi haushi yace to shike Nan sai kin dawo, Paracetamol ta Sha Kawai ta shirya Yana kallonta har kitchen ta shiga a Haka tana aiki tana kwanciya Amma sai da tayi kokarin hada musu chips da tea lafiyayye,Shi kuwa fushi yakeyi yace bazai ci ba,a hankali tace sabo da Kai fa nayi Dan Allah kaci,ga zazzabi na damunta ta saki masa kukan Shagwabarta data saba. 

     tausayi ta bashi yaci abincin sannan tace tunda Office zaka wuce ka saukeni a schl din,Tare suka fita yau shike driving da kansa ya kaita har schl,ya bude ya fita sannan ya zagayo tare da bude Mata kofa ta fito a hankali,Sai kallonsu akeyi anga Kyau na gugan Kyau,Frnds din Khairat da sauri suka zo wajenta Dan su kalle Mata miji sabo da sau daya suka taba ganin Hunaif,Dan munafunci suka fake da gaidashi sai kallonsa suke kamar zasu cinyeshi sunga Handsome.

   Khairat tana kallonsu ta Bata fuska kishin mijinta ya rufeta ta riko Hannunsa tana Wasa da yatsunsa,Rungumeta yayi ta dage kafafunta yace basai kin wahalar da kanki ba,Tsaiwarta ta daidaita ta tsaya cak Hannayenta Yana kugunsa ta rike,rankwafowa yayi tare da Kara Mata kunnensa a kunnenta yace fada min Abinda kike so naji, a kunne ta rada Masa pls ka turo Driver ya daukeni Karka dawo schl dinnan wannan jiba kowa sai kalle min Kai sukeyi.
   Murmushin Jin Dadi ya saki sannan shima ya rada Mata yanda Baki da lfy Babu Wanda Zan Bari yazo daukanki da kaina zanzo.
   Shagwaba ta Fara ajiye Masa Amma yace shi zai dawo,Fushi tayi tace da frnds din kuzo mu wuce tana harararsu Cike da kishin mijinta.
  Mota ya koma Yana Murmushi ya bar schl din.
   Bayan Sunyi Test dinsu sun fito zazzabi ya sake Rufe Khairat ta dinga sheka Amai a Bayan Class Frnds nata ne suka dauki wayarta tare da Kiran Hunaif cewar yazo ya dauki Khairat tana ta Amai,yasan zaa rina,Minti kadan yazo tare da daukanta ya wuce da ita Hospital har ruwa aka Kara Mata sannan aka Basu Magunguna suka dawo gida.
   Ya dinga Mata fada,kinga irin taurin kanki ko,an fada Miki magana bakya ji,ai Gashi Nan kinsha wahala a banza,Ana tausayinki ke bakya Jin tausayin kanki, ai Ni Dadi ma naji da Haka ta sameki Nan gaba sai ki kiyaye,Khairat tace Dama ai baka so na,Ni nace bana sonki? Ae Mana Gashi kace Allah ya Kara,dama Ciwon ya kashe Ni,sannan sai zagin iyayena kakeyi Akan naje schl,Dariya Hunaif yayi yace sharri Zaki min? Yaushe na zagi Iyayenki? Haka kawai Khairat ta kalawa Hunaif Sharri Wai ya zagi iyayenta Akan taje schl, taci gaba da cewa indai akan ka sani schl ne kake min Gori to ga schl dinka Nan na daina zuwa,sai ka Kai wacce kake so.

   Ummi da tazo dubiya fada ta samesu suna tayi  Ita Khairat Dole Hunaif Wai zaginta yayi taji Haushi,Ummi tace Kai mene Haka?
