   Hunaif yace Ummi wlh karya take min,yanzu ko ya akayi Abu sai ta canja min magana tana takalata da fada,kullum neman fada takeyi.
   Ummi tace Khairat jeki shirya mu tafi Gidana yau acan Zaki yini ki bar Masa gidan ya cinye abinsa.
   Ta mike da murna tace ba sai ka cinye gidanka ba Bari na shirya Dan Allah Ummi zanyi sati daya,to Kawai Ummi tace mata,Khairat tana tafiya Shirin bin Ummi,Nan Ummi ta fayyacewa Hunaif halayen wasu masu ciki na takalar Miji fada,idan suna da ciki an dinga tashin hankali kenan,Suma ba kowanne ciki ba,Amma Ana samun Mata da yawa masu laulayi na neman fada,yanzu sai su canja Magana ayi ta fada.
   Hunaif yace Ummi gwara da kika fada min nayi tunanin canja Hali tayi,ko Frnds ke zugata,kullum Bata Bari ayi zaman lfy sai ta San yanda tayi ta kaini bango tunda na yanzu na gane to na daina biye Mata.

    Khairat harda shirya kayanta tabi Ummi suka tafi,Ummi tace da Hunaif ka kyaleta zata nemeka ne,Khairat Kuma ganin tabi Ummi Amma Bai nuna ya damu da ita ba ko hanata baiyi ba,sai tace ai dama ya daina sonta,dama maza Haka suke munafukai Da kin samu ciki sai su daina sonka su tsaneka,suna ma kallon ka tsufa, ita kadai ta Gama tunaninta sai sake sake takeyi harda suka je gidan Ummi ta Hana zuciyarta sukuni, Hunaif Kam shi bazai iya Zama ba Khairat ba ko Mai fadan da zasuyi yafi son Abarsa kusa dashi,Amma Dole ya Dan daure da abinda Ummi tace.
  Khairat Kam jira take taga kiran Hunaif ko a waya Amma Shuru,Bai zo ya ganta ba,wani masifa ce da bakin ciki ke taso Mata a ranta kawai so take ta ganshi.

   Wasa Wasa Har dare Shuru,sai ta tura Masa text ka manta Dani ko? Dama baka damu Dani ba na sani.
   Shuru baiyi replying ba,sai ta samu Ummi tace nayi mantuwa a gida Ummi zanje na dauko,Ummi ta ganeta sai tace sai kin dawo.
   Da sauri ta zurma Hijab fiya fiya tana sauri Hunaif sai ganinta yayi ta banko kofa a fusace ta shigo,Yana Palo Yana aiki a system,ta kalleshi kawai tace wato Dan cikin ba ajinka yake ba shine kake wulakantani kullum,Hunaif ya kalleta farin ciki ya kamashi ta kawo kanta,yace me nayi Kuma sabo da Allah?
    Idan Ban Sha fiya-fiya na Mutu Baki daya ba kace ba sunana Khairat ba.
   Jikinsa ya jawota ta zauna ya shafa cikinta yace gaskiya ko waye wannan Dan nawa Masifaffe za a Haifa,Yana magana ita Kuma sai kuka takeyi ta kalleshi tace Allah sai na kyastawa kaina wuta na kone du, dan Allah a cire min cikin Nan na huta.

   Akan me za a cire? Hunaif ya tambaya,Sabo da ya jawo ka tsaneni yanzu ka daina so na,baka damu Dani ba,sai kayi ta min fada kana zagina, Hunaif sai ta bashi tausayi ya Shiga Lallashinta Yana lallabata tare da Furta Mata dadan kalamai Yana yabonta,Yana kodata,sai lokacin ya samu ta daina fushin zuciyarta tayi sanyi yace idan cikine ya dameki za a cire ki huta kwana Nan,Amma ki daina fada kinji? Ki daina masifa, Khairat tace ai na daina bazan Kara ba.
   Nan ya dauketa suka koma Bedroom ya Shiga jiyar da ita Dadi ta Hanyar Sunna, sosai suka jiyar da juna Dadi,Wanda baza su manta da wannan Rana ba.

   Washe gari kuwa tunda Khairat taje schl ta dawo da fushi ta dawo gida ta Gama tunaninta tace sabo da baya kauna ta Akan nace a cire min ciki shine ya yarda za a cire min, Dana Wanda nafi so za a kasheshi Lallai Hunaif baya kaunata Bari ya dawo daga Office.
 Kasa jurewa tayi sai da ta turawa Hunaif text kamar haka:
     dama nace baka kaunata gashi Nan Akan nace a cire min ciki gudan jinina ka yarda.

   Tunda Hunaif yaga text abin ya bashi dariya sannan ya San Yana komawa Gida to fa akwai daru,sai daya tanaji kalmomin da zai tsara Khairat sannan Ya Shiga gidan,a main Palo ya iske  ta sanye cikin doguwar rigar shadda Fara tayi kyau cikin Nan ya girma ta zauna a kasa tare da mike kafafu ta zube Green Apples a gabanta tana ta ci,kanta ba dankwali tayi kyau,Sallama kawai ta amsa Masa Amma Bata ko kulashi ba,haushinsa take ji yace za a cire Mata cikin ta.yace Ummi tace jiya Baki koma ba,ta bar Miki kofa a bude Amma Baki koma ba.

    Khairat tace to ai cewa kawai zaka Yi na tashi na bar maka gidanka ka gaji Dani,fuuuuu ta mike ta dauki Hijab dinta sai gidan Ummi,Ummi sai ganin Khairat tayi ta dawo tace Ummi ya koreni daga Gidansa yace na taho nan sai ya neme Ni,Ummi tace to Lallai Abin na Hunaif ya fara fin karfina Yi zamanki karki koma,Khairat tace bazan koma ba ai.
   Ta bude Fridge din Ummi ta ebo Apples dinta taci gaba da ci,Hunaif dai ya samu har Dining ta shirya Masa Already,Zama yayi yaci ya koshi sannan yayi wanka ya kwanta bacci ya kwashe shi sai kusan Magrib ya tashi baya baccin yamma sai Dole,ji yayi ba abinda yake bukata sai Khairat dinsa.
   Khairat Kuma tana can gidan Ummi tana fushi ita Babu Wanda yake kaunarta a duniya,Talatu ma ko kiranta basa Yi a waya ba komai wlh itama ta daina kulasu.

    Tana zaune Sadiya ta kirata a waya daga Cewa Khairat ta Hunaif kin Gama Mallake bawan Allah bazai iya Miki kishiya ba,shike Nan Khairat taji Haushi Wai Sadiya ta fada Mata bakar magana tana so mijinta ya Mata kishiya,a Palo ta samu Ummi tace Ummi kinji Sadiya Ashe badan Allah take so na ba,ba kawar kirki bace,har fata take min ayi min kishiya ba komai na daina kulata.

    Ummi tasan cikin Khairat ne haka yake ta sata fada kowa haushinsa takeji,Sadiya yau ta jawowa kanta sai ta Kira Hunaif a waya Yana dagawa tace Mijin Khairat zaka iya yi min kishiya? Hunaif yace a'a na Isa ai ban Isa ba yanda nake sonki Ina Zan iya hadaki da wata,To Kaji Sadiya Banza Yar iska Wai fata take min ta Allah ba Tata ba.
  A Nan Hunaif ya samu dama ya lallaba Khairat har ya samu tace yazo ya dauketa a gida zata kwana.

   Haka yaje ya dakkota a mota,Ummi ta fito Palo sai gani tayi Babu Khairat Wai Hunaif yazo ya tafi da ita,me aiki ta fada Mata.
  Haka cikin Khairat ya kasance kullum sai tace anyi Mata Abu,Hunaif yayi kokari da hakurin jurewa,Watarana har kokawa takeyi dashi harda cizo yasha wurin Khairat.
  Har cikinta ya Shiga wata 9 cif Khairat yanzu Bata fiye neman fada ba sai dai kuka ba gaira ba dalili sai ta fashe da kuka sai tayi ta gaji,ko tace ita Dole sai an cire Mata ciki ko ta kashe kanta.
   Hunaif sai ya Kira Ummi sannan ake samu ta hakura.

  Yau ma tunda ta tashi take kukanta,Babu lallashin da Hunaif baiyi ba Taki yin shuru,ta kalleshi tace Mugu azzalumi kaki kaini a cire min cikin Nan na huta,Hunaif tausayi take bashi da Yana da iko wlh da cire Mata za ayi ta huta gashi yayi Kato ya hanata sakewa,Lallashinta yayi ta hakura da kyar tace zata haihu da kanta.

    Shi Kam sai faman Kashe kudi yakeyi Akan cikin,ya Mata dinkuna na Alfarma Banda Wanda ba a dinka bama,readymade iri iri,kusan kayanta da nasa kaf ya canja musu sababbi, Haka jariri ma yasha siyayya tunda ance Mace ce a cikinta da aka auna.

    Ummi da kanta tazo da dare ta tafi da Khairat wajenta,Hunaif Yana ta bakin ciki an raba shi da Matarsa,Ummi tace wlh bazan bar Yar mutane Babu me kula da ita ba ciki ya tsufa Haka baza a barta ita kadai ba.
   Sosai Ummi ke bawa Khairat kulawa a gidanta,Hunaif shima a gidan ya tare kullum Yana can makale da Khairat ko Office ba kullum yake zuwa ba sabo da Wai ta haihu a gabansa.

    Yau Monday yace zai leka Office Yana barin gidan Ummi,Khairat ta yunkura zata tashi kenan kafa ta rike,tayi tayi ta kasa,sai Ciwon baya Kuma,daga Nan sai Mara gadan gadan,Ummi tana kitchen sai Karar Khairat ta jiyo tana Wayyo Ummi,Ummi...marata Zan mutu,ai ko Ummi ta daka wani tsalle Tayo sufa waje ba ko gyale ta Kira Driver suka tafi da Khairat Asibiti,Khairat ta Hana driver tuki cikin jin Dadi Sai kwarototo takeyi,wayyo marata,gashi Nan Ummi Ciwon ta Nan wajen ya taho...ya tsaya a nan wajen,ta bayana wayyo Allah.

    Ummi tace sannu addua akeyi ai,Khairat ta fashe da sabon kuka tace ni ban iya wata Addua ba,na manta...yiiii....Ni a Nemo min Mijina kowa baya kauna ta Ana gani Zan mutu,Dan Ubanka Driver kayi sauri Dan baka San daraja ta ba shi yasa kake tuki a hankali.

   Ummi tace Nasan Yanzu idan Na fadawa Hunaif zai tashi hankalinsa Khairat a kyaleshi,yanzu zai iya hatsari ma a hanya sabo da Yanayinsa,Ni na mutu ko kenan? Sabo da Ni bake Kika haifeni ba kinfi son danki,Ni anfi so na Mutu shi lallabashi akeyi sabo da Ni daga sama na fado, Bayan shine ya jefa Ni a halin da nake ciki shi Yana can Yana Jin dadinsa Ni Zan mutu.

      Tun Khairat na magana har tayi laushi ta kasa magana har suka Isa asibiti aka Basu daki,Ciwo idan ya taso gadan gadan Sai dai kawai Khairat tace Ni marainiyace Ya Allah....Marainiyace Ni...idan ma ta Fara Addua mantawa takeyi Bata iya karasawa,Ummi tace ko Fatiha ki karanta Mana Alhmdllhi rabbil alamin Arrahmanirrahim shike Nan abinda take fada ta dawo baya ko ta dauko karshe ta kawoshi Farko waladdualllin Arrahmanirrahim..Maliki...maliki...shike Nan sai ta koma suratul Iklas Kuma ta Karasa Fatiha da ita,Allahussamad Arrahmanirrahim....

     Shegun likitoci Yan iska Haka Khairat take zagin Likitoci tana tsine musu Albarka,Tun safe Har 12pm Khairat na ciwon Nakuda sai 12:30 Allah ya taimaketa ta Haifo yarta mace katuwar gaske me kama da Hunaif sak kamar an tsaga Kara,Sai lokacin kuma Khairat ta dinga sheka Amai sosai ta Gama,Aka gyara ta fes dake private Hospital ne daki mutum daya,kamar Hotel Haka asibitin yake,Ummi tasa aka gogewa yarinyar jikinta da man Zaitun,sannan Khairat Bayan ta huta Ko ta Yar Tata Bata yi,sai da tayi wanka da kanta ta gasa jikinta har kuka tayi sabo da zafi tana gashin,Allah yasa sai da Nurses suka Sa machine suka kwashe Mata jinin dake mararta,yanzu kadan ne ke fita ba da yawa ba,Khairat ta Dade tana gashin Nan kamar zata kone gabanta,sannan ta dinga wanka ba ji ba gani da sabulu me kamshi dama Ummi ta tanadi komai na kayan da zasu bukata a Hospital.
    Bayan ta Gama Wankan ta shirya kanta tsaf ta fito Ummi tace karfa zafin gashin yayiwa jikinki yawa,ki kula,Kai kawai Khairat ta daga Mata duk jikinta ba karfi kamar iska zata dauketa Haka take ji.

     Yarinyar Ummi ta wanke Cikin Bahonsu na jariri da Ummi ta dakko sabo,Bayan an wanke yarinya Ummi ta shiryata cikin kayan sanyi designers masu kyau cikin Wanda Hunaif ya siyo farare tas,Khairat Doguwar arabiyan riga tasa ta,Ummi ce ta gyara Mata gashinta me tsayi ta Mata parking nasa tare da shafa Mata Vaseline cream a hannu da kafafu,ta fesa Mata turaruka masu dadin kamshi.
   Khairat sai tsamtsamin kanta takeyi.

   Ganin Haka Ummi tasa Aka canja musu daki na hutu,Khairat taci abincin da Yar aiki ta kawo ta koshi sannan Tasha Magunguna,suka Sa Mata drip da Allurai na karfin jiki.
   Sai kallon Yar Tata takeyi tana Jin kunyar Ummi tana so tace a Bata Yar ta ganta tana Jin kunya Haka har bacci ya kwasheta,lokacin Ummi ta Kira Hunaif yazo da sauri ya shigo ya Iske Khairat dinsa lfy tana bacci,ajiyar zuciya ya saki Yana godewa Allah ya dauki Yar sa,ya Shiga kwarara Mata adduoi na sunna.

    Bayan wani lokaci me Dan tsayi Khairat ta samu wani cikin,sai murna sukeyi,Hunaif ya rungume Khairat dinsa a Palo suna Murna kamar ta fari ce, tana jikinsa a kwance yace My Life ta Amsa na'am, Makkah zamu tafi next Month tare da Noor da Ummi gaba daya muyi Umrah,Farin ciki ya lullube Khairat dama duk shekara sai sunje,Haka Zainab Da Mus'af ma,Sadiya da Farouq dinta.
Rahinatu kuwa Suna China ita da mijinta Yana karo karatu.
   Su Talatu,Ammar Soja suna zamansu lfy,Ladi ta daina siyar da abinci a Tasha yanzu Cotono take zuwa Saro Kaya iri iri,ta Zama Yar kasuwa Sosai.

    Yau Friday Khairat da yaranta tare da Hunaif gidan Ummi suka yini,Noor ta Dan Kara Hankali yanzu Amma akwai fitina,tana jikin Hunaif tana Daddy Bari nayi maka kitso sai lalata Masa gashi sukeyi,Shima Irfan Cumb ya dakko ya taho zaiyi kitso.
   Fada ya fara musu,Ummi tace Kai nifa bana son wannan Masifar taku da kukewa yaran Nan,me sukayi? wani yace ka Tara Sumar Haka,ba dama Yara suyi walwala sai ku Fara fada.
  Dariya Khairat tayi tare da cewa Ummi Basu Jin magana ne Musamman Noor, Allah ya kyauta ya shirya Mana Zuriya Baki daya cewar Ummi.
    Ameeeeeen...cewar Noor ta Riga kowa amsawa da karfi.

   Gidan Ummi suka bar yaran Ya dauki Khairat dinsa me yaron ciki suka tafi gida,Tun a mota suka Fara murza juna,Suna Isa gida a Palo suka ya da zango kamar zasu cinye kansu Haka suke sarrafa juna cike da zallar so da kauna.

   Na kawo Karshen ME MAGANI lafiya.
   Ina matukar Godiya Fans Dina masu bibiyar Novels Dina,da masu Sharhi kullum,Masu kirana da Yi min Addua,da masu yabon Novels dina ina Miko dubun Godiya da Jinjina ta, Allah ya bar kauna.

    Masu Sharhi Wanda ban Basu page ba ayi min afwa,Abubuwa ne sukayi min yawa,kuyi hakuri.
 
    Kuskuren da mukayi Allah ya yafe Mana ya bamu ikon Gyarawa gaba,Allah yasa Kuma mu Karu da sakon da Novel din yazo dashi.
